### [1] [From Affect to Complex Behavior: Advancing Multimodal Human-Centered AI at the 10th ABAW Workshop & Competition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27451)
*Dimitrios Kollias,Panagiotis Tzirakis,Alan Cowen,Stefanos Zafeiriou,Irene Kotsia,Eric Granger,Marco Pedersoli,Simon Bacon,Jens Madsen,Soufiane Belharbi,Muhammad Haseeb Aslam,Chunchang Shao,Guanyu Hu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ABAW 2026继续推动在真实、无约束环境中对人类情感与行为建模与理解的研究，涵盖连续情绪估计、离散情绪识别及复杂行为分析等挑战，并提供大规模数据集作为基准。论文赛道涵盖姿态、运动与行为估计、多模态学习、公平性与鲁棒性等方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推动在真实场景下对人类情感与行为的准确建模与理解，促进多模态人机交互系统的发展。

Method: 基于大规模真实世界数据集，开展连续情绪（愉悦-唤醒）估计、离散情绪（表情与动作单元）识别、情绪模仿强度、矛盾/犹豫识别、细粒度暴力检测等任务的竞赛与研究。

Result: 提供了全面的基准测试平台，推动了下一代以人类为中心的多模态AI系统的创新与发展。

Conclusion: ABAW 2026作为关键的学术平台，持续促进跨领域协作与技术创新，引领情感计算与行为分析领域的前沿发展。

Abstract: The 10th Affective & Behavior Analysis in-the-Wild (ABAW) Workshop and Competition, held at CVPR 2026, continues to advance research on modelling, analysis, understanding of human affect and behavior in real-world, unconstrained environments. The workshop maintains its dual structure, comprising both a competition and a paper track. The ABAW Competition introduces a diverse set of challenges targeting key aspects of affective and behavioral understanding, including continuous affect (valence-arousal) estimation, discrete affect (expression and action unit) recognition, as well as more complex behavior analysis tasks, such as emotional mimicry intensity estimation, ambivalence/hesitancy recognition and fine-grained violence detection. These challenges are built upon large-scale in-the-wild datasets, providing comprehensive benchmarks for state-of-the-art approaches. In parallel, the paper track presents a wide range of contributions spanning pose, motion & behavior estimation, affect modelling & multimodal learning, benchmarks, datasets & evaluation protocols, fairness, robustness & deployment. Overall, the 10th ABAW Workshop and Competition continues to serve as a key platform for benchmarking, collaboration and innovation, shaping the development of next-generation multimodal, human-centered AI systems.

</details>


### [2] [Fine-Tuning Vision-Language Models for Understanding Current Damage and Scoring Priority with Quality Guard Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27452)
*Takato Yasuno*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于微调视觉-语言模型（VLM）的桥梁损伤自动化分析与维修优先级评分方法，通过在4000张配对的桥梁损伤图像和检测文本记录上微调LLaVA-1.5-7B模型，实现自然语言描述输出，并结合规则引擎生成五级维修优先级。实验表明2000样本即可达到近似最优性能，数据量超过2000后收益递减；3000样本时语义相似性达峰值，4000样本反而下降，说明中等规模高质量数据优于大规模噪声数据。推理优化使单图处理时间缩短至10.06秒（较基线减少70.2%）。引入双阶段质量保障机制，利用微调后的Swallow-8B小型语言模型过滤低质量输出，防止错误评分。该方法有助于降低人为评估差异、提升管理一致性，并支持专家高效工作流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日本桥梁检查需每五年进行强制性人工视觉评估，但不同工程师给出的定性损伤等级（a-e）存在显著主观差异，且资深工程师老龄化导致检查能力下降，亟需一种可减少人为偏差、提升效率的自动化辅助系统。

Method: 采用QLoRA对LLaVA-1.5-7B模型进行微调，使用最多4000组桥梁损伤图像与对应文本记录；构建规则引擎从模型输出的自然语言描述中提取结构部件与损伤模式，生成五级维修优先级评分；通过分阶段训练（1k/2k/3k/4k样本）分析性能变化；引入torch.compile()与批量处理（batch_size=8）优化推理速度；设计双阶段质量保障机制，用微调的Swallow-8B SLM识别并剔除低质量或无法识别的图像输出。

Result: 2000个训练样本即达到接近最优验证损失（仅需2.9小时训练），后续样本增加带来的改进不超过0.2%每翻倍，呈现明显边际效益递减；语义相似性在3000样本时最高（0.6909），4000样本时下降至0.6739，表明中等规模高质量数据更优；推理效率提升70.2%，单图处理时间为10.06秒；双阶段质量保障有效过滤低质量输出，避免错误评分。

Conclusion: 所提方法能有效实现桥梁损伤理解与维修优先级自动评分，显著降低评估间差异，增强数据治理能力，并通过优化推理与质量控制提升实用性，为智能基础设施管理提供可靠技术支撑。

Abstract: Bridge inspection in Japan requires mandatory visual assessments every five years, yet qualitative damage ratings (levels a-e) assigned by different engineers exhibit significant inter-rater variability -- a critical barrier to consistent infrastructure management. The aging of skilled engineers further threatens inspection capacity. This paper presents a methodology for automating bridge damage understanding and repair priority scoring using fine-tuned Vision-Language Models (VLMs).
  We fine-tune LLaVA-1.5-7B with QLoRA on up to 4,000 paired bridge damage images and inspection text records, then evaluate on a fixed test set of 800 images. The model outputs natural language descriptions identifying structural members and damage patterns, from which a rule-based scoring engine calculates a five-level repair priority index. A progressive training study (1k/2k/3k/4k samples) reveals that 2k training samples achieve near-optimal validation loss in only 2.9 hours of training; beyond 2k, validation loss improves by no more than 0.2% per doubling of training samples, exhibiting clear diminishing returns. Furthermore, semantic similarity on the held-out test set peaks at 3k (0.6909) and degrades at 4k (0.6739), indicating that quality-curated mid-scale data outperforms larger but noisier corpora. Inference optimization combining torch.compile() and batch processing (batch_size=8) achieves 10.06 seconds per image -- a 70.2% reduction over the unoptimized baseline.
  Our approach contributes to data governance in bridge inspection, reduces inter-rater variability, and provides AI-assisted triage to augment expert engineers in inspection workflows. Furthermore, we introduce a two-stage Quality Guard using a fine-tuned Swallow-8B SLM to reject low-quality VLM outputs before priority scoring, preventing spurious scores from damaged or unrecognised images.

</details>


### [3] [Generic Interpretation Approach for Transformer Models Incorporating Heterogenous Attention Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27458)
*Yongjin Cui,Xiaohui Fan,Huajun Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究Transformer模型中异源注意力结构的可解释性问题，提出一种新的解释方法，并通过实验分析代表性模型的运行机制，进行语义与逻辑层面的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer模型在人工智能和智能体发展中具有重要意义，尤其异源注意力结构能融合多源信息实现复杂功能，但其内部机制缺乏透明度，亟需可解释性研究以满足学术探索与政策需求。

Method: 提出针对异源注意力结构的可解释性方法，重点分析多源输入信息的交互机制。

Result: 通过实验验证了所提方法的有效性，成功揭示了代表性模型在语义和逻辑层面的运作机制。

Conclusion: 异源注意力结构是实现复杂功能的基础，本文提出的解释方法有助于深入理解Transformer模型的内部机理，推动AI系统的可信与可控发展。

Abstract: Transformer has significantly propelled the development of artificial intelligence, and certainly the development of agents as well. We categorize attention structures of Transformer into two types based on the source of the input information: homogenous and heterogenous attention structures. Heterogenous attention structures, with co-attention as a typical example, process information from different sources. Heterogenous attention structure is the foundation for Transformer models to achieve more complex functions and integrate more modal information. Whether for research purposes or policy requirements, the interpretation of Transformer models with heterogenous attention structures is an important task. The fusion of information from different sources brings new challenges. Our work mainly includes two parts: method and experimentation. In terms of method, we propose an interpretation method for Transformer models with heterogenous attention structures. In terms of experimentation, based on our experimental analysis paradigm, we interpret the operating mechanisms of representative models, conduct semantic interpretation and logical interpretation.

</details>


### [4] [D$^2$Turb: Depth-Aware Simulation and Decoupled Learning for Single-Frame Atmospheric Turbulence Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27460)
*Zixiao Hu,Tianyu Li,Guoqing Wang,Wei Li,Guoguo Xin,Xun Liu,Peng Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: D$^2$Turb提出一种统一框架，通过引入深度感知的湍流合成协议生成物理一致的退化图像，并将恢复过程分解为纹理去模糊和几何校正两个交互阶段。采用自适应结构先验注入机制（ASPI）动态传递深层结构信息以增强空间校正精度。在合成与真实数据集上均取得领先性能，显著提升纹理恢复与几何保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端方法在平坦场仿真上训练，难以平衡纹理恢复与几何校正，且面临空间变化模糊与非刚性畸变带来的病态问题。

Method: 提出深度感知湍流合成协议，构建物理一致的退化模型；设计双阶段恢复框架（纹理去模糊 + 几何校正），并引入ASPI机制实现结构信息跨阶段传递。

Result: 在合成与真实世界数据集上均达到当前最优性能，显著改善纹理细节恢复与几何一致性。

Conclusion: D$^2$Turb通过物理驱动的模拟与解耦恢复设计，有效解决了单帧大气湍流抑制中的核心挑战，具备良好的泛化能力与实际应用价值。

Abstract: Single-frame atmospheric turbulence mitigation is inherently ill-posed due to spatially varying blur coupled with non-rigid geometric distortion. Existing end-to-end approaches trained on flat-field simulations often struggle to balance texture recovery with geometric rectification. To overcome this limitation, we propose D$^2$Turb, a unified framework that bridges physics-grounded simulation with explicitly decoupled restoration. First, we introduce a Depth-Aware Turbulence Synthesis protocol that incorporates scene depth into the phase-to-space formulation. This generates physically consistent, depth-dependent degradations and provides a crucial intermediate tilt supervision signal for disentangled learning. Building upon this simulation engine, D$^2$Turb decomposes restoration into two interactive stages: texture deblurring and geometric rectification. The texture deblurring stage employs a deblurring backbone to recover fine-grained details while preserving geometric distortion for the subsequent rectification stage. To mitigate the information fragmentation commonly observed in cascaded designs, we further propose an Adaptive Structural Prior Injection (ASPI) mechanism that dynamically transfers deep structural representations from the deblurring module to guide dense flow prediction for spatial unwarping. Extensive experiments demonstrate that D$^2$Turb achieves state-of-the-art performance on both synthetic and real-world datasets, with consistent improvements in both texture recovery and geometric fidelity. Our code and pre-trained models are publicly available at https://github.com/HertzDot222/D2Turb.

</details>


### [5] [Beyond Motion Primitives: Behavioral Activity Recognition from Head-Mounted IMU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27464)
*Chung-Ta Huang,Leopold Das,Jeffrey Zhou,Faizaan Siddique,Julia Seungjoo Baek,Serena Liu,Andrew Rusli,Todd Y. Zhou,Freddy Yu,Sinclair Hansen,Ziling Hu,Arnav Sharma,Mengyu Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为HiT-HAR的703K参数分层模型，利用头戴式惯性测量单元（IMU）实现从运动基元到行为级识别的突破，构建了包含160K样本的Ego4D数据集，并在五类动作与八类场景识别任务中超越现有头戴式IMU模型。通过类别可区分性分析，揭示了不同行为类别的可观测性边界，表明利用时间上下文和场景结构的架构优于单纯扩大模型规模。代码与数据集已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AR智能眼镜需要持续的行为上下文以提供主动协助，但当前最实用的始终开启传感器——头戴式惯性测量单元（IMU）仅能检测如行走或站立等基本运动模式，无法满足高级行为理解需求，因此亟需提升至行为级识别能力。

Method: 构建一个包含8个活动场景、160K样本的Ego4D数据集，采用四层质量保障框架；提出一种703K参数的分层模型HiT-HAR，结合时间上下文与场景结构信息，实现对五类动作与八类场景的高精度识别。

Result: HiT-HAR在五类动作与八类场景识别任务上均优于现有头戴式IMU模型；通过可区分性分析发现：‘移动’类行为可观测性强，‘物品传递’和‘任务操作’依赖时间上下文，而部分场景间信号重叠导致识别挑战。

Conclusion: 利用时间上下文和场景结构的模型架构比单纯增大模型规模更有效，证明了在有限传感器条件下实现高级行为理解的可行性，为未来智能眼镜的主动辅助提供了重要技术支撑。

Abstract: AR smart glasses need continuous behavioral context to offer proactive assistance, yet their most practical always-on sensor, the head-mounted Inertial Measurement Unit (IMU), detects only motion primitives such as walking or standing. We push beyond motion primitives to behavioral-level recognition, defining five categories that balance AR application need with sensor observability. To this end, we construct a 160K-sample Ego4D dataset with a four-tier quality assurance framework spanning 8 activity scenarios, and propose HiT-HAR, a 703K-parameter hierarchical model that outperforms prior head-mounted IMU models on five-class action and eight-class scenario recognition. We further map the observability frontier of head-mounted IMU through per-class separability analysis, identifying which behavioral categories are reliably observable (Locomotion), which benefit from temporal context (Object Transfer, Task Operation), and where scenario-dependent signal overlap poses remaining challenges. Our results indicate that architectural choices exploiting temporal context and scenario structure outperform simply scaling model size. The code and dataset are publicly available at https://github.com/Harvard-AI-and-Robotics-Lab/HiT-HAR.

</details>


### [6] [Diffusion-Based Ukrainian Handwritten Text Generation with Cross-Domain Style Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27487)
*Andrii Ahitoliev,Pavlo Berezin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究构建了一个包含308位作者的126,177张乌克兰手写单词图像的数据集，用于填补乌克兰语（西里尔字母）在手写文本生成领域的空白。通过在不修改架构的情况下重新训练DiffusionPen模型，验证了从拉丁字母到西里尔字母的直接迁移能力。实验涵盖跨语言迁移、零样本迁移至20世纪初乌克兰手稿以及少量样本模仿当代作者三种场景，结果表明模型能生成可读且风格一致的手写文字，证明了少样本潜在扩散模型在非拉丁文字域中的泛化能力。研究公开数据集、训练模型与评估协议，为其他低资源书写系统提供可复现的基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有手写文本生成模型主要集中在拉丁字母系统，对低资源及非拉丁书写系统如西里尔字母中的乌克兰语研究不足，缺乏大规模标注数据和跨域泛化实证。因此亟需构建相关数据集并测试模型在非拉丁环境下的表现，以推动手写风格生成技术向更多语言扩展。

Method: 采用连通域分割、质量过滤和针对代表性不足字符的定向过采样方法构建乌克兰手写单词数据集；在不改变架构的前提下，使用该数据集重新训练DiffusionPen模型（基于MobileNetV2的三元组损失风格编码器与CANINE条件化的潜在扩散U-Net）。通过三种设置评估跨域风格迁移：从IAM英语样本进行跨语言迁移、零样本迁移至早期20世纪乌克兰手稿、以及少量样本模仿当代作者。

Result: 模型成功生成可读性强、风格一致的手写单词图像，在三种迁移设置中均表现出良好性能，证实了少样本潜在扩散模型具备将风格迁移能力推广至非拉丁脚本的能力。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，当前基于潜在扩散的少样本手写文本生成模型能够有效泛化至非拉丁书写系统，如乌克兰语西里尔字母。所构建的数据集与开源工具为未来在低资源书写系统上的手写风格生成研究提供了可靠基准，具有重要的扩展价值。

Abstract: Handwritten text generation (HTG) conditioned on writer style has been widely studied for Latin scripts, but remains underexplored for low-resource and non-Latin writing systems, leaving open how well existing models generalise beyond the Latin domain. Cyrillic, particularly Ukrainian, lacks both large-scale writer-labeled datasets and empirical evidence of such generalisation. To address this gap, we construct a Ukrainian handwritten word dataset of 126,177 images from 308 writers using connected-component segmentation, quality filtering, and targeted oversampling of underrepresented Ukrainian characters. We retrain DiffusionPen, a MobileNetV2 triplet-loss style encoder with a CANINE-conditioned latent diffusion U-Net, on this dataset without architectural modification, testing direct transfer from Latin to Cyrillic. We evaluate cross-domain style transfer in three settings: cross-lingual transfer from IAM English samples, zero-shot transfer to an early 20th-century Ukrainian manuscript, and few-shot imitation of contemporary writers. The model produces legible, style-consistent word images, indicating that few-shot latent diffusion models generalize beyond the Latin-script domain. We release the dataset, trained models, and evaluation protocol as a reproducible benchmark for writer-aware Cyrillic HTG, providing a foundation for extending stylized HTG to other underrepresented writing systems.

</details>


### [7] [Representation-Conditioned Diffusion Models for Guided Training Data Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27495)
*Nithesh Chandher Karthikeyan,Jonas Unger,Gabriel Eilertsen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究评估了基于生成式深度学习合成图像数据集在分类任务中的表现，采用由DINOv2、DINOv3和CLIP学习表征条件化的潜在扩散模型。结果表明，这种表征条件化方法显著优于传统类别条件化生成方式，在ImageNet100上提升10.76个百分点的准确率，同时改善了样本质量和模式覆盖。通过扩大合成数据规模，模型甚至超过了使用真实数据训练的分类器（提升2.0个百分点）。此外，合成图像可用于数据增强，效果优于传统方法，并可通过条件空间进行样本筛选以提升训练效率。总体表明，表征条件化扩散模型为大规模视觉学习任务中数据集的扩充、补充甚至替代提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界数据集的收集、整理和标注成本高昂，限制了监督学习方法的可扩展性和应用范围。因此，探索高效、低成本的数据生成方式成为关键挑战。本研究旨在利用生成式模型克服数据瓶颈，特别是通过更高质量的合成数据提升模型性能。

Method: 使用基于潜在扩散模型的生成方法，结合DINOv2、DINOv3和CLIP提取的视觉表征作为条件输入，生成具有高保真度和多样性的合成图像数据集。通过对比类条件生成与表征条件生成的效果，评估其在图像分类任务中的表现。进一步研究合成数据用于数据增强及样本筛选的有效性。

Result: 表征条件化生成在ImageNet100上比类条件生成高出10.76个百分点的Top-1准确率；扩大合成数据规模后，模型性能超过真实数据训练的基准模型（+2.0 p.p.）；合成图像在数据增强方面优于传统方法；通过条件空间筛选样本可进一步提升训练价值。

Conclusion: 表征条件化扩散模型能够生成高质量、高多样性且具训练价值的合成图像，是解决数据稀缺问题的有效手段，可广泛应用于大规模视觉学习任务中，实现对真实数据集的增强、补充甚至替代。

Abstract: Data availability remains a critical bottleneck in many deep learning applications. Large-scale datasets are often expensive to collect, curate and annotate, which can limit the scalability and applicability of supervised learning methods. In this work, we evaluate the classification performance of models trained on synthetic image datasets produced by generative deep learning. In particular, we use latent diffusion models conditioned on learned representations from DINOv2, DINOv3, and CLIP. Our results demonstrates that this representation-conditioned formulation significantly outperforms class-conditioned generation by a large margin (+10.76 p.p. top-1 accuracy on ImageNet100), by improving sample quality and mode coverage. Furthermore, by scaling the size of the synthetic dataset, we are able to outperform a classifier trained on the real data (+2.0 p.p top-1 accuracy).
  We also demonstrate how generated images can be used for augmentation purposes, outperforming classical augmentation methods, and how the conditioning space can be used for sample filtering to further improve training value. Collectively, these findings highlight that representation-conditioned diffusion models provide a promising approach for augmenting, complementing, or potentially replacing real-world datasets in large-scale visual learning tasks.

</details>


### [8] [Clinical Validation of the Melanoscope AI Mobile Dermoscopy Clinical Decision Support System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27561)
*Elena Sergeevna Kozachok,Sergey Sergeevich Seregin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种用于级联深度学习模型的定量可解释性评估方法，并提出三区患者分流算法，在俄罗斯奥尔洛地区进行了单中心前瞻性临床验证。结果显示无假阴性，特异性达88.3%，且各模型注意力图与专家标注的IoU值良好，证明该AI辅助诊断系统在皮肤癌早期筛查中具有高可靠性与可解释性，适用于资源水平不同的医疗环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 俄罗斯地区皮肤病学家短缺限制了恶性皮肤病变的筛查覆盖率，亟需可解释、标准化的移动数字皮肤镜临床决策支持系统（CDSS）以提升基层筛查能力。

Method: 采用两级级联分类对皮肤镜图像进行分析；使用注意力图可视化技术（ViT和Swin采用注意力传播法，ConvNeXt和EfficientNetV2采用Grad-CAM）；通过基于交并比（IoU）的定量评估方法比较激活图与专家标注的一致性；在奥尔洛地区开展四次“黑色素瘤日”活动进行单中心前瞻性验证（2025年6月–2026年4月）。

Result: 共纳入176名患者：与专家评估一致率达88.6%；5例恶性病变均未出现假阴性（95%置信区间：47.8%-100.0%）；特异性为88.3%；经组织病理学确诊3例黑色素瘤、2例基底细胞癌，6例发育不良痣进入随访；平均IoU值（n=180）：ViT为0.69，Swin为0.64，ConvNeXt为0.53，EfficientNetV2为0.51；分流阈值设定为P<0.15 / 0.15-0.50 / ≥0.50。

Conclusion: 系统未出现假阴性，特异性达88.3%，支持其在筛查中的应用。集成的级联分类、注意力图可视化结合IoU评估以及三区分流策略，提供了可重复、可解释的临床决策支持，具备根据不同资源水平灵活部署的能力。

Abstract: Introduction. Early detection of malignant skin lesions is critical for prognosis, yet dermatologist shortages in Russian regions limit screening coverage. Mobile dermoscopy clinical decision support systems (CDSS) offer a promising approach, with model interpretability and standardised patient routing remaining key barriers to adoption.
  Aim. To develop a quantitative interpretability assessment method for cascade deep learning models and a three-zone patient routing algorithm, and to conduct a preliminary single-centre prospective clinical validation of the Melanoscope AI CDSS in Russian outpatient practice.
  Material and methods.   Results. On 176 patients: agreement with expert assessment 88.6%; no false negatives among 5 malignant lesions (95% CI: 47.8-100.0%); specificity 88.3%. Three melanomas and two basal cell carcinomas were histologically confirmed; six dysplastic naevi placed under follow-up. Mean IoU (n=180): ViT - 0.69; Swin - 0.64; ConvNeXt - 0.53; EfficientNetV2 - 0.51. Routing thresholds: P<0.15 / 0.15-0.50 / >=0.50.
  Conclusion. No false negatives were observed; specificity was 88.3%, supporting screening use. The integrated cascade classification, attention map visualisation with IoU assessment, and three-zone routing provide reproducible, interpretable clinical decision support adaptable to varying resource levels.

### [10] [Not All NVFP4 QAT Recipes Are Equal: How Architecture and Scale Shape Model Quality for Anomaly Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27616)
*Zijian Du,Oleg Rybakov*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了模型架构、模型规模与FP4量化感知训练（QAT）方案在脑肿瘤异常分割任务中的三重交互作用，发现架构选择对量化鲁棒性影响最大，注意力机制架构（如Swin Transformer）对QAT方案选择具有强鲁棒性，而CNN在大规模下易受梯度量化方案影响。FP4在低容量时可离散化softmax注意力，但高级QAT方案可防止其崩溃；在大尺度下，先进QAT方案能缓解梯度量化噪声导致的性能下降。五折患者级交叉验证验证了结果的稳健性，最终推荐Swin Transformer作为FP4量化异常分割的首选架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实时异常分割需兼顾高召回率与高效低精度推理，但现有方法在量化压缩后性能下降明显，尤其在关键医疗任务中，如何选择合适的模型架构、规模与量化策略仍不明确，亟需系统评估三者交互影响以指导实际部署。

Method: 在统一协议下，系统评估多种模型架构（如CNN、Transformer）、不同模型规模及多种FP4 QAT方案在脑肿瘤异常分割任务上的表现，采用五折患者级交叉验证验证结果稳健性，并分析量化鲁棒性与架构/规模/配方间的相互关系。

Result: 注意力机制架构（特别是Swin Transformer）在各种模型规模和QAT方案下均表现出优异的量化鲁棒性；CNN在大规模下对梯度量化敏感，性能显著下降；高级QAT方案可有效抑制梯度量化噪声并防止注意力机制的退化。

Conclusion: Swin Transformer因其对QAT方案的强鲁棒性，在所有规模下均表现稳定，是实现高效、高召回率的FP4量化异常分割的最优架构选择。

Abstract: Real-time anomaly segmentation demands both high recall and efficient low-precision inference. We study the three-way interaction of model architecture, model scale, and FP4 quantization-aware training (QAT) recipe on a recall-critical brain tumor segmentation task, evaluating multiple architectures, scales, and QAT recipes under a unified protocol. We find that architecture choice has the largest impact on quantization robustness, with attention-based architectures showing remarkable resilience to recipe choice while CNN degrades under gradient-quantizing recipes at larger scales. At low capacity, FP4 can discretize softmax attention, but advanced QAT recipes prevent this collapse. At larger scales, advanced recipes mitigate gradient quantization noise that degrades CNN quality. Five-fold patient-level cross-validation confirms these findings are robust to data partition. Our results show that the Swin Transformer is robust to QAT recipe choice across all scales, making it the recommended architecture for FP4-quantized anomaly segmentation.

### [11] [Tensor Memory: Fixed-Size Recurrent State for Long-Horizon Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27686)
*Kabir Swain,Sijie Han,Daniel Karl I. Weidele,Mauro Martino,Antonio Torralba*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Tensor Memory模块，通过固定大小的3D记忆张量增强Transformer，实现空间感知的持久状态，解决长序列视频理解与遮挡推理难题。该模块支持可微软写入、局部交互和门控递归更新，并以连续采样读取上下文，具有恒定内存大小，不依赖输入长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Transformer在处理图像和视频时将时空信息展平为长序列，导致注意力机制和KV缓存随序列增长而增加内存开销，且缺乏显式持久的空间状态，难以进行长时程视频理解及遮挡敏感推理。

Method: 引入轻量级的Tensor Memory模块，采用固定大小的3D记忆张量，通过可微软写入将内容以高斯加权体积形式写入连续3D位置；使用高效的局部交互算子与门控递归动态更新记忆；并通过门控残差融合实现连续采样读取上下文。

Result: 在标准语言、图像和视频基准测试以及专门设计的诊断任务中表现优异，能有效提升长期依赖建模能力；模块可无缝集成至现有Transformer训练流程，无需修改架构即可添加或移除。

Conclusion: Tensor Memory通过引入恒定大小的3D空间记忆，实现了状态容量与输入长度解耦，保留了空间归纳偏置，在长时视频理解与复杂场景推理中展现出显著优势。

Abstract: Transformers process images and videos by flattening space and time into long token sequences. While attention and KV caching preserve past features, their memory grows with sequence length and they lack an explicit, persistent spatial state, making long-horizon video understanding and occlusion-sensitive reasoning difficult. We propose Tensor Memory, a lightweight module that augments Transformer blocks with a fixed-size recurrent 3D memory tensor: tokens write into a voxel grid via a differentiable soft write that deposits content as a Gaussian-weighted volume around a predicted continuous 3D location, the memory is updated with an efficient local interaction operator and gated recurrent dynamics, and tokens read back context via continuous sampling with gated residual fusion. Because the memory tensor has a constant size, Tensor Memory decouples state capacity from input length while preserving a spatial inductive bias. We evaluate the module on standard language, image, and video benchmarks and on a controlled toy diagnostic suite designed to isolate when persistent state is beneficial; it integrates with standard Transformer training pipelines and can be attached to or removed from existing blocks without other architectural changes.

### [12] [Structure over Pixels: Learning Variable-Length Visual Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27696)
*Piotr Wyrwiński,Kacper Dobek,Krzysztof Krawiec*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: STROP 是一种新型离散视觉分词器，能够同时学习图像的结构化场景表示和自适应的序列长度。它通过四阶段课程学习，利用冻结的 DINOv3 特征进行局部率-失真探测监督，优化一个长度头，在单次前向传播中估计有效前缀长度。该方法避免了像素级重建梯度，使代码本完全由高层次潜在表示的质量决定，从而更关注结构而非纹理。随着场景复杂度增加，生成的程序长度也随之增长，并在下游密集预测任务和代码词汇表的直接观察中显现出组合性结构特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自适应分词器通常依赖后处理搜索或在预训练速率集合中选择，无法连续学习每张图像的序列长度，且多以像素重建为目标，强调纹理而非结构。因此需要一种能同时学习结构表示与自适应序列长度、并基于高层语义优化的分词器。

Method: STROP 采用四阶段课程学习策略，以冻结的 DINOv3 特征为监督信号，通过局部率-失真探针指导训练。设计了一个专用的长度头，可在一次前向传播中预测图像的有效编码前缀长度。代码本的优化不依赖像素重建梯度，而是基于高层特征质量，从而更关注结构信息。

Result: STROP 能够根据场景复杂度自动调整程序长度，生成具有组合性结构的视觉代码序列。在下游密集预测任务中表现优异，且对代码词汇表的分析揭示出有意义的结构模式。

Conclusion: STROP 成功实现了结构感知的自适应视觉分词，突破了传统方法在序列长度控制与表示目标上的局限，为构建更具语义意义的视觉程序提供了新路径。

Abstract: Discrete visual tokenizers translate images into ordered sequences of codes, providing a natural representation for structural description of scenes. Yet existing adaptive tokenizers either require post-hoc search or select among a discrete set of pre-trained rates, rather than learning a continuous per-image sequence length coupled to the model and scene, and they typically train against pixel reconstruction, emphasizing texture rather than structure. We propose STROP, a discrete visual tokenizer architecture that forms structural scene representations and simultaneously learns how long an image's visual program should be. Using a four-phase curriculum supervised by local rate--distortion probes against frozen DINOv3 features, STROP optimizes a dedicated length head that estimates the active prefix length in a single forward pass. By bypassing pixel-level reconstruction gradients, the codebook is shaped entirely by the quality of higher-level latent representations. Program length grows with scene complexity, and signs of compositional structure emerge both in downstream dense-prediction transfer and in direct inspection of the learned code vocabulary.

### [13] [Asynchronous Remote Sensing Time-Series Fusion for Cloud Removal and Anytime Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27726)
*Forouzan Fallah,Chia Yu Hsu,Wenwen Li,Anna Liljedahl,Yezhou Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AGFlow是一种基于流匹配的时空模型，用于融合Sentinel-1（S1）和有云覆盖的Sentinel-2（S2）数据，实现无云图像重建与时间序列补全。它具备三个核心能力：（1）基于时间戳条件的内部对齐，无需预处理配准即可融合异步获取的S1和S2数据；（2）联合建模空间结构与时间动态的上下文感知去噪；（3）支持任意时间点查询，可在监测窗口内生成用户指定时间的无云S2图像。在RESTORE-DiT基准测试中，该方法在完全缺失帧重建上表现显著优于现有方法（MAE和RMSE降低16-19%），且在长期数据缺失情况下仍能提供可靠重建，同时具备良好的云去除性能和灵活的时间查询能力，适用于密集植被监测等下游任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 云层遮挡严重限制了Sentinel-2光学遥感数据在地表监测中的应用；虽然Sentinel-1 SAR可提供全天候观测，但其与S2数据在时间上异步且不规则，导致两者融合困难。现有方法通常依赖时间对齐或最近邻匹配，仅能恢复观测时刻的数据，无法应对长时间缺失或按需生成特定时间的图像，难以满足实际监测需求。因此亟需一种能够处理异步数据、支持灵活时间查询的高效融合与重建方法。

Method: 提出AGFlow（Time Aligned Generative Flow Matching）模型，采用生成式流匹配框架，通过时间戳条件控制实现异步S1/S2数据的内部对齐；利用时空联合建模方式捕捉像素间的空间相关性与时间演化规律，实现上下文感知的去噪；引入可任意查询机制，允许在监测期内任意时间点生成无云的S2图像，无需额外训练或插值。

Result: 在RESTORE-DiT基准测试中，AGFlow在完全缺失帧重建任务上表现出色，平均绝对误差（MAE）和均方根误差（RMSE）相比RESTORE-DiT降低16%-19%；在长期数据缺失场景下仍能保持稳定重建质量；同时具备优异的云去除效果，并支持灵活的时间点生成，适用于如植被生长周期分析等高精度时序任务。

Conclusion: AGFlow成功实现了异步多源遥感数据的高效融合与高质量时间序列重建，突破了传统方法在时间对齐和生成灵活性上的局限，为复杂云覆盖环境下的地表连续监测提供了强大工具，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Frequent cloud cover severely limits the usability of Sentinel-2 (S2) optical time series for Earth surface monitoring. Sentinel-1 (S1) SAR provides all-weather complementary observations, but practical S1/S2 fusion remains difficult because acquisitions are irregular and asynchronous. Many existing approaches assume temporally aligned inputs (or require external nearest-date matching) and typically restore only observed timestamps, limiting reconstruction under long gaps and preventing on-demand synthesis. We propose AGFlow (Time Aligned Generative Flow Matching), a spatiotemporal flow-matching model for S1/S2 cloud removal and time-series reconstruction with three capabilities: (1) timestamp-conditioned internal alignment that fuses asynchronous S1 and cloudy S2 observations without preprocessing-based pairing; (2) spatiotemporal, context-aware denoising that models spatial structure jointly with temporal dynamics (rather than independent per-pixel time series); and (3) anytime querying, enabling generation of cloud-free S2 frames at both observed and user-specified timestamps within the monitoring window. We evaluate on the RESTORE-DiT benchmark protocol with quantitative metrics, qualitative comparisons, and component ablations. AGFlow notably improves fully missing-frame reconstruction (MAE and RMSE reduce by 16-19% over RESTORE-DiT) and provides reliable reconstructions under persistent gaps, while also yielding competitive cloud removal performance and flexible temporal querying for downstream tasks such as dense vegetation monitoring.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准PatchCore使用欧氏距离，忽略特征相关性，且需一次性存储全部正常图像块；在工业视觉异常检测中，内存受限且缺陷样本稀少，需高效、低内存消耗的在线学习与检索方法。

Method: 引入协方差感知的马氏距离检索，通过降维空间中的正则化协方差估计与嵌入白化，使欧氏最近邻搜索等价于马氏检索；采用增量降维、在线协方差估计与流式聚合，实现可迭代、内存受限的训练流程。

Result: 在公开基准上保持接近原始PatchCore的图像级性能，峰值内存从5.41 GB降至2.78 GB；在三个工业数据集上，平均AUC从0.981提升至0.986，验证了方法在实际应用中的有效性与高效性。

Conclusion: Mahalanobis PatchCore有效解决了传统PatchCore在内存和特征相关性建模上的局限，为工业视觉异常检测提供了一种高效、可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Industrial visual anomaly detection is usually one-class: normal images are abundant, while defects are rare, heterogeneous, and often unavailable during system design. PatchCore-style retrieval suits this setting because it scores test images from a memory bank of normal patch features, but the standard Euclidean geometry ignores feature correlations and its offline construction materialises the full patch pool before subsampling.
  We introduce Mahalanobis PatchCore, a covariance-aware, streaming-compatible extension of PatchCore. Its artificial intelligence contribution is a retrieval detector that estimates a regularised covariance model in reduced feature space and whitens embeddings, so Euclidean nearest-neighbour search after transformation implements Mahalanobis retrieval. A bounded-memory, re-iterable training pipeline builds the memory bank without storing all normal patches at once, using incremental dimensionality reduction, online covariance estimation, and streaming aggregation.
  The engineering application is automated industrial inspection, where visual anomaly detection must remain accurate under practical memory limits. We evaluate the method on a public 15-category industrial anomaly-detection benchmark and three industrial datasets covering blow-fill-seal strip-ampoule meniscus inspection, amber-glass-ampoule bottom inspection, and lyophilised-cake vial inspection. Mahalanobis PatchCore preserves most offline PatchCore image-level performance on the public benchmark while reducing peak memory from 5.41 to 2.78 GB, and improves the selected industrial mean image area under the receiver operating characteristic curve from 0.981 to 0.986.

</details>


### [16] [Can Segmentation Models Understand the World? Towards Proactive Affordance Reasoning via Visual Chain-of-Thought](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27764)
*Yuchen Guo,Junli Gong,Hongmin Cai,Yiu-ming Cheung,Weifeng Su*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SegWorld introduces a multi-level visual chain-of-thought framework that enables segmentation models to reason about scenes proactively and infer intent-based actions before generating masks, improving performance on high-level goal-driven instructions. It formalizes reasoning as probabilistic inference and introduces a new benchmark for intent-to-part segmentation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing segmentation models rely on target-referential instructions that specify regions directly, but real-world human instructions often express intentions without naming specific regions. This gap limits models' ability to support embodied interaction tasks where goals are expressed at the intent level.

Method: SegWorld employs a multi-level visual chain-of-thought process: first, it proactively observes the scene and describes visible objects and plausible events; then, given an intent-level instruction, it traces a reasoning path from relevant objects to actions and physical interaction sites, ultimately identifying the part of an object that affords the action. The model uses probabilistic inference grounded in linguistic scene context derived from proactive observation.

Result: Experiments show SegWorld performs comparably to instruction-driven baselines on target-referential instructions and significantly outperforms them on intent-level instructions. A new intent-to-part benchmark demonstrates its effectiveness in segmenting parts based on high-level goals.

Conclusion: By incorporating proactive scene understanding and multi-level reasoning, SegWorld advances vision-language models toward more natural, intent-aware interaction, enabling accurate segmentation even when instructions do not explicitly identify target regions.

Abstract: Recent segmentation models couple large language models (LLMs) with mask decoders to ground complex language expressions into masks, yet their instructions remain target-referential: they describe, constrain, or imply the region to be segmented. However, in real-world embodied interaction, human instructions are often at the intent-level, which includes the desired outcome without naming the region that enables it. To bridge this gap, we introduce SegWorld, where the model reasons about the scene through a multi-level visual chain-of-thought (CoT) before committing to a mask. Before receiving any instructions, it proactively observes the scene, describing visible objects and inferring plausible events they may support. Given an instruction, it continues the chain: from the object relevant to the intent, through the action that satisfies it, to the physical interaction site, the object part that affords the action. We formalize SegWorld as probabilistic inference, in which proactive observation supplies a linguistic scene context that improves mask prediction when instructions are given at the level of intent. We construct an intent-to-part benchmark for evaluating affordance-bearing part segmentation from high-level goals. Experiments show SegWorld matches instruction-driven baselines on target-referential instructions and improves substantially on intent-level ones.

Abstract: CASTLE 2026 asks 185 multiple-choice questions over 600+ hours of synchronized multi-view egocentric video. Approach A, SVA: Search-Verify-Answer, is a three-stage pipeline that hierarchically narrows to a primary window, verifies sub-windows with a VLM under four anti-confabulation rules, and fuses evidence with an LLM judge under an evidence-priority hierarchy. Approach B, TMKG: Temporal-Multimodal-Knowledge-Graph, is the contrast: it builds a temporal multimodal knowledge graph, locates a primary cell via graph search, and produces the final answer with a single grounded VLM. SVA reaches a leaderboard accuracy of 0.50 and is our final challenge submission; TMKG reaches 0.35.

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于扩散模型激活轨迹的残差化时间稀疏自编码器（Residualized Temporal SAE），通过捕捉非线性动态结构，提升对文本到图像生成过程中激活轨迹的可解释性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多在单一时步或条件于时间分析扩散模型的激活，难以捕捉完整的时序动态结构，因此需要一种能直接建模完整激活轨迹的方法以揭示更深层次的语义特征。

Method: 收集去噪过程中的多时步激活，构建相邻时步间的线性预测器，用初始激活与未被线性预测解释的残差成分表示轨迹；在此残差表示上训练稀疏自编码器，使潜在变量捕捉超出线性可预测部分的结构。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在重建精度、消融研究、时空特征分析和定性控制实验中均表现优异，能够有效解析扩散模型中随时间演化的特征轨迹。

Conclusion: 残差化时间稀疏自编码器为理解扩散模型内部时序结构提供了有力工具，有助于揭示生成过程中的动态语义演化机制。

Abstract: Text-to-image diffusion models generate images through an iterative denoising process, so internal neural layers produce trajectories of activations rather than single static representations. Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have recently been used to decompose diffusion activations into interpretable feature directions, but most approaches analyze activations at individual timesteps or condition on time rather than learning directly from full activation trajectories. In this work, we introduce residualized temporal SAEs for diffusion activation trajectories. We collect activations across denoising time, fit linear predictors between neighboring timesteps, and represent each trajectory using an initial activation together with residual components not explained by these linear dynamics. Training an SAE on this residualized representation encourages sparse latents to capture structure beyond what is linearly predictable. The residualized decoder directions can be mapped back into activation space, allowing each latent to be analyzed as a feature trajectory over denoising time. Through reconstruction and ablation studies, spatiotemporal feature analysis, and qualitative steering experiments on Stable Diffusion~1.5, we show that residualized temporal SAEs provide a useful framework for studying temporally structured diffusion activations.

In the present research endeavor, this article undertake a comprehensive comparative analysis of seven distinct PFL algorithms deployed across three diverse datasets, namely MNIST, SignMNIST, and Digit5. Method: 设计OphIn-Engine流水线，包括多模态转录、视觉线索分离与评分、指令合成与质量控制，从开放获取的眼科视频中构建高质指令数据；基于该数据构建OphIn-500K数据集，并训练OphIn-VL模型。

Result: OphIn-VL在多项任务中表现优于当前最先进的通用及专用医学多模态大模型，在视觉问答、多轮对话和链式推理任务中均展现出更强的能力。

Conclusion: OphIn-Engine成功构建了大规模、高质量的眼科多模态指令数据集，推动了眼科专用多模态大模型的发展，为临床辅助诊断系统提供了有力支持。

Abstract: The advancement of general medical Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) has shown great potential for building conversational assistants to support clinical diagnosis. However, their adaptation to highly specialized domains such as ophthalmology remains underexplored, primarily due to the scarcity of large-scale, domain-specific instruction-tuning data. Existing ophthalmic datasets for conversational agents are often limited in scale and largely rely on images from established public benchmarks, limiting the scalability of ophthalmic MLLMs and their ability to capture real-world clinical complexity. To address this gap, we propose $\textbf{OphIn-Engine}$, an ophthalmology-specific instruction data curation pipeline that constructs high-quality instruction data from open-access ophthalmology web-scale videos. The pipeline integrates multimodal transcription for extracting image-transcript pairs, visual cue separation and scoring for identifying clinically relevant visual descriptions, and instruction synthesis with quality control for generating accurate and diverse clinical dialogues. Using this engine, we introduce $\textbf{OphIn-500K}$, a large-scale multimodal ophthalmology instruction-tuning dataset containing over 500,000 instruction instances and more than 151,000 unique images from over 29,000 video clips, formatted as visual question answering (VQA), multi-turn conversational interactions, and chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning. Built upon this dataset, we further develop $\textbf{OphIn-VL}$, an ophthalmology-specific MLLM with advanced visual understanding and conversational capabilities. Comprehensive experiments and case studies demonstrate that OphIn-VL achieves superior performance compared with state-of-the-art general medical and domain-specific MLLMs.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先从原始文本生成正负文本以聚焦特定文本组件；其次提出基于属性的文本推理策略，挖掘生成文本的细粒度语义；最后设计视频引导的自加权损失，实现跨模态对齐与桥接。

To this end, in this paper, we propose a novel plug-and-play framework for various VLM-based methods to fully bridge videos and texts. Specifically, we first generate positive and negative texts from the original ones to target specific text components. Extensive experiments show that the proposed method can serve as the plug-and-play module to effectively improve the performance of state-of-the-art VLMs.

### [26] [SIGMA: Semantic-Difference Instruction-Grounding Mask Annotator for Text-Driven Image Manipulation Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27924)
*Peiyu Zhuang,Jianquan Yang,Haodong Li,Zhuoying Cai,Ruitao Xie,Jishen Zeng,Baoying Chen,Jiwu Huang,Xiaochun Cao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出SIGMA（Semantic-difference Instruction-Grounding Mask Annotator），一种用于自动标注文本驱动图像编辑中像素级掩码的新方法。该方法通过语义特征差分与指令引导的空间先验融合，有效增强目标编辑区域的差异信号，克服了扩散模型带来的像素扰动问题。SIGMA采用两阶段训练：第一阶段基于修复掩码监督；第二阶段通过VAE回路噪声校准、EMA自训练和编辑噪声解耦损失缓解域偏移。在五个基准测试中，其性能优于现有自动掩码生成器（F1提升12.20%，IoU提升11.16%）。将SIGMA应用于公开编辑数据集，构建了约110万样本的IML训练集，显著提升六种不同检测器的性能（平均F1提升18.34%），实现了对海量未利用编辑数据的高效再利用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前文本驱动图像编辑虽快速发展，但图像操作定位（IML）模型依赖大规模像素标注数据，而高质量标注数据获取成本高、难以规模化。然而，公开的编辑数据集中已存在大量结构相同的原始-编辑图像对，仅缺少像素级掩码。如何低成本、高精度地从中恢复掩码成为关键挑战。传统像素差分易受扩散扰动影响，而仅依赖指令的定位又忽略编辑的非预期副作用。因此亟需一种能精准捕捉意图编辑区域并抑制噪声干扰的自动标注方法。

Method: SIGMA采用双阶段训练策略：第一阶段在视觉基础模型中进行语义特征差分，并引入由指令生成的空间先验，通过双向跨模态精炼增强目标编辑区域的差异信号；第二阶段通过VAE回路噪声校准消除扩散域偏差，结合EMA自训练和编辑噪声解耦损失进一步优化模型鲁棒性。整体框架融合语义感知与指令引导，实现对意图编辑区域的精准定位与掩码生成。

Result: SIGMA在五个基准测试中表现优异，相比现有自动掩码生成方法，F1得分提升12.20%，IoU提升11.16%。将其应用于公开编辑数据集后，成功构建了一个包含约110万样本的高质量IML训练集，使得六种不同的图像操作定位检测器在五个数据集上的平均F1提升达18.34%。该成果将原本无法使用的编辑数据转化为可广泛复用的监督资源，具有显著的模型无关性和应用价值。

Conclusion: SIGMA提供了一种高效、低成本的自动掩码生成方案，成功挖掘了公共编辑数据中的隐藏标注信息。其创新的语义差分与指令引导融合机制有效应对了扩散模型带来的噪声挑战，显著提升了掩码生成精度。所生成的大规模标注数据集为未来图像操作定位研究提供了重要基础设施，推动了文本驱动图像编辑向更精准、可扩展的方向发展。

Abstract: Text-driven image editing has advanced rapidly, but reliably localizing these manipulations requires image manipulation localization (IML) models trained on large pixel-annotated datasets, and there is still no low-cost way to obtain such training data at scale. We observe that these data already exist in disguise: public editing datasets contain millions of structurally identical (original, edited) pairs to IML training samples, lacking only pixel-level masks. Recovering these masks automatically is non-trivial: pixel differencing is overwhelmed by diffusion-induced perturbations across all pixels, and instruction-only grounding localizes only what the prompt describes, missing unintended editor side-effects. We propose SIGMA (Semantic-difference Instruction-Grounding Mask Annotator), which performs semantic-feature differencing in a vision foundation backbone and injects an instruction-derived spatial prior into this visual stream via bidirectional cross-modal refinement, amplifying the difference signal at intended-edit regions when the editor faithfully realizes user intent. SIGMA is trained in two complementary stages: Stage I supervises on inpainting masks; Stage II closes the diffusion-domain shift via VAE-roundtrip noise calibration, EMA self-training, and an edit-noise disentanglement loss. SIGMA outperforms existing automatic mask generators on five benchmarks (+12.20% F1, +11.16% IoU). When applied to public editing corpora, it produces a ~1.1M IML training set that improves six diverse detectors by +18.34% F1 across five datasets, turning previously unused editing data into a model-agnostic supervisory resource for IML. We'll release the full codebase as soon as the paper is accepted.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用先验结构提取以增强LVLM兼容性，并通过动态引导中和实现高效扰动抑制，构建轻量级、无需额外训练的防御框架。

Abstract: Image inputs enable Large Vision Language Models (LVLMs) to perceive fine-grained visual information, but also introduce a pixel-level attack surface through which adversarial perturbations can elicit unsafe model behaviors. However, most existing defenses are designed for traditional computer vision settings and thus often overlook the cross-modal alignment required by LVLMs, leading to degraded performance. Meanwhile, the limited defenses tailored to LVLMs often require substantial image modifications and introduce considerable computational overhead, thereby compromising inference quality and efficiency. To address these limitations, we propose Structure-Induced Guided Neutralization (SIGN), a lightweight, plug-and-play defense framework that improves LVLM compatibility via Prior Structural Extraction and achieves efficient perturbation suppression via Dynamic Guided Neutralization. Extensive experiments show that SIGN achieves over 87\% defense success rate with only 0.5\% pixel modification and 0.16 seconds per image, while nearly preserving original visual representations and benign task performance. Our work offers a lightweight alternative to defenses that require costly model training and highlights the potential of exploiting a vision encoder for efficient adversarial protection. Our code is open source on https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SIGN-BCB1.

### [28] [When Think-with-Image Meets Safety: What Determines Multimodal Jailbreak Robustness?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27932)
*Yuan Tian,Bing Hu,Fang Wu,Xiaomin Li,Binghang Lu,Neil Zhenqiang Gong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究了大视觉语言模型中‘思考-图像’推理范式对多模态越狱攻击的鲁棒性影响。实验表明，显式图像工具交互可将越狱成功率平均降低约30%，且即使返回图像内容被手动覆盖或存在安全隐患，该优势依然存在；而仅依赖文本前序轮次的系统则表现接近直接回答，安全性显著下降。研究提出‘图像工具安全向量’框架，解释该现象源于图像工具调用在隐藏表示空间中引入了一个指向安全方向的残差偏移。通过表征分析与激活干预验证了该机制。结果表明，显式图像工具交互是提升模型抗越狱能力的有效设计模式，并强调需针对不同流程进行针对性安全评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大视觉语言模型中‘思考-图像’推理范式的安全影响，特别是其对多模态越狱攻击的鲁棒性，以指导更安全的模型设计。

Method: 对比多种过程设计（直接生成、纯文本前序、视觉状态操作、显式外部图像工具调用），在多个视觉语言模型上测试越狱攻击成功率；引入图像工具安全向量框架，分析隐藏表示空间中的变化，并通过激活干预验证机制。

Result: 显式图像工具交互显著降低越狱成功率（平均降低约30%），且该效果不依赖于返回图像内容的安全性或文本追踪信息；表征分析和激活干预支持‘安全向量’解释。

Conclusion: 显式图像工具交互是一种提升多模态模型抗越狱能力的有效设计模式，但应结合具体流程开展针对性安全评估。

Abstract: Think-with-image reasoning is emerging as a new inference paradigm for large vision-language models, but its safety implications remain poorly understood. Existing systems already span multiple process designs, including direct response generation, text-only prior turn, visual-state manipulation, and explicit external image-tool invocation. In this paper, we ask which of these evaluated paradigms improves multimodal jailbreak robustness, and why. Across multiple vision-language models, explicit image-tool interaction yields the lowest attack success rates in our experiments, reducing jailbreak success by around 30% relative on average across the evaluated models. This finding is initially surprising: ASR remains low even when the returned image-tool output is manually overridden or itself unsafe-looking, but returns near direct-answering levels under text-only prior turn controls. These results indicate that the lower ASR is not explained by benign returned-image semantics or by the textual image-tool trace alone. To explain the pattern, we introduce an image-tool safety vector framework that models image-tool invocation as a residual shift in hidden representations toward a safety-relevant direction. Representation-level analyses and activation interventions support this account. Overall, our results suggest that explicit image-tool interaction is a promising design pattern for improving jailbreak robustness, while also motivating pipeline-specific safety evaluation.

### [29] [SEMAGIC: Learning Semantically Consistent Deformable 3D Representations from In-the-Wild Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27938)
*Sky Cen,Wufei Ma,Guofeng Zhang,Alan Yuille,Adam Kortylewski*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SEMAGIC提出了一种从单视角野外图像中学习语义一致的可变形3D表示的新框架。与以往将重建作为最终目标的方法不同，SEMAGIC利用可变形建模来发现类别级别的对应关系。通过引入规范模板网格和学习到的形变场，实现顶点在跨实例间保持稳定的语义一致性。训练过程中采用特征级一致性损失和基于顶点索引的形变机制，强制语义对齐。实验表明，该方法在SPair-71k基准上使语义对应性能提升+14.7 PCK@0.1，证明了可变形模型作为有效语义3D表示的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可变形3D重建方法虽能生成视觉上合理的几何形状，但其跨实例的对应关系不稳定，在语义对应任务中表现不佳。因此需要一种能够同时保证几何重建质量与语义一致性的新方法。

Method: SEMAGIC使用一个类别级的规范模板网格和一个由图像特征驱动的可学习形变场，构建类似自编码器的结构，以实现从图像特征到实例几何的重建。通过特征级一致性损失和顶点索引条件化的形变策略，确保不同实例间的顶点具有稳定的语义对应关系。

Result: 在SPair-71k语义对应基准上，SEMAGIC实现了+14.7 PCK@0.1的性能提升，显著优于现有方法，验证了其在保持语义一致性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: SEMAGIC成功地将可变形建模用于发现类别内稳定且语义一致的对应关系，使得可变形3D模型不仅具备良好的几何重建能力，更成为有效的语义3D表示形式。

Abstract: Learning deformable 3D object models from single-view in-the-wild images has enabled impressive 3D shape reconstruction without supervision. However, it remains unclear whether these models capture the semantic structure required for downstream tasks. We find that existing deformable reconstruction approaches, despite producing visually plausible geometry, yield unstable correspondences across instances and perform poorly on semantic correspondence benchmarks. We introduce SEMAGIC, a framework for learning semantically consistent deformable 3D representations from single-view in-the-wild images. Rather than treating reconstruction as the end goal, SEMAGIC uses deformable modeling as a mechanism to discover category-level correspondences. Each category is represented by a canonical template mesh and a learned deformation field, functioning similarly to an autoencoder that reconstructs instance geometry from image features, enabling vertices to maintain consistent semantic meaning across instances. Semantic consistency is enforced during training through (i) a feature-level consistency loss aligning semantic features between canonical and deformed meshes, and (ii) vertex-index-conditioned deformation that preserves semantic correspondence across instances. By explicitly coupling geometric deformation with semantic alignment, SEMAGIC produces representations that maintain stable part correspondences across intra-category variation. Experiments demonstrate that SEMAGIC improves semantic correspondence of deformable models by +14.7 PCK@0.1 on SPair-71k, establishing deformable models as effective semantic 3D representations.

However, self-report-based assessment of behavior change receptivity is sparse and delayed, limiting its practical use in continuous monitoring. To explore whether passive sensing may help address this challenge, this study conducts a pilot investigation of inferring participants' self-reported behavior change receptivity from egocentric eating images collected by a wearable camera. We use pilot data obtained from free-living eating episodes using the Automatic Ingestion Monitor v2 (AIM-2). The data included egocentric image sequences captured during eating and paired with responses to questions assessing specific dimensions of behavior change receptivity (awareness, interaction capability, and motivation). To examine whether visual information contained any relevancy to these responses, we evaluated a transfer-learning-assisted framework that combines a pre-trained Contrastive Language-Image Pre-Training (CLIP) vision encoder with a lightweight transformer classifier. The model processes eating episode image sequences to extract potential semantic and temporal cues related to behavior change receptivity. Preliminary experimental results show promising improvements over simple baseline models for behavior change receptivity indicators. ### [31] [ROVER: Routing Object-Centric Visual Evidence for Grounded Multi-Image Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27959)
*Guannan Lv,Ren Nie,Hongjian Dou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ROVER，一种轻量级可学习的插件，用于高效全局视觉证据路由。通过在每个对象定位预测时注入特定步骤的令牌三元组，协同聚合推理上下文、通过对象中心差分注意力将图像内线索提炼到视觉工作空间，并在该空间中跨对象和图像路由与整合历史感知证据，从而提升多图像推理性能。集成至Qwen2.5-VL-7B并采用交错SFT-to-GRPO训练流程，在MM-GCoT和VideoEspresso上分别取得+4.8%和+8.6%的答案准确率提升，且在多个基准测试中表现出优异的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于定位的方法通常聚焦于感兴趣区域（RoIs），虽能增强局部推理，但削弱了整体场景理解与物体间关系建模，同时带来随RoI数量和大小增加的解码开销；而自适应视觉特征选择常需细粒度监督或复杂启发式规则，难以兼顾效率与效果。因此亟需一种轻量、高效且能保留全局信息的视觉证据路由机制。

Method: ROVER是一种轻量级可学习插件，利用步骤特定的令牌三元组，在每次对象定位预测时：(i) 聚合当前推理上下文；(ii) 通过对象中心差分注意力将图像内线索提炼至视觉工作空间；(iii) 在该空间中实现跨对象与跨图像的历史感知证据路由与融合。结合交错的SFT-to-GRPO训练策略，嵌入Qwen2.5-VL-7B模型中。

Result: 在严格遵循原始数据集与评估协议的前提下，ROVER在MM-GCoT任务上实现+4.8%答案准确率和+14.6%定位准确率提升，在VideoEspresso上达+8.6%答案准确率提升。经VideoEspresso训练的模型在多个不同基准上平均表现优于基线模型+4.7%，展现出强迁移能力。

Conclusion: ROVER通过对象中心的视觉证据路由机制，在不增加显著计算负担的前提下，有效增强了多图像推理中的全局理解与跨对象关联建模能力，显著提升了多模态大模型在复杂任务上的性能与泛化性，为高效视觉推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have increasingly localized and interleaved visual evidence for deliberative reasoning. Grounding-based approaches typically focus on regions of interest (RoIs) by injecting cropped image patches or RoI-specific features into the reasoning context. However, such designs can weaken holistic scene understanding and inter-object relations, while incurring decoding costs that scale with the number and size of RoIs. Alternatively, adaptive visual feature selection often requires fine-grained supervision or complex heuristics. To address these limitations, we propose ROVER (Routing Object-centric Visual Evidence for grounded multi-image Reasoning), a lightweight, learnable plugin for efficient global visual evidence routing. Upon each object grounding prediction, ROVER injects a step-specific token triplet to synergistically: (i) aggregate the ongoing reasoning context, (ii) distill intra-image cues into a visual working space via object-centric differential attention, and (iii) route and integrate history-aware evidence across objects and images within this space for subsequent reasoning. We integrate ROVER into Qwen2.5-VL-7B and develop an interleaved SFT-to-GRPO training pipeline. Strictly adhering to the original datasets and evaluation protocols, our method achieves the best performance on MM-GCoT (+4.8% answer accuracy, +14.6% grounding accuracy) and VideoEspresso (+8.6% answer accuracy). The VideoEspresso-trained model demonstrates strong transferability, outperforming the base model by +4.7% on average across diverse benchmarks.

### [32] [ABot-OCR Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27978)
*Kaitao Jiang,Ruiyan Gong,Xiaolong Cheng,Kangning Niu,Tianlun Li,Mu Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ABot-OCR 是一个端到端的视觉语言模型，能够直接将页面图像转为干净的 Markdown，无需复杂的模块化流程。通过大规模结构一致的数据引擎和一种结构约束的强化学习方法（DHD-O），显著提升文本准确性和标记格式正确性。在 OmniDocBench v1.5 和 v1.6 上表现优于所有现有端到端系统，分别达到 92.81 和 93.30 的得分，并在十种语言上验证了其强大的多语言泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统文档解析依赖多模块流水线，易受各环节误差累积影响，且难以保证输出格式一致性。本文旨在构建一个端到端的高精度、高鲁棒性的文档转 Markdown 框架，避免模块间耦合与错误传播。

Method: 提出 ABot-OCR 框架，包含专用数据引擎生成大规模结构一致标注数据；采用解耦异构文档优化（Decoupled Heterogeneous Document Optimization, DHD-O）策略，结合结构约束的强化学习，提升文本准确性与 Markdown 格式合规性。

Result: 在 OmniDocBench v1.5 和 v1.6 上分别取得 92.81 和 93.30 的领先分数，显著缩小与强流水线基线的差距；在十种语言上均表现出优异的跨语言泛化能力。

Conclusion: ABot-OCR 实现了高效、精准、格式正确的端到端文档转 Markdown，克服了传统方法的局限，为文档智能处理提供了新范式。

Abstract: We introduce ABot-OCR, an end-to-end vision-language model that transcribes a page image directly into clean Markdown in a single forward pass. By doing so, our approach completely eliminates the need for brittle modular orchestration. To maximize parsing fidelity, we develop a dedicated data engine to provide large-scale, structurally consistent supervision. Furthermore, we propose Decoupled Heterogeneous Document Optimization, a structure-constrained reinforcement learning method that sharpens textual accuracy and strictly enforces markup well-formedness beyond supervised fine-tuning alone. Extensive evaluations demonstrate the superior performance of our framework. On the OmniDocBench v1.5 and v1.6 benchmarks, ABot-OCR achieves state-of-the-art scores of 92.81 and 93.30 among all end-to-end systems, substantially narrowing the performance gap relative to strong pipeline baselines. Finally, comprehensive multilingual text recognition across ten diverse languages further confirms the robust generalizability of ABot-OCR.

### [33] [Automated Estimation of Impact Time, Impact Location, and Shuttlecock Speed in Badminton Smashes Using Event Cameras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28011)
*Yudai Washida,Yuto Kase,Kai Ishibe,Ryoma Yasuda,Sakiko Hashimoto*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于双同步事件相机的测量方法，可自动估算羽毛球扣杀中的击球时间、球拍面击球位置及击球后球速，无需复杂准备，且在单次试验中实现集成评估。通过与高速摄像机参考方法对比，该方法在124次可分析试验中成功估计了击球时间和球速，击球位置估计成功率为93.5%。各项指标偏差均在可接受范围内，无比例偏倚，表明该方法适用于实际场景中对运动员表现和装备性能的综合评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统测量系统在时间分辨率、数据效率和准备成本之间存在权衡，难以高效、准确地量化羽毛球扣杀中的冲击现象，亟需一种更实用、集成化的测量方法。

Method: 利用两个同步事件相机，通过事件率统计检测挥拍区间；从侧视事件数据中识别球轨迹拐点以估计击球时间；通过后视图像中球拍面的椭圆拟合确定击球位置；在矢状面内计算击球后球速。

Result: 在125次扣杀试验中，124次可分析试验成功估计击球时间和球速，击球位置估计成功率达93.5%（116/124）。击球时间、横向击球位置、纵向击球位置和球速的偏差（95%置信区间）分别为1.84 ms（1.45–2.23）、3.45 mm（2.18–4.72）、-1.92 mm（-2.97–0.88）和-1.00 m/s（-2.46–0.46），无比例偏倚。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于事件相机的方法能够高效、准确地实现羽毛球扣杀中关键参数的集成测量，具备在实际训练与装备评估中应用的潜力。

Abstract: Quantifying impact phenomena in badminton smashes is important for evaluating both athletic performance and equipment; however, conventional measurement systems involve trade-offs between temporal resolution, data efficiency, and preparation effort. This study proposes a measurement method using two synchronized event cameras to automatically estimate impact time, impact location on the racket face, and post-impact shuttlecock speed in an integrated manner within the same trial. The swing interval was detected from event rate statistics, impact time was estimated from the shuttlecock trajectory inflection in the lateral-view event data, impact location was determined by ellipse fitting to the racket face in the rear-view event image, and shuttlecock speed was calculated in the sagittal plane. To validate the proposed method, Bland-Altman analysis was performed against a high-speed camera-based reference method using 125 smash trials from five players. Impact time and shuttlecock speed were estimated in all 124 analyzable trials, and impact location was estimated in 93.5% (116/124). The bias (95% CI) for impact time, medio-lateral impact location, longitudinal impact location, and shuttlecock speed were 1.84 ms (1.45 to 2.23), 3.45 mm (2.18 to 4.72), -1.92 mm (-2.97 to -0.88), and -1.00 m/s (-2.46 to 0.46), respectively. No proportional bias was observed for any metric. These results suggest that the proposed method can serve as a useful tool for integrated assessment of badminton smash performance and equipment in practical settings.

### [34] [VCap: Hypergeometric Rewards for Weak-to-Strong Visual Captioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28023)
*Xingyu Lu,Jinpeng Wang,Yi-Fan Zhang,Yankai Yang,Yancheng Long,Yiyang Fan,Xuanyu Zheng,Haonan Fan,Kaiyu Jiang,Tianke Zhang,Changyi Liu,Bin Wen,Fan Yang,Tingting Gao,Han Li,Chun Yuan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VCap奖励机制，通过参考描述（见证者）与视觉信号（仲裁者）结合，实现对生成描述的事实一致性精细验证，显著提升视觉描述模型的准确性与鲁棒性，尤其在弱监督条件下表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉描述任务中的强化学习奖励设计缺乏细粒度且可靠的事实验证信号，限制了模型性能提升，尤其在处理不完美参考描述时效果不佳。

Method: 设计基于见证者-仲裁者框架的VCap奖励机制，利用参考描述与视觉信号联合验证生成描述的事实一致性，提供高精度的奖励信号。

Result: 8B规模模型在多个图像和视频描述基准上超越开源与闭源领先模型；人类评估显示其生成内容高度符合事实；同时增强模型感知能力并具备跨任务泛化能力，优于最佳多候选集成方法。

Conclusion: VCap通过引入细粒度的事实验证机制，显著提升了视觉描述模型的准确性与鲁棒性，为强化学习在视觉语言模型中的应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Visual captioning requires models to capture visual content faithfully while minimizing both omission and hallucination. As the dominant paradigm for captioning, MLLMs have achieved strong performance through scaling and high-quality data. Recently, RL has emerged as a key route to driving MLLMs toward higher precision and broader coverage, however, existing reward designs for captioning fail to provide fine-grained and reliable signals for factual verification, limiting their effectiveness. To address this, we propose VCap, a Witness-Adjudicator reward that pairs the reference caption (a witness) with the visual signal (an adjudicator). By explicitly verifying factual consistency between the reference and policy-generated captions grounded in the visual signal, VCap delivers a reward signal with hypergeometric-distribution-level precision for caption quality verification. This design enables effective learning even from imperfect references, facilitating weak-to-strong generalization in RL training. In our experiments, an 8B model trained with VCap outperforms open- and closed-source SOTA models on multiple image and video captioning benchmarks. Human evaluation further confirms its strong alignment with factual correctness. Additionally, VCap improves MLLM perceptual capability, generalizes across tasks, and surpasses best-of-N distillation, challenging prior assumptions about RLVR.

### [35] [Stay Fair! Ensuring Group Fairness in Diffusion Models Across Guidance Scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28036)
*Myeongsoo Kim,Eunji Kim,Minwoo Chae,Sangwoo Mo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出StayFair，一种在扩散模型中实现跨引导尺度公平性的新方法。通过分解总偏差为模型偏差和引导偏差，发现引导偏差随引导尺度单调增长，主导高引导场景。为此，论文扩展强人口均等性至引导设置，并推导出目标分布保持组比例的条件。StayFair通过调整分类器输出分布或零嵌入偏移来实现公平引导，且不依赖于模型去偏，可与现有公平扩散模型结合使用，在不牺牲图像质量的前提下，解耦公平性与引导尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有去偏技术仅针对单一引导尺度优化，当用户调整引导尺度时，公平性会下降。根本原因在于未考虑引导偏差随引导尺度增加而增长的现象。因此需要一种能够适应不同引导尺度的公平生成方法。

Method: 将总偏差分解为模型偏差和引导偏差；扩展强人口均等性至引导设置；推导目标分布保持组比例的条件；针对分类器引导设计输出分布均衡策略；针对无分类器引导设计提示相关偏移的零嵌入调整；所有修改仅作用于引导步骤，与模型去偏独立。

Result: 在类别条件生成和文生图任务中，StayFair成功实现公平性与引导尺度解耦，无论引导尺度如何变化，均保持公平性，同时维持高质量图像生成效果。

Conclusion: StayFair通过引入对引导偏差的建模与控制，实现了在不同引导尺度下的持续公平性，是一种高效、可叠加的去偏框架，适用于多种扩散模型生成场景。

Abstract: Diffusion models steer conditional generation with a tunable guidance scale to trade off prompt alignment and diversity. However, existing debiasing techniques are optimized for a single scale, degrading fairness when users adjust this parameter. We trace this behavior to a previously overlooked source by decomposing total bias into two components: a model bias and a guidance bias. While prior work primarily targets the former, we show that the guidance bias grows monotonically with the guidance scale, eventually dominating the high-guidance regimes users prefer. To address this, we extend Strong Demographic Parity to guidance and derive a condition under which the target distribution retains its group ratio across guidance scales. We propose StayFair, which leverages this condition to design fair guidance algorithms in both regimes. For classifier guidance, it equalizes the classifier's output distributions across groups; for classifier-free guidance, it shifts the null embedding by a prompt-dependent offset. Because StayFair modifies only the guidance step, it is orthogonal to model debiasing and can be layered onto existing fair diffusion models to extend their fairness across guidance scales. Across class-conditional and text-to-image generation, StayFair decouples fairness from the guidance scale without sacrificing image quality.

</details>


### [36] [Qwen-Image-Bench: From Generation to Creation in Text-to-Image Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28091)
*Niantong Li,Guangzheng Hu,Weixu Qiao,Ying Ba,Qichen Hong,Shijun Shen,Jinlin Wang,Fan Zhou,Jianye Kang,Xin Shang,Ziyi He,Wei Wang,Dalin Li,Jiahao Li,Jie Zhang,Kaiyuan Gao,Kun Yan,Lihan Jiang,Ningyuan Tang,Shengming Yin,Tianhe Wu,Xiao Xu,Xiaoyue Chen,Yuxiang Chen,Yan Shu,Yanran Zhang,Yilei Chen,Yixian Xu,Zekai Zhang,Zhendong Wang,Zihao Liu,Zikai Zhou,Hongzhu Shi,Yi Wang,Bing Zhao,Hu Wei,Lin Qu,Chenfei Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Qwen-Image-Bench 是一个由专业艺术家共同设计的、以创作者为中心的文本到图像生成评估基准，旨在解决现有基准在真实世界还原度和创造性生成方面不足的问题。该基准引入了两个应用驱动维度：真实世界保真度与创意生成，并基于专业艺术创作流程构建了包含23个二级子能力与56个可验证评价标准的分层分类体系。通过1000个分层提示词覆盖多个细粒度方面，结合由80名全球艺术学院专业人士盲评与三重评审训练的统一判别模型Q-Judger（基于Qwen3.6-27B），实现对每张图像在所有56个维度上的细粒度、可追溯诊断评分，显著提升了对先进T2I模型的区分能力，尤其在真实世界保真度与创意生成方面优于传统基准，为生产级T2I开发提供了可信优化信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到图像生成评估基准仍停留在基础的文本-图像对齐层面，无法满足专业创作中对真实世界重建和原创性表达的高阶需求，导致难以有效区分当前最先进的T2I模型。因此亟需一个更贴近真实创作场景、具备细粒度评价能力的新评估体系。

Method: 提出Qwen-Image-Bench，采用自上而下的层级分类结构，涵盖真实世界保真度与创意生成两大应用驱动维度；构建23个二级子能力与56个可验证的三级评价标准；设计1000个分层提示词，每个提示覆盖多个细粒度方面；训练基于Qwen3.6-27B的统一判别模型Q-Judger，由80名全球艺术学院专业人士在盲评与三重评审机制下进行标注监督，实现多维度、可溯源的细粒度评分。

Result: Qwen-Image-Bench 能够有效区分领先T2I模型，在真实世界保真度与创意生成两个关键维度上表现出最强的区分力，填补了现有基准在此方面的空白；提供的细粒度诊断报告为生产级文本到图像模型的优化提供了可靠依据。

Conclusion: Qwen-Image-Bench 是首个面向专业创作实践的文本到图像生成评估基准，其基于真实艺术工作流设计的多维、分层、可验证评价体系，显著提升了评估的准确性与实用性，为未来T2I技术的发展提供了可信的衡量标准与优化方向。

Abstract: Text-to-Image generation has evolved from basic image synthesis into a frequently used core capability in professional creative workflows, where simple text-image alignment can no longer satisfy users' pressing demands for faithful real-world reconstruction and genuine creative expression. Existing benchmarks, however, remain anchored in these foundational criteria and do not yet capture the nuanced capabilities that matter in authentic artistic practice, making it difficult to reliably distinguish state-of-the-art T2I models. To address the gap, we introduce Qwen-Image-Bench, a creator-centric benchmark co-designed with professional artists and grounded in real-world creation scenarios. Qwen-Image-Bench enriches conventional evaluation with two application-driven dimensions: Real-world Fidelity and Creative Generation. Drawing on the staged reasoning inherent in professional artistic workflows, we organize these five pillars into a top-down hierarchical taxonomy that further decomposes into 23 second-level sub-capabilities and 56 third-level verifiable rubrics. To ensure broad coverage, we curate 1000 stratified prompts with each prompt jointly exercising more than four fine-grained facets across multiple pillars. We train a unified judge model Q-Judger based on Qwen3.6-27B, supervised by 80 professional annotators from global art academies under blind labeling and triple-review protocols, that scores every image across all 56 verifiable facets, producing fine-grained, rubric-grounded, and fully attributable diagnostics rather than a single opaque score. Empirically, Qwen-Image-Bench reliably distinguishes leading T2I models, achieving the greatest separation on the two application-driven dimensions of Real-world Fidelity and Creative Generation where existing benchmarks provide little insight, while also providing a trustworthy optimization signal for production-level T2I development.

### [37] [Revisiting Change Detection Methods for their Application to Serac Fall Time-Lapse Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28100)
*Arthur Dérédel,Carlos Crispim-Junior,Pierre Lemaire,Johan Berthet,Laure Tougne Rodet*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对时间序列相机和斜坡不稳定的新型变化检测子任务——体积变化检测。研究回顾了最先进的变化检测方法，分析其核心组件并评估其适用性，引入新数据集SeracFallDet以支持该任务。实验表明，密集和半密集特征匹配在未专门训练的情况下表现稳健，而监督方法受限于数据稀缺和标注不平衡。因此，混合方法可能成为未来方向，凸显特征匹配技术的潜力及实际部署中需进一步创新的需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气候变化加剧环境不确定性，事件前兆的识别与检测对减轻自然灾害影响至关重要。传统传感器（如干涉激光仪或地震仪）虽可靠但部署成本高、存在盲区。时间序列相机提供低成本、高分辨率视觉信息，是潜在替代方案，但自动处理面临极端形状和光照变化的挑战，限制了大规模应用。因此，亟需发展适用于此类场景的高效变化检测方法。

Result: 密集和半密集特征匹配即使未经特定任务训练也表现出鲁棒性能；监督方法受制于数据稀缺和标注不平衡问题，表现不佳；结果表明，结合两种方法优势的混合策略可能是突破当前局限的有效路径。

Conclusion: 特征匹配技术在环境监测中的体积变化检测任务中展现出巨大潜力，但实际大规模部署仍面临挑战，需进一步创新以克服数据、标注和环境复杂性等问题。

Abstract: In an era where climate change aggravates environmental uncertainties, the identification and detection of event precursors are becoming crucial to mitigate the impacts of disastrous natural hazards. While classical sensors such as interferometric lasers or seismometers are reliable, their widespread deployment is often hindered by logistical and economic barriers, leaving numerous blind spots. Time-lapse cameras, which already provide cost-effective, high-resolution visual context to such sensors, present a promising alternative. However, processing their output automatically faces significant challenges, notably linked to extreme shape and lighting variations. Overcoming those issues is essential to deploy them at large-scale as a monitoring tool. This paper introduces a novel sub-task of change detection, namely volumetric change detection, applied to time-lapse cameras and slope instabilities. We conduct a comprehensive review of state-of-the-art change detection methods and related tasks, analyze their core components and assess their applicability to this context. To that end, we introduce the new dataset SeracFallDet, which contains serac fall annotations and has been thoroughly annotated to meet the latter demand. Through generalization experiments, we demonstrate that dense and semi-dense feature matching, although not trained specifically for this task, exhibit robust performance. Alternatively, supervised approaches struggle with data scarcity and annotation imbalance. This suggests that hybrid methods may offer a path forward by leveraging the strengths of both tasks. These findings highlight the potential of feature matching techniques and the need for further innovation to overcome the challenges of real-world deployment in environmental monitoring.

</details>


### [38] [CLEAR-NeRF: Collinearity and Local-region Enhanced Accurate 3D Reconstruction in Unbounded Scenes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28125)
*Vladislav Polianskii,Elijs Dima,Isabel Salmerón Marazuela,Gergő László Nagy,Sigurdur Sverrisson,Volodya Grancharov*

Method: 提出多区域感兴趣区无界场景下的自适应NeRF框架，包含：(i) 自动化局部区域定位与重建以优先处理兴趣区域；(ii) 共线性约束的射线采样以学习平滑表面；(iii) 深度局部邻域点提取以减少表面伪影；(iv) 几何相关颜色聚合以缓解光照和姿态引起的差异。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提方法在多个指标上均优于基准NeRF模型及成熟的SfM-MVS解决方案，展现出更高的重建质量、更强的鲁棒性与更好的度量一致性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了一个适用于复杂无界场景的高保真、度量准确的NeRF重建系统，为数字孪生等高要求应用提供了有效技术支撑。

Abstract: Many real-world 3D reconstruction applications demand photorealism and metric accuracy across unbounded, complex scenes with challenging lighting and imperfect captures that current Neural Radiance Field (NeRF) pipelines only partly satisfy. This study adapts NeRF-based 3D reconstruction to multi-region of interest unbounded scenes to improve robustness to lighting and pose variation while enforcing metric accuracy suitable for digital-twin applications. Our approach introduces (i) automated local region localization/detection and reconstruction to seamlessly prioritize areas of interest without proliferating submodules, (ii) collinearity-enforcing ray sampling to learn smooth planar and curved surfaces, (iii) depth-localized neighborhood point extraction to suppress surface artifacts, and (iv) geometry-relevant color aggregation to mitigate lighting- and pose-caused variations. Results indicate superior performance of the proposed pipeline over the baseline NeRF models and established Structure from Motion (SfM) - Multi-View Stereo (MVS) solutions.

### [39] [Which Pretraining Paradigm Better Serves Spatial Intelligence? An Empirical Comparison of Vision-Language and Video Generation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28132)
*Haozhan Shen,Tiancheng Zhao,Kangjia Zhao,Jianwei Yin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文首次系统地通过冻结特征探测研究了视觉语言模型（VLMs）和视频生成模型（VGMs）在空间智能三个关键维度上的表现：语义标记、实例分组和3D几何预测。实验表明，VLMs在语义和实例分组上更优，而VGMs在密集几何和相机运动信号方面更具优势，二者融合可同时提升几何与语义能力，提示未来构建更强空间智能基础模型的方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前空间智能依赖于能同时捕捉语义对象与几何结构的视觉表征，但视觉语言模型（VLMs）与视频生成模型（VGMs）哪一种更适合作为基础表示尚不明确，亟需系统性比较以揭示其各自优势与互补性。

Method: 采用轻量级探测器对冻结的VLM和VGM特征进行系统性探测，评估其在语义标记、实例分组和3D几何预测三个任务上的表现，实现可控对比。

Result: VLMs在语义标记和实例分组任务中表现更优；VGMs在密集几何与相机运动预测中提供更易提取的信号；简单融合两者特征即可在几何与语义任务上均取得优异表现。

Conclusion: VLMs与VGMs在空间智能表征上具有明显互补性，有效融合二者特征是构建更强空间智能基础模型的可行路径。

Abstract: Spatial intelligence requires visual representations that capture both semantic objects and geometric structure in the physical world. To support this, two major pre-training schemes are now widely used as foundation backbones: Vision-Language Models (VLMs), which use language supervision to align visual observations with semantic concepts, and Video Generation Models (VGMs), which learn from temporally evolving visual worlds. However, it still remains unclear which pre-training scheme provides a better representation substrate for spatial intelligence. In this paper, we present the first systematic frozen-feature probing study of VLMs and VGMs across three representative axes of spatial intelligence: semantic tagging, instance grouping, and 3D geometry prediction. Using the lightweight probe, our framework enables a controlled comparison of what information is already encoded in frozen representations from two model families. Experimental results reveal a clear complementarity: VLMs are stronger at semantic tagging and instance grouping, while VGMs provide more accessible signals for dense geometry and camera motion. Moreover, a naive fusion of the two already yields a representation that excels at both geometry and semantics, suggesting a promising direction for building stronger spatial-intelligence backbones by effectively integrating features from both model families. Our code is available at \href{https://github.com/om-ai-lab/Probing-VLM-VGM}{https://github.com/om-ai-lab/Probing-VLM-VGM}.

### [40] [No Safe Dose: How Training Data Drives Unsafe Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28137)
*Felix Friedrich,Lukas Helff,Niharika Hegde,Patrick Schramowski,Kristian Kersting*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究通过控制训练数据中不安全图像的比例（0%至9.6%），在不同数据规模下训练相同文本到图像模型，发现输出不安全性随不安全数据比例单调上升，且比例是关键变量而非绝对数量。即使在零污染情况下仍存在16.6%的基线不安全性，表明冻结的文本编码器等组件也带来残留风险；使用SafeCLIP可将基线降至9.6%，但剂量反应效应依然存在。安全性提升未伴随生成质量下降，说明数据净化与文本编码器安全为互补且独立有效的干预手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究训练数据组成是否直接驱动文本到图像模型输出安全性，以及其与其他因素（如冻结文本编码器）的关系，以明确安全风险来源并提出有效干预策略。

Method: 在多个数据规模（10万至800万样本）下，仅改变不安全图像占比（0%至9.6%），训练相同模型，并使用四种独立的安全分类器评估生成图像的安全性；采用因子设计分析比例与绝对数量的影响；通过文本编码器消融实验验证编码器对残留风险的作用。

Result: 输出不安全性从0%污染时的16.6%升至5%污染时的25.5%；比例是决定性因素，而非绝对数量；零污染下的16.6%基线揭示了其他组件（如冻结文本编码器）的残留风险；使用SafeCLIP可将基线降至9.6%，但剂量反应效应持续存在；安全性提升未导致FID、CLIPscore和ImageReward等质量指标下降。

Conclusion: 数据净化与文本编码器安全性是互补且独立有效的安全干预手段；尽管如此，当前模型仍存在不可忽视的残余不安全性，提示未来研究需关注新兴能力与组合性带来的新挑战。

Abstract: Text-to-image models trained on large-scale data often inevitably ingest unsafe content. While some people observe input-output amplifications, it remains unclear whether and how training data composition directly drives model output safety or by other factors. We shed light on this question by isolating this variable: we train the same text-to-image model on datasets that differ \emph{only} in their fraction of unsafe images (0\% to 9.6\%), across several dataset scales (100K to 8M). Then we generate images with the resulting models, and evaluate them with four independent safety classifiers. Output unsafety rises monotonically from 16.6\% at 0\% contamination to 25.5\% at 5\%. A factorial design reveals that the \emph{proportion}, not the absolute count, of unsafe training images is the operative variable. The 16.6\% irreducible baseline at zero contamination implicates the other components, e.g. frozen text encoder, as a residual safety risk -- confirmed by a text encoder ablation showing that SafeCLIP reduces this floor to 9.6\%, while the dose-response effect persists across all three encoders tested. Critically, no quality degradation in terms of FID, CLIPscore and ImageReward accompanies safety filtering. These results establish that data curation and text encoder safety are complementary and independently effective interventions. At the same time, the remaining level of unsafety poses questions for future research about emerging capabilities and compositionality.

</details>

Method: 利用深度学习技术分析口腔内照片，通过训练模型识别龋齿与MIH的特征，结合图像预处理和特征提取方法，提升病变检测的准确性与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Clinical diagnosis of meniscus injuries requires radiologists to integrate volumetric MRI evidence with patient context (e.g., sex, age, BMI) and to produce structured diagnostic reports. ### [43] [DebFilter: Eradicating Biases Stashed in Value](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28167)
*Seung Hyuk Lee,Songkuk Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DebFilter框架，一种无需训练、在推理阶段即可减轻文本到图像扩散模型中社会偏见的轻量级方法。通过调整跨注意力机制中的值组件，施加固定偏移以引导语义方向至无偏表示，从而在不损害文本对齐的前提下实现更均衡的生成结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到图像扩散模型受预训练视觉-语言模型（如CLIP）中固有的性别、年龄等社会和语义偏见影响，这些偏见在多步去噪过程中被放大，导致生成图像出现偏差。需要一种无需重新训练或微调的高效偏见缓解方法。

Method: 基于观察到模型每一步去噪误差主要受跨注意力动态影响，提出在推理时对跨注意力的值部分施加固定偏移，调整引导嵌入的特定切片，以改变得分景观并实现无偏生成。该方法完全在推理阶段执行，不依赖额外数据或模型更新。

Result: 实验表明，DebFilter能有效缓解生成图像中的社会偏见，提升输出公平性，同时保持与原始文本描述的一致性，具有高效性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: DebFilter是一种无需训练的推理阶段偏见缓解框架，通过简单调整跨注意力值实现对社会偏见的有效抑制，为构建更公平、包容的文本到图像生成系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Text-to-image diffusion models, which are theoretically equivalent to score-based generative models, generate images through a multi-step denoising process guided by text embeddings extracted from pretrained vision-language models such as CLIP. However, these text embeddings inherently encode social and semantic biases -- such as those related to gender and age -- that are subsequently propagated and amplified through the guidance mechanism, along with the model's training on large-scale datasets that are imbalanced with respect to these bias-related concepts, often leading to skewed outputs in text-to-image generation. We propose DebFilter, a lightweight and training-free framework for mitigating such biases in text-to-image diffusion models. Observing that the model's error prediction at each denoising step is primarily influenced by cross-attention dynamics, we introduce a bias-correction strategy that adjusts the value components within cross-attention. Specifically, we apply a fixed offset to the slice of guidance embedding, effectively steering the semantic direction of cross-attention values toward unbiased representations. This adjustment reconfigures the score landscape to produce balanced outputs while maintaining alignment with the intended text semantics. Unlike prior approaches that rely on fine-tuning or retraining, DebFilter operates entirely at inference time, requiring no additional data or model updates. Our results demonstrate that this method effectively mitigates social biases in generated images, offering an efficient and scalable pathway toward fairer and more inclusive text-to-image generation.

</details>

### [44] [ICG: Improving Cover Image Generation via MLLM-based Prompting and Personalized Preference Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27374)
*Zhipeng Bian,Jieming Zhu,Qijiong Liu,Wang Lin,Guohao Cai,Zhaocheng Du,Jiacheng Sun,Zhou Zhao,Zhenhua Dong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ICG是一种新颖的框架，结合多模态大语言模型（MLLM）提示与个性化偏好对齐，用于生成高质量、上下文相关的个性化封面图像。该框架通过元标记提取项目标题和参考图像的语义特征，利用用户嵌入进行优化，并将个性化上下文注入扩散模型。为解决缺乏标注监督的问题，采用融合公共美学与相关性奖励及基于用户行为训练的个性化偏好模型的多奖励学习策略。不同于依赖手工提示和分离模块的先前方法，ICG使用适配器实现MLLM与扩散模型之间的端到端训练。实验表明，ICG显著提升了图像质量、语义保真度和个性化程度，增强了用户吸引力并提高了下游任务中的离线推荐准确性。作为可即插即用的适配器，ICG兼容常见检查点且无需在优化过程中使用真实标签。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 个性化封面图像生成在提升数字平台用户参与度方面具有重要作用，但当前研究仍较为薄弱。现有方法依赖于手工设计的提示词和孤立的模块化流程，难以有效捕捉用户个性化偏好，且缺乏有效的监督信号。因此，亟需一种能够整合多模态理解与个性化偏好、支持端到端训练并减少对标注数据依赖的新框架。

Method: ICG框架首先利用元标记从项目标题和参考图像中提取语义特征，再通过用户嵌入对特征进行个性化调优，最终将融合后的上下文信息注入扩散模型以生成封面图像。为避免依赖人工标注，引入多奖励学习机制，结合公开的美学与相关性奖励以及基于用户行为数据训练的个性化偏好模型。同时，设计一个适配器模块，实现多模态大语言模型与扩散模型之间的无缝连接，支持端到端训练。

Result: 实验结果显示，ICG在图像质量、语义一致性及个性化表现上均优于现有方法，在用户吸引力和下游推荐任务的离线评估中也表现出更强的效果。此外，该框架具备良好的兼容性，可适配主流预训练模型，且在训练过程中无需真实标签，具有较强的实用性与扩展性。

Conclusion: ICG提出了一种高效、可扩展的个性化封面图像生成框架，通过融合多模态理解与用户偏好建模，实现了高质量、高相关性的内容生成。其无需标注数据、支持即插即用的特点，使其在实际应用中具有广泛前景，为AI生成内容领域提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) and diffusion models (DMs) have opened new possibilities for AI-generated content. Yet, personalized cover image generation remains underexplored, despite its critical role in boosting user engagement on digital platforms. We propose ICG, a novel framework that integrates MLLM-based prompting with personalized preference alignment to generate high-quality, contextually relevant covers. ICG extracts semantic features from item titles and reference images via meta tokens, refines them with user embeddings, and injects the resulting personalized context into the diffusion model. To address the lack of labeled supervision, we adopt a multi-reward learning strategy that combines public aesthetic and relevance rewards with a personalized preference model trained from user behavior. Unlike prior pipelines relying on handcrafted prompts and disjointed modules, ICG employs an adapter to bridge MLLMs and diffusion models for end-to-end training. Experiments demonstrate that ICG significantly improves image quality, semantic fidelity, and personalization, leading to stronger user appeal and offline recommendation accuracy in downstream tasks. As a plug-and-play adapter bridging MLLMs and diffusion models, ICG is compatible with common checkpoints and requires no ground-truth labels during optimization.
