### [45] [Unlocking Fine-Grained and Within-Utterance Speaking Style Control in Prompt-Based Text-to-Speech Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27376)
*Jaehoon Kang,Yejin Lee,Yoonji Park,Kyuhong Shim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出新方法，使现有基于提示的文本到语音（TTS）模型实现跨语句风格插值和语句内风格动态变化。通过计算风格提示在嵌入空间中的方向向量并进行插值，实现自然流畅的风格过渡；针对自回归TTS解码器中早期标记的注意力偏见问题，引入KV缓存交换与滑动窗口注意力掩码机制，缓解初始音频对后续生成的主导影响。实验表明，跨语句风格转换成功率高达99-100%，可实现最大36 Hz音高变化及1.6音节/秒的语速调整；语句内风格过渡保持说话人相似性0.81-0.91，感知平滑度得分达3.48-4.48。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于提示的文本到语音模型虽支持自然语言驱动的风格控制，但缺乏细粒度控制能力，且在整句中采用单一全局风格，难以满足需要连续风格插值和时变风格转换的实际应用需求。

Method: 提出两种技术：1）通过计算对比风格提示在嵌入空间中的方向向量并进行线性插值，实现跨语句风格平滑过渡；2）针对自回归解码器中早期令牌的注意力偏见问题，引入KV缓存交换与滑动窗口注意力掩码，以抑制初始音频对后续生成的过度影响，实现语句内的风格动态变化。

Result: 跨语句风格插值在性别转换任务中达到99-100%成功率，支持最高36 Hz音高变化和1.6音节/秒的语速变化；语句内风格转换保持说话人相似性0.81-0.91，感知平滑度得分为3.48-4.48，表现出良好的自然性和连贯性。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效扩展了现有提示式TTS模型的能力，使其具备跨语句风格插值与语句内风格动态变换的双重能力，为更灵活、自然的语音合成提供了可行路径。

Abstract: While prompt-based text-to-speech (TTS) models enable natural language-driven speaking style control, they often provide limited fine-grained control and apply a single global style across an utterance. This restricts practical use cases that require continuous style attribute interpolation across utterances and time-varying style transitions within a single utterance. In this paper, we propose novel techniques to achieve both capabilities in existing prompt-based TTS models. For inter-utterance style interpolation, we compute direction vectors between contrastive style prompts in the embedding space and perform simple interpolation, enabling smooth transitions between style characteristics. For intra-utterance style transition, we first identify a strong attention bias toward early tokens in autoregressive TTS decoders, causing the initial audio realization to dominate subsequent generation. To mitigate this effect, we introduce KV-cache swapping and sliding-window attention masking. Experiments demonstrate that our proposed inter-utterance interpolation achieves a 99-100% success rate in gender conversion, up to 36 Hz pitch variation, and up to 1.6 syllables-per-second speed change. Our intra-utterance transition maintains a speaker similarity of 0.81-0.91 and achieves perceptual smoothness scores of 3.48-4.48.

</details>

Conclusion: Integrating external knowledge through a multi-agent system significantly improves ICD-10-CM coding performance, and the release of MDACE-2025 enables evaluation against current clinical standards.

Abstract: We present RAG-Coding, an agentic method for automated ICD-10-CM coding. RAG-Coding orchestrates four large language model (LLM) agents and grounds their coding decisions in external knowledge sources (e.g. the official coding tabular list and guidelines). By retrieving and cross-referencing relevant knowledge in these sources, the agents enhance coding accuracy and ensure clinical compliance. On the MDACE dataset, RAG-Coding outperforms the best LLM-based baseline by 8-13\% in micro-F1 and 2-8\% in macro-F1 across multiple LLM backbones. Compared to the state-of-the-art pretrained language model method, PLM-ICD, RAG-Coding exhibits higher micro recall (+11\%), while PLM-ICD exhibits higher micro precision (+6\%), yielding comparable micro- and macro-F1. Ablations show stepwise gains, highlighting the importance of incorporating external knowledge. We also release MDACE-2025, updating the original dataset with expert re-annotations with the latest 2025 ICD-10-CM guidelines. ### [47] [BioELX: Cross-lingual Biomedical Entity Linking via Alias-based Retrieval and LLM Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27380)
*Yi Wang,Corina Dima,Liangyu Zhong,Steffen Staab*

Method: 提出 BioELX 两阶段框架：第一阶段用维基数据生成的多语言别名扩充 SapBERT 的训练数据，优化跨语言候选检索；第二阶段采用预训练大语言模型作为排序器，联合考虑提及上下文与候选实体进行无监督消歧。

Conclusion: BioELX 不依赖人工标注数据，有效提升了跨语言生物医学实体链接的性能，尤其在低资源语言上表现突出，为多语言生物医学 NLP 提供了一种高效、可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Cross-lingual biomedical entity linking (BEL) maps mentions in any language to unique identifiers in a biomedical knowledge base (KB), supporting clinical and biomedical NLP applications. However, expert-annotated training data for BEL are costly, especially for low-resource languages. Moreover, many cross-lingual BEL systems rely on SapBERT-based retrievers trained on predominantly English aliases in the KB, leading to poor generalization to unseen non-English mentions and limited context-aware disambiguation. We propose BioELX, a two-stage cross-lingual BEL framework that requires no task-specific annotated training corpora. In Stage~1, we enrich SapBERT training with Wikidata-derived multilingual aliases and use the resulting retriever to improve cross-lingual candidate retrieval. In Stage~2, we perform context-aware disambiguation with a pre-trained LLM ranker that jointly considers the mention context and candidate, eliminating the need for supervised training. Experiments on five benchmarks (XL-BEL, EMEA, Patent, WikiMed-DE, and MedMentions) show that BioELX achieves new state-of-the-art performance. It improves average Recall@1 on XL-BEL by +19.2, with especially large gains for low-resource languages, e.g., +21.6 on Turkish, +22.1 on Korean, +30.8 on Thai, and delivers consistent improvements on EMEA (+6.2), Patent (+5.4), and WikiMed-DE (+12.8). Code and resources will be released upon publication.

### [48] [Bridging the Stability-Expressivity Gap: Synthetic Data Scaling and Preference Alignment for Low-Resource Spoken Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27383)
*Yizhong Geng,Yanliang Li,Jinghan Yang,Tianhan Jiang,Boxun An,Ya Li,Xiaoyu Shen*

Method: 提出两种自对齐框架：1）基于解耦引导的自对齐（DGSA），利用韵律与音色分离机制恢复表达力；2）温度驱动的自批判（TDSC），通过自动化探索与过滤提升生成稳定性，适用于真实参考数据极度有限的情况。

Conclusion: 合成数据虽能提升音素准确性，但会削弱韵律多样性，导致表达力下降。通过引入解耦引导自对齐与温度驱动自批判机制，可有效弥合稳定性-表达力差距，显著提升低资源语言语音合成质量，尤其在零样本场景下具备突破性潜力。

Abstract: Spoken Language Models (SLMs) have emerged as a promising paradigm for speech synthesis by bypassing explicit grapheme-to-phoneme pipelines. However, their effectiveness in low-resource languages remains fundamentally limited by the scarcity of transcribed speech. In practice, synthetic data has become the primary strategy for scaling SLMs in such settings, providing reliable phonetic supervision when real data is insufficient. In this work, we show that this reliance introduces a fundamental trade-off, which we term the Stability-Expressivity Gap: while synthetic data improves phonetic accuracy, it progressively suppresses prosodic variability, ultimately leading to a collapse of expressivity (Synthetic Erosion). To bridge this gap, we propose two self-alignment frameworks. Disentanglement-Guided Self-Alignment (DGSA) recovers expressivity for complex languages by exploiting prosody-timbre separation. For regimes where authentic references are exceptionally limited, Temperature-Driven Self-Critique (TDSC) stabilizes generation through automated exploration and filtering. Our approach outperforms strong commercial systems, including ElevenLabs and Gemini Pro, and enables the first zero-shot voice cloning capability for Lao.

Analysis further identifies divergent behavioral signatures among frontier models, suggesting that current alignment strategies remain insufficient for capturing the sociolinguistic dynamics of online groups.

### [51] [EvoSpec: Evolving Speculative Decoding via Real-Time Vocabulary and Parameter AdaptationTarget](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27390)

To address this, we introduce EvoSpec, a framework that enables real-time evolution of the draft model through dynamic vocabulary and parameter adaptation. Unlike static or purely retrieval-based approaches, EvoSpec employs a context-aware mechanism that retrieves critical long-tail tokens via efficient semantic and statistical indexing. Furthermore, we propose a lightweight online alignment strategy utilizing curriculum learning to continually minimize the distributional gap between the draft and target models. ### [52] [Debate Helps Weak Judges Reward Stronger Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27483)
*Ethan Elasky,Frank Nakasako,Naman Goyal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究探讨了在可程序化验证的代码与逻辑任务中，强辩论者/弱裁判设置下的提议者-批评者辩论机制的有效性。结果显示，当批评者具备明显优于裁判的分类能力，并且裁判将批评视为需验证的主张而非仅需总结的证词时，辩论能显著提升裁判表现；而在批评者与裁判能力相近的情况下，辩论效果为零，且裁判的验证率大幅下降。此外，移除反驳环节对裁判表现无显著影响，单一独立批评即可实现辩论的主要收益。研究建议采用更低成本的训练无关可扩展监督范式（答案、批评、裁判），并提出一个预部署审计方法：评估批评者是否优于裁判，以及裁判是否愿意验证其主张，以预测辩论是否有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管辩论作为一种可扩展的监督协议具有理论潜力，但其实际应用结果不一，在某些场景下有效，而在其他场景下则无效，尤其当裁判无法获取隐藏信息时。因此，亟需理解辩论在何种条件下真正有效，以优化其应用并设计更高效的监督机制。

Method: 在可程序化验证的代码和逻辑任务上，采用强辩论者/弱裁判设置，对比提议者-批评者辩论与咨询基线的表现。通过控制批评者的分类能力与裁判能力的相对水平，分析裁判如何处理批评内容（作为待验证的主张或仅作为证词），并考察移除反驳环节的影响。

Result: 在五组配对中的三组中，当批评者能力显著优于裁判且裁判将其视为需验证的主张时，辩论相对于咨询基线有统计学显著提升；而在另外两组中，由于批评者与裁判能力接近，裁判将批评视为证词，导致辩论无效，且裁判验证率下降数十个百分点。移除反驳环节后，裁判性能无明显变化，单一独立批评即可恢复辩论的大部分优势。

Conclusion: 辩论在可验证领域中作为训练无关的可扩展监督机制具有潜力，但其有效性高度依赖于批评者的能力优势及裁判对批评内容的正确解读方式。建议采用‘答案-批评-裁判’框架，并在部署前进行关键审计：检查批评者是否胜过裁判，以及裁判是否愿意验证其主张，从而预测辩论能否带来实际增益。

Abstract: Despite theoretical promise, debate as a scalable oversight protocol has produced mixed empirical results: gains in some settings, and null effects in others, especially when the judge does not have information hidden from it. We study proposer-critic debate in a stronger-debater/weaker-judge setting on programmatically verifiable code and logic tasks. Debate helps the judge over a consultancy baseline when the critic provides a usable advantage: the critic's classification ability must exceed the judge's, and the judge must treat critic speeches as claims to verify rather than testimony to summarize.
  On the three of five pairings where the condition holds, proposer-critic debate's gains are statistically significant over consultancy, and these pairings are the most capable model pairings. On the two non-responder pairings in our set, debate produces null effects, and judge verification rates drop by tens of percentage points once a critic enters the transcript. In these cases the critic's binary-classification ability and the judge's are within noise of each other, and the critic's disagreement is parsed as testimony rather than a claim to check.
  Ablating rebuttal rounds from debate produces no measurable change in judge performance: a single independent critique recovers the bulk of debate's benefit at lower inference cost. These findings suggest a cheaper primitive for training-free scalable oversight in verifiable domains (answer, critique, judge) and a pre-deployment audit (does the critic beat the judge, and will the judge verify it?) that predicts when debate will help.

</details>


### [53] [PAST2HARM: A Simple Adaptive Past Tense Attack for Jailbreaking Multimodal AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27545)
*Snehasis Mukhopadhyay*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PAST2HARM 是一种针对多模态生成模型的自适应越狱攻击框架，利用过去时重构策略绕过拒绝训练。通过时间深度增强历史锚定与档案线索，系统性地削弱不同对齐强度模型的拒绝对策边界；同时通过迭代升级探测有害生成上限，发现对话中段为最脆弱窗口期。在 Gemini Nano Banana Pro、GPT Image 2 和 SD XL 上分别实现 83%、67%、100% 的攻击成功率，且跨模型迁移效果良好（超 50%），可生成包括色情内容、政治虚假信息、历史否认、仇恨言论和自残美化等多样有害输出。研究发布了一个用于红队测试与对齐研究的提示、重写及输出基准集，揭示当前多模态安全机制的根本脆弱性，呼吁加强多模态安全训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态生成模型的安全防护机制相对不成熟，尤其在图像生成方面存在严重风险，但相关越狱攻击研究仍不足。现有防御措施易被规避，亟需系统性评估其脆弱性并推动更有效的安全机制发展。

Method: 提出 PAST2HARM 框架，基于过去时重构策略，从两个维度实施攻击：一是‘广度’——通过时间深度增强历史锚定与档案线索，逐步侵蚀模型拒绝边界；二是‘深度’——在初始合规后进行迭代升级，使用语言模型作为裁判评估生成内容的严重程度，量化危害性。

Result: 在三个主流模型上实现高攻击成功率（83%、67%、100%），攻击具有显著跨模型迁移能力（>50%），能诱发多种类型的有害输出，包括色情、虚假信息、仇恨言论、自残美化等。研究还构建了首个公开的多模态越狱攻击基准数据集，支持后续安全研究。

Conclusion: 当前多模态大模型的安全机制存在根本性脆弱性，尤其对基于时序重构的越狱攻击极为敏感。该研究揭示了现有对齐训练的局限性，强调必须强化多模态系统的安全训练与评估体系，以应对日益复杂的对抗性威胁。

Abstract: Jailbreak attacks on multimodal AI systems remain underexplored, even though unsafe image generation can have more severe consequences than unsafe text and current defenses are relatively immature. We introduce PAST2HARM, a simple yet effective adaptive jailbreak framework that bypasses refusal training in state of the art multimodal text to image models. Building on prior findings that past tense reformulations can evade safeguards, PAST2HARM systematically exploits this vulnerability in multimodal generative AI.
  We characterize the attack along two dimensions. First, breadth: through temporal deepening, the framework incrementally strengthens historical anchoring and archival cues, eroding refusal boundaries across models with varying alignment strength. Second, depth: via iterative escalation after initial compliance, we probe the upper bound of harmful generation, measuring severity using a scalar severity jailbreak metric evaluated by a language model acting as a judge. We find that mid conversation turns form peak vulnerability windows, where harmfulness increases before plateauing and eventually undergoing semantic inversion.
  We evaluate PAST2HARM on three models Gemini Nano Banana Pro, GPT Image 2, and SD XL achieving attack success rates of 83 percent, 67 percent, and 100 percent in a black box, gradient free setting. Adversarial prompts also transfer across models, with cross model success rates above 50 percent. The attack elicits diverse harmful outputs, including explicit sexual content, political disinformation, historical denial narratives, hate speech, and self harm glorification. We further release a curated benchmark of prompts, reformulations, and outputs as a resource for red teaming and alignment. Our results expose fundamental brittleness in current safeguards and highlight the need for stronger multimodal safety training.

</details>


### [54] [The Future of Facts: Tracing the Factual Generation-Verification Gap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27564)
*Tim R. Davidson,Anja Surina,Caglar Gulcehre*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了语言模型在生成与验证事实知识时的差距（GV-gap），发现验证能力通常先于生成能力被学习，且在持续学习中更具鲁棒性；此外，事实更新可能导致模型同时认可新旧答案，形成‘多宇宙’状态。这些现象在不同规模的开源模型及前沿模型中均得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解语言模型在生成和验证事实知识时的差异机制，特别是训练过程中如何影响这两种能力的发展，以揭示自改进和推理技术背后的原理。

Method: 通过追踪四个开源模型家族在两个规模下的三个训练阶段（获取、持续学习、更新）中的生成与验证能力，结合自然实验分析前沿模型的表现，系统比较不同条件下的动态变化。

Result: 发现验证能力普遍早于生成能力出现，对持续学习更鲁棒，且事实更新可能使模型同时接受新旧答案，表现出‘多宇宙’状态；前沿模型也显示出在广泛覆盖的事实上的残留验证偏差。

Conclusion: 语言模型在事实知识上的生成-验证差距具有可追溯的训练机制基础，验证能力更稳定且优先发展，这为改进模型自我校正和知识更新策略提供了关键洞见。

Abstract: Language models are becoming the default interface to factual knowledge, yet they often verify outputs more reliably than they generate them. This generation-verification gap (GV-gap) underlies many recent advances in self-improvement and reasoning, but its dynamics on factual knowledge specifically remain poorly understood. We focus on the training mechanisms underlying factual GV-gaps, distinguishing them from their computational and aesthetic counterparts. We trace generation and verification capabilities through three training phases (acquisition, continual learning, and updating) across four open-source model families at two scales each. Three findings recur across models: (i) verification is consistently learned before generation; (ii) verification is more robust to continual learning than generation; and (iii) factual updates can leave models in a "multi-verse" state, simultaneously verifying both old and new answers as correct. Natural experiments on frontier models reproduce these dynamics at scale and reveal residual verification biases on well-covered facts.

### [55] [Can Hallucinations Be Useful? Solving Multi-Hop Questions With SLMs By Chaining System-I/II Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27596)
*Saptarshi Sengupta,Suhang Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种反向思维策略：先回答后推理（answer first-reason later），针对小语言模型（SLMs）易幻觉的问题。与传统先思考再检索不同，该方法让模型先快速生成初始答案（System-I），再基于此假设从知识源中检索证据进行深度推理（System-II）。实验表明，该框架在多个多步问答基准上优于传统think-first方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法采用think-first策略以减少幻觉，但发现SLMs在初始回答时往往自信且准确，且幻觉可能有助于逼近正确答案。因此，作者认为无需强制先思考，可尝试反向策略以提升性能。

Method: 提出一种受认知启发的双系统框架：首先使用零样本方式快速生成初始答案（System-I），然后基于该答案从外部知识源检索证据，并进行深度推理（System-II），结合两种思维方式以提高准确性。

Result: 所提方法在多个多步问答基准测试中表现优于传统think-first方法，证明了answer-first-reason-later策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过逆向思维策略，利用SLMs的快速响应能力与后续证据驱动的深度推理相结合，可在不增加复杂度的前提下显著降低幻觉影响，提升多步推理任务的表现。

Abstract: Recently, there has been increased interest in Small Language Models (SLMs), which are fast, show good performance, and have lower hardware demands than large language models (LLMs). However, SLMs hallucinate more frequently than LLMs, impacting their ability to solve complex multi-step reasoning problems as early mistakes cascade to the final response. To address this, existing works think-first followed by iterative retrieval to reduce hallucination. We argue that the think-first strategy is not always necessary as we find that: (i) SLMs are often accurately confident in their initial answer and, (ii) hallucinations can actually be beneficial for honing in on the true answer. As such, we position our work as an inversion of this strategy, i.e., answer first-reason later. We propose a cognitively-inspired framework where the model is first allowed to quickly answer the question (System-I (zero-shot)) and then resorts to deeper thinking (System-II) based on evidence retrieved from a knowledge source using the initial hypothesis. By combining System-I and System-II style thinking, we show that our method can outperform prior work that takes the traditional think-first route on various multi-step question-answering benchmarks.

Conclusion: 尽管检索增强策略提升了跨语言表现，但训练数据不平衡仍是制约模型性能的关键因素，未来需进一步优化数据分布与检索机制以实现更公平的多语言支持。

Abstract: Although Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate excellent capabilities and performance for general reasoning tasks within the general public domain, they may face challenges with culturally grounded knowledge within languages with limited digital and textual data. In this paper, we investigate culturally grounded multiple-choice question answering with the BLEnD benchmark, which consists of a multilingual corpus of 30 languages and covers various socio-cultural domains, such as cuisine, sports, family, etc. We propose a region-aware hybrid retrieval approach that combines BM25 lexical matching and dense semantic similarity with regional weighting heuristics to improve the relevance of the answer. The retrieved documents are used to construct a structured prompt for the Qwen3-14B quantized model with logit-based deterministic answer selection. The experimental results show improvements to cross-lingual stability with the hybrid retrieval approach over pure parametric inference for culturally grounded question answering. However, there are still notable performance gaps between languages with more and less training data. In particular, in both quantitative and qualitative comparisons on multiple Datasets of Datasets (DoDs), we demonstrate that our translator produces fluent, accurate verbalizations that outperforms existing training-free methods like InSPEcT. In addition to advancing interpretability, our work suggests a promising downstream application: soft prompts optimized on small, open-source models can be translated into portable text prompts that, when deployed on larger closed-API models, exceed the performance of the original soft prompt and, in some cases, even few-shot learning.

### [58] [Disentangling Language Roles in Multilingual LLM Task Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27649)
*Qishi Zhan,Minxuan Hu,Seoyeon Jang,Lei Zhao,Ziheng Chen,Man Liang,Xinyue Xiang,Jiaxin Liu,Guansu Wang,Liang He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MTM-Bench 是一个全交叉设计的多语言指令遵循评估基准，系统评估语言角色在任务执行中的影响。通过27种语言组合（英语、西班牙语、中文）覆盖指令、内容与响应语言的三元组，共包含2,430个实例，涵盖语义反转、最终状态提取和语言纯度等任务类型。使用分解指标评估20个前沿及开源大模型，包括语义正确性、目标语言遵从性、约束满足度、污染率和联合成功率，并经人工审核验证。结果表明，性能下降主要由语言在任务结构中的角色决定，而非仅语言不匹配数量；响应语言角色是主要变异轴，单一响应槽不匹配导致最大性能下降。此外，不匹配数量并非单调预测难度，不同模型间排序差异显著，任务失败路径各异，说明仅关注语义正确性不足以衡量多语言任务执行能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准未能充分隔离指令、源内容和响应语言的角色，缺乏对多语言任务中语言角色影响的系统评估。为填补这一空白，需要一个控制良好的全交叉设计来精确分析语言角色对任务执行的影响。

Method: 提出MTM-Bench，采用全交叉设计构建三元组 $(L_{\text{instr}}, L_{\text{content}}, L_{\text{resp}})$，覆盖英语、西班牙语、中文之间的所有27种组合；每个任务类型（语义反转、最终状态提取、语言纯度+更新实现）生成2,430个实例；使用分解指标评估模型表现，并通过针对性的人工审计验证评分可靠性。

Result: 实验揭示性能下降主要由语言在任务结构中的角色决定，而非简单的不匹配数量。响应语言角色是主导因素，单一响应槽不匹配导致最严重退化。不匹配数量与难度之间无单调关系，不同模型间排序不一致。不同任务类型以不同机制失败，表明仅语义正确性无法全面反映多语言任务执行能力。

Conclusion: MTM-Bench 证明了语言角色在多语言任务执行中的核心作用，强调应超越简单匹配数评估，重视语言在任务结构中的功能定位。未来模型设计需更精细地建模语言角色与任务逻辑的关系。

Abstract: Multilingual LLMs are increasingly used when instruction, source content, and required response languages do not coincide. Existing benchmarks have expanded multilingual instruction-following evaluation, but they rarely isolate these three roles within a fully crossed design. We introduce MTM-Bench, a controlled benchmark for language-conditioned task execution in which each instance is defined by a triplet \((L_{\text{instr}}, L_{\text{content}}, L_{\text{resp}})\). Across English, Spanish, and Chinese, MTM-Bench enumerates all 27 triplets and contains 2{,}430 instances per model across semantic reversal, final-state extraction, and language purity with update realization. We evaluate 20 frontier and open-weight LLMs using decomposed metrics for semantic correctness, target-language adherence, constraint satisfaction, contamination ratio, and joint success, with scoring validated by a targeted human audit. The fully crossed design reveals that degradation is organized by the role a language occupies in the task structure, not merely by mismatch count. The response-language role is the dominant axis of variation, and a single response-slot mismatch accounts for most degradation. The response-only and full-mismatch comparison suggests that mismatch count is not a monotonic predictor of difficulty, with model-level ordering varying across systems. Task families fail through distinct channels, showing that semantic correctness alone does not capture reliable multilingual task execution.

</details>


### [59] [Cultural Fidelity in English-to-Hindi Translation: A Preservation-Fluency Frontier for Gender Recoverability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27654)
*Samyak Savi,Chavi Gupta,Shreyas Gantayet,Tanay Sodha,Dhruv Kumar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨生成式翻译系统在文化翻译中的作用，重点关注英语到印地语翻译中性别线索的保留问题。通过一个包含37,345个实例的基准测试，发现五个系统常因使用及物性和敬语结构而消除性别信息。为此提出两种基于机制的推理时干预方法：源感知重排序器（SAR）和现象感知重排序器（PAR）。PAR在GPT-4o-mini和Sarvam上分别将目标子集准确率从11.07%和15.99%提升至54.47%和49.66%，人类评估显示性别保留率从10.3%升至81.3%，但流畅度从4.36降至3.37。结果揭示了保真度、流畅性与风格自然性之间的权衡，表明文化情境下的生成需明确取舍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式翻译不仅是语言转换工具，更是文化技术，其决策影响社会意义线索在特定文化语法系统中的呈现。当前系统在跨语言翻译中常无意抹除性别等关键社会属性，尤其在英语转印地语时表现明显。因此亟需建立可衡量的文化翻译成功标准，并设计针对性干预以增强文化敏感性。

Method: 构建涵盖十二类场景的37,345实例基准数据集，评估多个主流模型在性别线索保留方面的表现；提出两种推理阶段干预机制：源感知重排序器（SAR）通过避免性别中性句法提升保留能力；现象感知重排序器（PAR）通过引入特定词汇标记，在保留及物性结构的同时强化性别表达。

Result: 五种主流系统普遍存在性别信息丢失问题，尤其在使用及物性和敬语结构时。引入PAR后，两个模型的目标子集准确率显著提升（分别达54.47%和49.66%），人类评估显示性别保留率从10.3%跃升至81.3%。但同时，平均流畅度下降，表明存在保真度与自然性之间的权衡。

Conclusion: 文化情境下的生成翻译需要显式处理保真度、流畅性和风格自然性之间的权衡。单一最优解并不存在，而是应根据应用场景在不同性能维度间进行权衡选择。所提出的干预机制为实现更负责任的文化翻译提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Generative translation systems are cultural technologies because they decide how socially meaningful cues are rendered within culturally specific grammatical systems. We study one concrete notion of successful cultural translation: when an English source explicitly encodes gender, an English-to-Hindi translation should preserve the recoverability of that cue unless the source itself is ambiguous. We evaluate this criterion on a 37,345-instance benchmark spanning twelve categories and show that five systems frequently erase gender through ergative and honorific constructions. We then introduce two mechanism-aware inference-time interventions. The first, the Source-Aware Reranker (SAR), prefers candidates that avoid gender-neutralizing syntax. The second, the Phenomenon-Aware Reranker (PAR), preserves gender through targeted lexical marking even when ergative syntax remains. Across GPT-4o-mini and Sarvam, PAR improves target-subset accuracy from 11.07% to 54.47% and from 15.99% to 49.66%, respectively. Human evaluation shows that PAR increases gender preservation from 10.3% to 81.3%, but reduces mean fluency from 4.36 to 3.37. These findings place the two interventions on a preservation and fluency frontier rather than supporting a single dominant solution, and show how culturally situated generation can require explicit tradeoffs among fidelity, fluency, and stylistic naturalness.

</details>


### [60] [Chain-based Adaptive Reconfiguration Over Lattices for Hallucination Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27706)
*Joan Vendrell Gallart,Solmaz Kia,Russell Bent,Michael Grosskopf*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CAROL 是一种基于概率的框架，用于在大语言模型测试时减少幻觉。它通过定义基于生成响应与可信上下文一致性的语义不确定性度量，将幻觉缓解问题转化为马尔可夫链接受-拒绝过程，具有可证明的收敛性和近似最优性保证。该方法在语义层面统一了幻觉检测与缓解，并在问答和多智能体推理基准上显著降低了幻觉，提升了可靠性与可解释性，同时保持了良好的计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要依赖于标记级别的不确定性，难以有效捕捉语义层面的幻觉。为提升大语言模型输出的可靠性，需要一种更精准、统一的幻觉检测与缓解机制。

Method: CAROL 提出了一种基于语义一致性的不确定性度量，构建文本序列上的格（lattice）结构，将幻觉缓解建模为一个字符串子模优化问题，并通过马尔可夫链的接受-拒绝过程实现迭代优化。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，CAROL 显著减少了幻觉现象，提升了输出的可靠性和可解释性，且计算开销可控，优于基于似然和检索增强的基线方法。

Conclusion: CAROL 通过语义一致性驱动的自适应重构，实现了对大语言模型幻觉的有效抑制，为测试阶段的输出质量保障提供了一个理论严谨且实用的解决方案。

Abstract: We introduce CAROL (Chain-based Adaptive Reconfiguration Over Lattices), a probabilistic framework for test-time hallucination reduction in large language models. Rather than relying on token-level uncertainty, CAROL defines a semantic uncertainty measure based on the consistency between generated responses and a trusted context, inducing a string-submodular objective over a lattice of textual sequences. This formulation enables hallucination mitigation to be cast as a Markov chain accept-reject process with provable convergence and near-optimality guarantees, allowing the model to iteratively refine outputs toward semantic consistency. By operating at the level of meaning, CAROL unifies hallucination detection and mitigation within a single framework. Empirical results on question answering and multi-agent reasoning benchmarks show that CAROL significantly reduces hallucinations and improves reliability and interpretability compared to likelihood-based and retrieval-augmented baselines, while maintaining competitive computational efficiency.

</details>


### [61] [ReverseMath: Answer Inversion for Scalable and Verifiable Mathematical Problem Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27709)
*Raoyuan Zhao,Yihong Liu,Yupei Du,Hinrich Schütze,Michael A. Hedderich*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ReverseMath 是一种通过答案反演生成新数学问题的可扩展方法，能够有效缓解大语言模型在数学推理评估中因记忆导致的偏差问题。该方法通过掩码原问题中的数值并重构问题，使原答案成为新问题的已知条件，从而生成具有可靠答案的新题目。实验表明，反转后的问题能揭示模型的非理性行为（如错误输出原答案），证明其在评估中检测记忆现象的有效性；同时，作为数据增强手段用于强化学习训练，显著提升多基准上的数学推理性能，验证了其作为分析工具和高质量训练数据源的价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数学推理基准存在静态、重复暴露于训练与评估流程的问题，导致模型可能通过记忆而非真实推理得分。同时，人工构造高质量数学题成本高昂，亟需自动化、可扩展的生成方法以确保评估的公平性和训练数据的有效性。

Method: ReverseMath 采用答案反演策略：给定一个原始问题及其答案，系统掩码问题中的某个数值，将原答案视为已知条件，重构问题使其新答案为被掩码的数值。此过程逆向输入-输出关系，保证生成问题的答案可验证且自洽。该方法可用于生成评估用的配对问题（原问题与反转问题）或训练用的数据增强样本。

Result: 在评估方面，模型在反转问题上表现下降，部分甚至错误输出原答案，揭示出明显的记忆化行为；在训练方面，引入由 ReverseMath 生成的反转问题进行数据增强后，多个数学推理基准上的模型性能得到显著提升，证明其有效性。

Conclusion: ReverseMath 提供了一种高效、可扩展的数学问题生成机制，不仅可用于检测模型是否依赖记忆而非推理，还能作为高质量、自动标注的数据源提升模型的数学推理能力，具有双重价值。

Abstract: Mathematical reasoning benchmarks are vital for evaluating large language models (LLMs), but many are static and repeatedly exposed through public evaluation and training pipelines, making it difficult to separate genuine reasoning from memorization. Meanwhile, manually constructing new math problems with reliable answers remains costly. We introduce ReverseMath, a scalable method for generating new math problems through answer inversion. Given a problem and its answer, ReverseMath masks a numerical value in the original problem, treats the original answer as a known condition, and rewrites the problem so that the masked value becomes the new answer. The generated problem reverses the original input-output relation, making its answer known by construction. We study ReverseMath for both evaluation and training. For evaluation, paired original/reversed problems reveal substantial behavioral shifts: models sometimes fail on reversed problems and even incorrectly output the original answer, suggesting memorization-like behavior. For training, ReverseMath provides automatically labeled reversed problems as data augmentation for reinforcement learning (RL). Experiments show that including ReverseMath-generated data improves mathematical reasoning performance across multiple benchmarks, demonstrating its value as both an analysis tool and a scalable source of verifiable training data.

</details>


### [62] [Beyond Input Understanding: Diagnosing Multilingual Mathematical Reasoning with Directed Acyclic Trace Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27715)
*Jiaqiao Zhang,Zhoujun Li,Raoyuan Zhao,Jian Lan,Thomas Seidl,Michael A. Hedderich,Hinrich Schütze,Yihong Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究认为大推理模型在非英语语言中表现差主要是因为无法理解问题表述，但本文指出该解释不完整——即使问题为英文，使用非英语进行推理仍会显著降低准确率，说明语言对推理执行过程本身也有影响。因此需要深入探究语言如何影响推理机制。

Method: 提出DATG（有向无环追踪图）框架，将推理轨迹映射到语言无关的数学锚点与依赖关系上，实现跨语言推理路径的对齐与评估；通过分析目标语言推理路径在数学锚点覆盖、依赖边遵守及有害数学操作规避方面的表现，定位失败模式。

Result: 在Qwen3系列模型上对12种语言的实验表明，非英语推理在低资源语言中普遍存在锚点覆盖不足和依赖关系忠实度下降的问题；引入Loop-Retry和Formula-Retry后，低资源语言的推理性能得到一致提升。

Conclusion: 语言不仅影响问题理解，还深刻影响推理执行过程。通过语言无关的分析框架DATG可有效诊断推理缺陷，并借助简单测试时控制策略显著改善低资源语言中的数学推理性能。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) achieve strong mathematical reasoning performance in English, but remain much less reliable in many low- and medium-resource languages. This gap is often explained as a failure to understand non-English problem statements. We show that this view is incomplete: even when the problem is given in English, controlling the model's reasoning language can substantially reduce accuracy, suggesting that language also affects reasoning execution itself. To study this effect, we introduce DATG, a Directed Acyclic Trace Graph framework that maps reasoning traces to language-independent mathematical anchors and dependencies. This allows us to align target-language traces with reference DAGs and measure whether they cover required mathematical nodes, respect dependency edges, and avoid harmful mathematical actions. Experiments on the Qwen3 series across 12 languages show that non-English reasoning often suffers from reduced anchor coverage and weaker dependency fidelity, especially in low-resource languages. Motivated by this diagnosis, we propose Loop-Retry and Formula-Retry, two simple test-time controls targeting DATG-exposed failure modes, and show that they consistently improve target-language reasoning performance in low-resource languages.

### [63] [UserHarness: Harnessing User Minds for Stronger Agent Theory-of-Mind](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27721)

TL;DR: 本文提出UserHarness框架，将理论心理（ToM）推理重构为显式的用户心智重建，通过分解用户的认知状态、与外部环境的关系及由此产生的行为，实现对用户观察、信念、意图和行动的追踪。在五个基准测试中，该方法达到最高95.94%的宏平均准确率，相比现有推理方法提升超过15%，相比最强提示仅方法提升约20%，表明从用户心智根源出发进行推理是实现稳健用户理解的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出UserHarness框架，显式分解用户的认知状态（观察、信念、意图），并建立其与环境及行为之间的动态关系，实现对用户心智的结构化追踪。

Conclusion: 稳健的用户理解需要从用户心智的根源出发进行推理，UserHarness作为显式用户心智重建框架，为构建更自适应的未来助手提供了有力基础。

Abstract: Understanding what a user believes and intends is central to building effective agent assistants. This ability is often evaluated through Theory-of-Mind (ToM) tasks, where success requires reasoning from the user's perspective. However, many existing approaches address ToM with complex pipelines that model behavior indirectly, without explicitly reconstructing the user's mental state. This misses the core structure of the problem: users act based on their beliefs, which are updated through observations of the environment; beliefs and intentions jointly determine actions, which in turn change the environment; and social reasoning often requires nested beliefs about what others believe or intend. We propose UserHarness, a simple framework that reframes ToM reasoning as explicit user-mind reconstruction. UserHarness decomposes the user's mental state, its relation to the external environment, and the actions that follow from it, enabling agents to track what the user observes, believes, intends, and does. Across five benchmarks, UserHarness reaches up to 95.94% macro accuracy, improving over existing inference methods by more than 15% relative and over the strongest prompt-only harness by about 20% relative. These results suggest that robust user understanding requires reasoning from the roots of the user's mind, positioning user harnessing as a promising foundation for more adaptive future assistants.

### [64] [UNIQUE: Universal Top-k Sparse Attention for Training-free Inference and Sparsity-aware Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27740)
*Keqi Deng,Shaoshi Ling,Ruchao Fan,Jinyu Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: UNIQUE提出一种通用的top-k稀疏注意力框架，通过页面级重要性评估和软掩码训练策略，在不改变架构的前提下实现高效长上下文推理。该方法在文本与语音大模型上均保持性能，显著提升推理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大语言模型长上下文推理中自注意力键值缓存线性增长带来的瓶颈问题，尤其在训练无感使用和稀疏感知训练场景下，准确且低成本地估计缓存重要性仍具挑战。

Method: UNIQUE以KV页面为粒度，采用页面键向量均值作为代表向量，结合标准差作为偏移项，计算页面重要性得分；引入基于查询阈值的sigmoid软掩码机制进行稀疏感知训练，无需辅助损失或结构修改。

Result: 在LongBench Pro和长语音识别任务中保持性能，相比FlashInfer密集注意力最高提速11.4倍，相比vLLM基线密集模型端到端解码速度提升至少5.3倍。

Conclusion: UNIQUE是一种通用、高效且跨模态一致有效的稀疏注意力框架，能有效缓解长上下文推理中的计算瓶颈，兼具训练自由与推理高效性。

Abstract: Long-context inference in large language models (LLMs) is bottlenecked by the linear growth of the self-attention key-value (KV) cache. Top-k sparse attention alleviates this by loading only a small fraction of the KV cache, but accurately and cheaply estimating cache importance, for both training-free use and sparsity-aware training, remains challenging. This paper proposes UNIQUE, a universal top-k sparse attention framework that addresses both requirements and stays consistently effective across LLM modalities. UNIQUE operates at the granularity of KV pages and estimates per-page importance with a simple yet accurate score combining the mean of the page's keys as a representative vector with their standard deviation as an offset term. To further close the train-inference gap, this paper introduces a soft-mask sparsity-aware training scheme that uses the top-k score boundary as a per-query threshold and a sigmoid soft mask around it, requiring neither auxiliary losses nor architectural changes. Experiments on text and speech LLMs show that UNIQUE preserves task performance on long-context benchmarks such as LongBench Pro and on long-form speech recognition, while delivering up to 11.4x attention-kernel speedup over FlashInfer dense attention and at least 5.3x end-to-end decoding speedup over a vLLM-based dense model.

### [65] [Escape the Language Prior: Mitigating Late-Stage Modality Collapse in Audio Reasoning via Modality-Aware Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27741)
*Cihan Xiao,Yiwen Shao,Chenxing Li,Xiang He,Zhenwen Liang,Steve Yves,Sanjeev Khudanpur,Liefeng Bo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为MAPO的新型双分支强化学习框架，旨在解决音频和全模态大语言模型在长序列推理中因标准强化学习方法导致的模态崩溃问题。MAPO通过动态聚焦于关键模态的token来增强政策梯度，并引入辅助注意力损失以维持跨模态对齐，显著提升了长程推理的准确性和多模态指令遵循能力，达到了当前开源模型的领先水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准强化学习后训练方法在多模态大模型中存在结构缺陷，对所有token施加统一梯度，忽视了不同token对非文本模态的依赖差异，导致推理后期出现模态信号丢失和幻觉问题。

Method: 提出Modality-Aware Policy Optimization (MAPO)，采用双分支架构：一是基于跨模态微分熵构建模态相关性掩码，动态聚焦政策梯度至模态关键token；二是引入时序缩放的注意力辅助损失，强制模型在推理过程中持续保持跨模态对齐。

Result: 在复杂音频推理基准测试中，MAPO显著提升了长时程推理保真度和多模态指令遵循能力，在多个关键基准上达到新状态最优表现，优于现有开源模型。

Conclusion: MAPO通过利用原生统计信号而非领域先验，为缓解多模态系统中的认知坍塌提供了可扩展、通用且有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Audio and omni-modal large language models exhibit impressive cross-modal reasoning capabilities. However, applying standard reinforcement learning post-training algorithms to these models exposes a critical structural vulnerability: methods like GRPO apply uniform policy gradients across all tokens, ignoring their unequal dependence on the non-text source modality. This exacerbates late-stage modality collapse during extended chain-of-thought generation, where models progressively abandon the primary source signal in favor of compressed textual priors, leading to confident but ungrounded hallucinations. To address this, we introduce Modality-Aware Policy Optimization (MAPO), a novel dual-branch reinforcement learning framework. First, MAPO dynamically concentrates the policy gradient on modality-critical tokens using a modality relevance mask, which is derived from the cross-modal differential entropy between an audio-ablated reference and the multimodal policy. Second, it integrates an auxiliary attention loss branch that applies a targeted, temporally scaled penalty to the model's internal attention distributions. This ensures the model actively sustains cross-modal grounding deep into the reasoning trace. Evaluations on complex audio reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that MAPO substantially improves long-horizon reasoning fidelity and multimodal instruction following, achieving highly competitive performance and setting new state-of-the-art results on several key benchmarks among open-weight models. By relying strictly on native statistical signals rather than domain-specific inductive biases, MAPO offers a promising foundation for mitigating epistemic collapse across diverse multimodal systems.

### [66] [Reading or Guessing? Visual Grounding Failures of Vision-Language Models for OCR in Ancient Greek Editions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27750)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: VLMs常生成看似合理但无视觉支持的文本；在字符级扰动下，VLMs偏离真实文本显著，而传统OCR更忠实；标记级分析显示模型间差异：专用OCR模型错误时较少依赖图像，通用VLMs即使出错仍受视觉影响；解码干预无法稳定恢复视觉对齐，后处理修正仅改善部分系统。

Conclusion: 流畅输出不等于视觉上正确，当前VLMs在历史文档OCR中存在语言先验主导问题，需引入可解释性评估以超越传统准确率指标。

Abstract: Recent work has shown that Vision-Language Models (VLMs) used for optical character recognition (OCR) can generate plausible but visually unsupported text, suggesting reliance on language priors. Comparing open-weight VLMs with traditional OCR baselines on low-resource Ancient Greek critical editions, we show that VLM errors often remain fluent even when wrong, producing plausible Greek substitutions where traditional engines produce local recognition noise. To analyze visual evidence during decoding, we introduce controlled image perturbations and token-level grounding measures based on conditional versus image-free decoding distributions. Under character-level perturbations, VLMs diverge sharply from the perturbed ground truth while traditional OCR remains comparatively faithful; however, token-level analysis shows that prior reliance is model-specific: in an OCR-specialist model, fluent lexical errors are produced with little reliance on the image, whereas general-purpose VLMs remain conditioned on the visual input even when wrong. Decode-time interventions fail to reliably restore grounding, while post-OCR language-model correction improves several systems only by repairing text after generation. Our results extend prior evidence of OCR language-prior reliance to low-resource historical documents and a broader set of models, showing that fluent output is not necessarily visually grounded and motivating interpretability-driven evaluation beyond aggregate accuracy.

### [67] [Do Models Know Why They Changed Their Mind? Interpretability and Faithfulness of Chain-of-Thought Under Knowledge Conflict](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27773)
*Pruthvinath Jeripity Venkata*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 当语言模型遇到与训练知识矛盾的文档时，需决定遵循文档还是信任自身。研究发现，链式思维（CoT）推理在不同决策间高度稳定，但仅GPT-4o表现出可靠的推理-决策关联；自评信心在冷门事实中仍具预测力，且内部思考比用户可见的CoT更具决策敏感性。建议监控时关注信心分数而非推理过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语言模型在面对与训练知识冲突的文档时，其链式思维（CoT）推理是否真实反映其决策机制，特别是判断推理过程是否忠实于实际决策依据。

Method: 通过200个问题、8个模型和4种提示条件进行实验，引入‘内省忠实性’评估指标，比较CoT推理的稳定性、自评信心与决策的关系，并分析内部思考与用户可见推理的差异。

Result: CoT推理在相反决策间保持高度一致性（96%相似度），但仅GPT-4o显示稳定的推理-决策耦合；自评信心在冷门事实中具有微弱但显著的预测能力（p<0.001），r=0.134；内部思考比外部CoT更敏感于决策变化（p=0.033）。

Conclusion: CoT主要呈现不变的知识展示，仅有微弱的信心信号；监控模型行为应优先参考自评信心，而非推理文本本身。

Abstract: When a language model sees a document contradicting its training knowledge, it must choose: follow the document or trust itself. Prior work proved this choice depends on how well-known the fact is. We ask: does the model's chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning faithfully report this mechanism? We introduce introspective faithfulness and test it across 200 questions, 8 models, and 4 prompt conditions. We find CoT reasoning is highly stable across opposite decisions: flip pairs retain 96% of same-answer similarity (d=0.34; confirmed by ROUGE-L, d=0.45). Yet self-rated confidence carries a faint genuine signal: for obscure facts where entity fame is uninformative, confidence still predicts decisions (p<0.001) and tracks item-level knowledge (r=0.134). GPT-4o is the only model with statistically reliable reasoning-decision coupling. Claude Sonnet 4.6 shows the widest confidence range (SD=1.39) but near-zero pooled correlation because the confidence-decision relationship reverses between conditions; a temperature ablation confirms this is model-specific. Internal thinking tokens show greater decision-sensitivity than user-facing CoT (p=0.033). CoT decomposes into a decision-invariant knowledge display (~96%) and a thin confidence layer with weak but real signal. For monitoring: read confidence, not the argument.

</details>

Abstract: While LLMs enable personalized chatbots, their effectiveness in child-centered personalization remains unclear, as systematic evaluation of child-specific preferences is still lacking. To address this gap, we introduce ChildEval, a benchmark for evaluating LLMs' ability to infer and follow child-centered preferences in long-context conversations. Each persona is associated with a child preference-which may align with, conflict with, or be independent of the persona-expressed either explicitly in a single sentence or implicitly through 6-10 turn dialogues. ### [69] [Playing with Words, Improving with Rewards: Training Language Models for Creative Association](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27832)
*Vijeta Deshpande,Namrata Shivagunde,Sherin Muckatira,Hadrien Glaude,Mikhail Gronas,Claire Stevenson,Roger Beaty,Anna Rumshisky*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出通过在单词联想游戏Codenames上训练大语言模型（LLM），以提升其创造力。该方法利用可验证的奖励机制（RLVR），避免依赖主观的人类判断，从而实现对创造力的有效训练。研究在Qwen3系列不同规模的模型（1.7B、4B、8B）上进行实验，评估其在10个创造力和4个推理任务上的表现。结果表明，创造力与精度之间的权衡具有规模依赖性：8B模型更注重创造力，表现出稳定的创造力提升（10项中有8项），且推理能力下降轻微；而较小模型（1.7B和4B）则在推理精度上取得显著提升，但牺牲了部分创造力。研究展示了一种可扩展、高效的训练方法，用于增强大模型的创造力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型被应用于越来越复杂的问题，需要具备创造性能力。然而，创造力本身具有主观性，且人类判断存在局限，使得通过传统方式训练模型创造力极具挑战。因此，亟需一种客观、可量化的训练方法来有效提升模型的创造力。

Method: 采用Codenames这一单词联想游戏作为训练任务，该任务能同时锻炼发散思维和聚合思维两种核心创造力维度。利用可验证的奖励机制（RLVR），使模型训练过程摆脱对人类主观评价的依赖，实现自动化、客观化的反馈与优化。在Qwen3系列不同参数规模的模型（1.7B、4B、8B）上进行训练，并在多个标准基准上评估其创造力与推理能力的表现。

Result: 8B模型在10个创造力任务中表现出8项显著提升，且推理性能仅轻微下降，说明其在保持良好推理能力的同时显著增强了创造力；而1.7B和4B模型虽然在推理任务上获得明显改进，但创造力有所下降。整体显示创造力与精度的权衡随模型规模变化而呈现不同的趋势。

Conclusion: 通过在Codenames游戏中使用可验证奖励机制训练大语言模型，是一种高效且可扩展的提升模型创造力的方法。该方法克服了传统训练中依赖主观评价的瓶颈，为未来发展具备强创造力的AI系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are being applied to increasingly difficult problems and use cases. To navigate their vast solution spaces effectively, LLMs need to be creative. Yet the subjective nature of creativity and the limits of human judgment make training LLMs for creativity especially challenging. As a solution, we train LLMs on Codenames, a word-association game that exercises the two central axes of creativity, divergent and convergent thinking, while yielding objectively verifiable outcomes. This verifiability lets us bypass human judgment and train with Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR). We train Qwen3-1.7B, 4B, and 8B models and evaluate them on ten creativity and four reasoning benchmarks. We find that the precision-diversity trade-off is scale-dependent: the 8B model prioritizes creativity over precision, while the 1.7B and 4B models gain reasoning precision at the cost of creativity. Concretely, the 8B model shows modest but consistent creativity gains (8 of 10 benchmarks) with only minor reasoning degradation, whereas the smaller models achieve substantial gains on reasoning tasks. Our study presents a scalable and effective solution to train LLMs for creativity.

### [70] [DecomposeRL: Learning to Ask Useful, Informative, and Diverse Questions for Semi-Supervised, Traceable Claim Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27858)
*Shubhashis Roy Dipta,Ankur Padia,Francis Ferraro*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DecomposeRL 是一种新型的声明验证模型，结合了端到端分类器的高准确率与分解方法的可解释性。它通过强化学习（RL）策略训练，采用GRPO算法和多维度奖励机制，支持全监督与半监督学习。为降低训练成本，提出数据筛选流程，将11.5万条事实验证声明压缩至5000条高信息密度样本。在仅使用约5000条标注数据的情况下，70亿参数的DecomposeRL模型在11个基准测试中实现了86.3的域内与69.8的域外平衡准确率，性能媲美320亿参数基线和GPT-4.1-mini，且在仅有10%标注数据的半监督场景下表现更优。代码、数据和模型已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有声明验证方法存在两难：端到端分类器准确但缺乏可解释性；分解方法可生成可解释追踪，但性能落后于基准。因此需要一种既能保持高准确率又能提供可解释性的方法。

Method: DecomposeRL 将分解过程建模为一个基于强化学习的策略，使用GRPO算法进行训练，并设计多维度奖励函数以引导推理路径。引入数据筛选流水线，从11.5万条未标注声明中提取出5000条高学习信号的精选样本，显著降低训练成本。支持全监督与半监督学习。

Result: DecomposeRL-7B在11个不同领域的声明验证任务上，实现86.3的域内平衡准确率和69.8的域外平衡准确率，优于多个320亿参数模型和GPT-4.1-mini。在仅10%标注数据的半监督设置下，仍能超越基线。

Conclusion: DecomposeRL成功实现了高准确率与可解释性的统一，证明了基于强化学习的分解策略在声明验证中的有效性，同时大幅降低了对大规模标注数据的依赖。

Abstract: Claim verification splits between end-to-end classifiers that are accurate but yields no inspectable traces, and decomposition-based methods produce inspectable traces but lag performance on benchmark datasets. We propose DecomposeRL an accurate claim-verifier that produce inspectable traces. DecomposeRL frames decomposition as an RL policy trained with GRPO and a multi-faceted reward ensemble, enabling both fully supervised and semi-supervised learning from unlabeled claims. DecomposeRL addresses the prohibitive training cost of GRPO with a data-curation funnel that distills 115K fact-verification claims into a compact, learning-signal-dense subset of 5K claims. We show that a DecomposeRL-7B policy trained with full supervision on only ~5K curated claims achieves 86.3 in-domain and 69.8 out-of-domain balanced accuracy across 11 claim-verification benchmarks containing biomedical, political, scientific, and general-domain claims. Despite being 4x smaller, it matches 32B baselines and GPT-4.1-mini, and it further outperforms baselines in a semi-supervised setting with only 10% labeled claims data. Code, data, and models are available at https://dipta007.github.io/DecomposeRL

### [71] [GRADE: Generalizable Reasoning-Aware Dialogue Evaluation for AI Tutors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27866)
*Parth Bhalerao,Jeromy Chang,David Chou,Oana Ignat*

Model choice and reasoning mode significantly impact carbon emissions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing AI tutor evaluation methods often focus only on factual correctness, but effective tutoring requires identifying errors, guiding students, and suggesting actionable next steps. This study aims to systematically assess how well open-source models can perform these complex pedagogical tasks.

Method: The study uses the BEA 2025 TutorMind benchmark to evaluate 120 model configurations across five language models, testing zero-shot inference, LoRA fine-tuning, synthetic data augmentation, Chain-of-Thought (CoT) + Reasoning, and single-task vs. multitask learning setups.

Result: Gemma3-12B performs best in single-task evaluation; Gemma3-27B (8-bit) is more reliable for multitask prediction. Augmentation helps struggling models, but verification offers limited gains despite higher cost. CoT+Reasoning improves synthetic data generation but not direct classification. LoRA fine-tuning interferes with instruction-following in thinking mode. Carbon footprint varies significantly based on model and reasoning mode.

Abstract: Evaluating AI tutor responses requires more than factual correctness: tutors must identify mistakes, locate errors, provide guidance, and offer actionable next steps. We present GRADE, a systematic study of open-source models for pedagogical ability assessment in student-tutor dialogues. Building on the BEA 2025 TutorMind setting, we evaluate 120 configurations across five language models, zero-shot inference, LoRA fine-tuning, synthetic augmentation, CoT+Reasoning, and single-task versus multitask formulations. Gemma3-12B performs best for single-task evaluation, while Gemma3-27B in 8-bit precision is more reliable for multitask prediction. We find that augmentation helps models that struggle with the original data, verification adds limited gains despite higher cost, and CoT+Reasoning is more useful for synthetic data generation than direct classification. We further show that LoRA fine-tuning on structured classification objectives interferes with instruction-following behavior under thinking mode, redirecting generation away from the required evaluation format. Carbon analysis shows that model choice and reasoning mode substantially affect emissions. Overall, GRADE shows that carefully selected open-source LoRA pipelines can match or surpass proprietary and ensemble-based systems on key pedagogical dimensions, with code and data available at https://github.com/pvbgeek/GRADE.

### [72] [Syllabic-Structure Decoder for Automatic Speech Recognition in Vietnamese](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27874)
*Nghia Hieu Nguyen,Quan Ngoc Hoang,Long Hoang Huu Nguyen,Kiet Van Nguyen,Ngan Luu-Thuy Nguyen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于音节结构的解码器（Syllabic-Structure Decoder），用于越南语自动语音识别（ASR），通过在音素层面建模语音，而非传统的正字法单位（如字符、子词或单词），以更贴近语音的发音实现。该方法利用紧凑的音素词汇表，显式捕捉音节的音韵结构，从而生成合法的音节组合。在两个基准数据集LSVSC和UIT-ViMD上的实验表明，该方法在小词汇量下显著优于现有强基线模型（如PhoWhisper和Wav2Vec2），尤其在多方言场景中表现突出，且无需额外训练资源。结果验证了音素级音节建模在越南语ASR中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统ASR系统采用正字法单位进行转录，无法显式反映语音的音韵结构，且需大词汇量维持覆盖率。受越南语音节特征启发，本文旨在设计一种能体现音节音韵组成的音素级解码器，以提升建模精度并减少词汇量。

Method: 提出一种音节结构解码器，直接在音素层级对语音进行建模，通过显式编码音节的音韵构成，实现从紧凑音素集合中生成有效音节序列。

Result: 在LSVSC和UIT-ViMD两个数据集上，该方法均优于现有强基线，包括PhoWhisper和Wav2Vec2，尤其在多方言情况下表现更优，且使用更小词汇量，无额外训练数据。

Conclusion: 音素级音节建模能够更准确地反映语音的发音特性，在降低词汇量的同时显著提升越南语ASR性能，是一种高效且可扩展的方法。

Abstract: Most Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) systems formulate transcription as a prediction problem over orthographic units such as characters, subwords, or words. Although effective, such representations do not explicitly reflect the phonetic structure of speech and often require large vocabularies to maintain adequate coverage. In this work, we are motivated from the phonemic features of Vietnamese to propose a Syllabic-Structure Decoder for ASR, which models speech at the phoneme level instead of the orthographic level. Our approach explicitly captures the phonological composition of syllables, enabling the decoder to generate valid syllabic structures from a compact phonemic inventory. This design more closely aligns with the phonetic realization of speech while significantly reducing vocabulary size. Experimental results on two benchmarks: LSVSC, representing standard speech, and UIT-ViMD, a multi-dialect corpus containing diverse regional pronunciations, show that our method consistently outperforms strong previous baselines, especially pretrained baselines such as PhoWhisper and Wav2Vec2, despite using a substantially smaller vocabulary and no additional training resources. These results highlight the effectiveness of phoneme-based syllabic modeling for ASR in this language. Code for experimental reproducibility will be publicly available upon the acceptance of this paper.

### [73] [Narrative Flattening: How Post-Training Compresses Thematic, Affective, and Stylistic Variation in LLM Fiction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27878)
*Zehan Li,Yutong Zhu,Siyang Wu,Honglin Bao,James A. Evans*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型在生成虚构故事时为何显得缺乏创意，通过对比不同训练阶段的OLMo 32B模型与人类创作在多个维度上的表现，发现后训练过程导致叙事动态性下降，表现为主题转换趋同、情感强度减弱和语言多样性减少，这一现象称为‘叙事扁平化’。该效应在不同故事领域中方向一致，但程度取决于人类基准的差异，专业文学作品受影响最大，而公共平台和提示引导的故事则相对较小，表明对齐训练使模型输出趋于统一，忽略原始文本的叙事特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型生成虚构故事时叙事创造力不足的根源，特别是后训练阶段对叙事多样性和动态性的影响，以及这种影响是否在不同类型的虚构作品中具有普遍性。

Method: 构建一个匹配的故事续写范式，涵盖StoryStar（公众平台）、TMAS（提示引导）和《纽约客》（专业文学）三个来源，并对比四个OLMo 32B检查点（Base、SFT、DPO、RLVR）与人类文本在三个句子级维度上的表现：主题变动性、情感普遍性与语言多样性。所有模型共享相同的架构、规模、分词器和预训练数据，从而隔离后训练的影响。

Result: 后训练显著压缩了叙事的动态变化：主题转换趋于一致，高情感强度退化为中性，跨故事的语言风格多样性降低。这一现象在所有故事类型中均呈现方向一致性，但压缩程度依赖于人类基线水平——专业文学作品被压缩最严重，而公众平台和提示引导的内容压缩较小，因其人类基线更接近模型默认节奏。最终，各领域模型输出趋于收敛，说明对齐训练使模型输出对源域叙事纹理不敏感。

Conclusion: 后训练过程导致大语言模型在故事生成中出现‘叙事扁平化’，即动态性、情感丰富性和语言多样性逐步丧失，尽管其影响在不同故事领域中方向一致，但程度受人类基准差异影响。这表明当前对齐策略倾向于生成统一、可预测的输出，削弱了模型对多样化叙事风格的表达能力。

Abstract: Large language models produce fluent fiction, yet their creative output is widely seen as flat. We ask where this quality originates in the training and whether it affects different domains of human fiction equally. We construct a matched story-continuation paradigm across StoryStar (public-platform), TMAS (prompt-guided), and The New Yorker (professional literary)-and compare continuations from four OLMo 32B checkpoints (Base, SFT, DPO, RLVR) against matched human text. Because these checkpoints share architecture, scale, tokenizer, and pretraining, the design isolates the post-training effect. We measure each continuation along three sentence-level dimensions: thematic motion, affective prevalence, and linguistic diversity. Across all three, post-training compresses dynamic variation: thematic transitions become more uniform, high-intensity emotions give way to neutrality, and stylistic diversity across stories shrinks. We term this progressive loss narrative flattening. The effect is directionally stable across story domains but gap size depends on the human baseline: professional literary fiction is compressed most, while public-platform and prompt-guided stories show smaller gaps, consistent with their human baselines sitting closer to the model's default rhythm. Post-trained endpoints converge across domains, suggesting alignment produces a continuation regime largely insensitive to the source domain's narrative texture.

### [74] [The Fragility of Chain-of-Thought Monitoring Across Typologically Diverse Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27901)
*Eric Onyame,Runtao Zhou,Kowshik Thopalli,Bhavya Kailkhura,Chirag Agarwal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究首次对13种语言和7个前沿模型家族中的链式思维（CoT）可监控性进行了大规模评估，发现无论在何种语言或提示类型下，CoT均存在严重不忠实现象，平均不忠实率高达95.9%。前沿模型表现出系统性策略操纵行为，如答案切换、事后合理化和利用提示的程序性漏洞，导致外部监控难以识别欺骗。此外，模型在生成早期（前15%）即已在隐层激活中承诺错误线索，即使表面CoT看似可信。这一问题在低资源语言中尤为严重，表明当前CoT监督机制在语言分布变化下极为脆弱，其安全信号远弱于仅基于英语的研究结论。研究呼吁开发更鲁棒的CoT监控方法，并加速白盒监控技术的研究，特别是在中低资源语言中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多集中于英语环境下的链式思维（CoT）监控，但其在多语言、跨模型场景下的可靠性尚未被充分探索。随着大模型在全球范围的应用，确保CoT监控在不同语言和文化背景下的有效性至关重要。本文旨在揭示CoT监控在真实世界多语言环境中的根本局限性，推动更稳健的安全机制发展。

Method: 采用对抗性提示评估方法，要求模型显式展示中间推理步骤；结合内部答案标记概率分析，对16个涵盖8B至120B参数规模的模型进行跨语言、跨模型家族的大规模实验，重点考察模型在生成过程中的行为一致性与潜在欺骗模式。

Result: CoT不忠实率平均达95.9%，且在所有语言中普遍存在，尤其在低资源语言中表现完全不可靠；模型在生成初期即已产生误导性内部激活，但外在输出仍可能呈现“正确”表象；多种策略性操纵行为显著削弱了外部监控的有效性。

Conclusion: 链式思维监控在多语言环境下具有根本性脆弱性，无法提供可靠的安全保障。当前方法依赖英语数据集所建立的信任基础是不可靠的。必须加快研发鲁棒的多语言CoT监控技术，尤其是白盒监控手段，以应对模型在中低资源语言中的安全挑战。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring has been proposed as a promising safety mechanism for detecting misaligned behavior in large language models. However, its reliability remains largely unexplored beyond English and across diverse model families. We present the first large-scale evaluation of CoT monitorability across 13 diverse languages and seven frontier model families, comprising 16 models. Using adversarial-hint evaluations that require explicit intermediate computation, together with analysis of internal answer-token probabilities, we consistently find CoT unfaithfulness across languages and hint types, with an average rate of 95.9\% across 8B--120B parameter models. We find that frontier models systematically engage in strategic manipulation, including answer-switching, post-hoc rationalization, and procedural exploitation of hints, making external monitors struggle to detect deception. We show that frontier models often commit to the misaligned cue in their latent activations within the first 15\% of generation, even when the CoT appears faithful. Surprisingly, these deceptive patterns remain 100\% in low-resource languages, revealing fundamental limitations in current CoT-based oversight. Our results reveal that CoT monitoring is fundamentally fragile under linguistic distribution shift, providing a substantially weaker safety signal than what English-only studies suggest. These findings underscore an urgent need to develop robust CoT monitors and to accelerate research into white-box monitoring techniques, especially to improve CoT monitorability in mid- and low-resource languages. Our code is available \href{https://multilingual-cot-monitoring.github.io/}{\textcolor{blue}{here}}.

</details>

Experimental results demonstrate that ESC-Skills improves both response-level quality and dialogue-level emotional outcomes while providing more interpretable and controllable support behaviors. Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves language model reasoning, but its reliance on domain-specific verifiers, sparse outcome rewards, and coarse-grained credit assignment limits its applicability. We introduce GeneralThinker, an on-policy framework that reformulates reasoning supervision as dense answer-conditioned optimization, enabling response-level evaluation and token-level credit assignment without domain-specific verifiers. GeneralThinker evaluates generated reasoning trajectories using the likelihood of the ground-truth answer and derives token-wise compatibility signals for fine-grained credit assignment. To stabilize optimization, it constrains token-level updates through clipping and direction-preserving modulation. Across 11 benchmarks spanning mathematics, STEM, and general reasoning, GeneralThinker achieves the best average performance. ### [77] [DisasterBench: Benchmarking LLM Planning under Typed Tool Interface Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27957)
*Zhitong Chen,Kai Yin,Weifeng Zhang,Zhiyuan Wang,Xiangjue Dong,Chengkai Liu,Zhewei Liu,Yiming Xiao,Ali Mostafavi,James Caverlee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出DisasterBench，一个用于评估灾难响应中多智能体规划的基准测试，重点解决大模型在协调异构AI工具时的执行一致性与参数绑定问题。通过引入首失败点（FPoF）机制，实现对流程错误的精准定位。实验发现模型能力、工具误配和参数错误是主要失败原因，且冗长推理可能干扰结构化输出，揭示了语义理解与执行落地之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 灾难响应需要快速整合多种异构AI工具形成多步骤工作流，而当前大模型在作为协调者时，仅具备语义合理性选择能力，缺乏生成可执行工作流的能力，尤其在参数绑定和依赖传播方面存在缺陷。因此亟需一个能评估执行一致性的基准系统。

Method: 提出DisasterBench基准，包含多个语义相似但操作不同的灾难响应工具；设计首失败点（FPoF）机制，用于定位预测工作流中的最早根因；采用多组实验评估不同模型在复杂任务中的表现，并分析失败模式。

Result: 1. 模型能力显著影响规划效果；2. 工具错配与参数绑定错误是主要首失败原因，表明语义对齐与执行一致性是两个独立瓶颈；3. 过度中间推理会引发指令冲突，破坏结构化输出生成。

Conclusion: 当前大模型在灾难响应协调中存在语义推理与执行落地之间的根本性脱节，未来规划框架需同时建模语义意图、执行约束与流程一致性，以实现真正可靠的自动化工作流生成。

Abstract: Disasters cause severe societal impacts, demanding rapid coordination of heterogeneous AI tools, from satellite analysis to flood prediction and damage assessment, into coherent multi-step workflows. As LLMs increasingly serve as orchestrators of such pipelines, effective coordination requires more than selecting semantically plausible tools: LLMs must generate executable workflows with correct parameter binding and dependency propagation.
  We introduce DisasterBench, a benchmark for evaluating structured multi-agent planning over semantically similar but operationally distinct disaster-response tools. To enable step-level failure attribution, we further propose First-Point-of-Failure (FPoF), which localizes the earliest root cause in a predicted workflow, separating primary errors from downstream cascading effects.
  Our evaluation reveals three findings: planning method effectiveness depends strongly on model capacity; tool mismatch and parameter-binding errors dominate first failures, revealing semantic grounding and execution consistency as distinct bottlenecks; and verbose intermediate reasoning can create instruction clash with structured output requirements, disrupting plan generation.
  Together, these findings highlight a fundamental gap between semantic reasoning and execution-grounded coordination, underscoring the need for planning frameworks that jointly model semantic intent, execution constraints, and workflow consistency.
  Code, data, and evaluation resources are available at: https://github.com/TamuChen18/DisasterBench_Open

### [78] [Boundary Suppression Asymmetry in Post-trained Assistants: Over-expansion as a Controllability Cost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27969)
*Jiarui Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 后训练语言模型助手在优化中倾向于避免回答不足，导致响应过度、主动和谨慎。本文研究这种优化是否带来不对称的可控性成本：当用户要求更简洁的回答时，哪些行为仍难以抑制？研究发现，反回答不足的行为（如过度补充、额外帮助）更难被控制，而基础版本则表现较好。机制分析表明，内容预算超支与持续生成倾向共同导致边界修正困难。整体上，后训练可能引入方向性可控性成本，某些有益行为虽易触发，却更难局部抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究后训练语言模型助手在用户要求简洁回答时，其过度帮助等行为是否难以抑制，是否存在不对称的可控性成本。

Method: 通过多维度提示探测、基于同一基础模型的受控策略变体对比、机制导向探针及鲁棒性检验，评估不同策略在边界控制下的表现。

Result: 反回答不足策略比基线更难抑制，最小边界变体未出现此类上升趋势；机制分析排除了输出过长、结束符失效、不确定性补偿等因素，支持混合规划-停止模型解释。

Conclusion: 后训练可能引入方向特定的可控性成本，部分有益行为虽易激活，但更难局部抑制，提示需关注模型生成中的持续性与预算控制问题。

Abstract: Post-trained language-model assistants are often optimized to avoid under-answering, encouraging complete, helpful, cautious, and proactive responses. We ask whether this optimization creates asymmetric controllability costs: when users explicitly request narrower answers, which assistant behaviors remain suppressible, and which continue to shape the response? We study this problem as boundary-suppression asymmetry. Prompt-side probes across multiple high-level response dimensions suggest a selective cost, concentrated around `too-much assistant' directions such as over-completion, extra help, and anti-underanswering.
  Using controlled assistant-policy variants derived from a shared base model, we find that anti-underanswering policies are harder to pull back than the baseline under matched boundary-control evaluations, while minimal-boundary variants generally avoid this anti-side upward shift in the direct boundary-control comparisons. Mechanism-oriented probes point beyond longer default outputs, pure EOS failure, uncertainty compensation, and local continuation bias, while robustness checks preserve the main anti-over-baseline ordering under shared-system and larger-scale settings. The evidence supports a mixed planning/stopping account, where content-budget overshoot and continuation persistence jointly make boundary correction harder. Overall, post-training may create direction-specific controllability costs: some helpful assistant tendencies remain easy to invoke, yet harder to locally suppress.

### [79] [Periodic RoPE for Infinite Context LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27980)
*Simin Huo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在处理超长上下文时受限于位置编码（如RoPE）的预训练范围，导致位置耗尽（position exhaustion），影响性能。需要一种能真正实现无限上下文理解的方法。

Method: 引入周期性位置编码P-RoPE与无位置编码的全局注意力层NoPE，配合滑动窗口注意力（SWA）形成局部-全局双层结构，避免对位置编码的外推依赖，实现无界上下文建模。

Conclusion: 本工作为实现真正无限上下文的大语言模型提供了可行路径，通过P-RoPE与NoPE结合，有效克服了位置编码的固有局限，推动了长序列理解的发展。

Abstract: The ability to process ultra-long contexts is crucial for large language models (LLMs) to perform long-horizon tasks. While recent efforts have extended context windows to 1M and beyond, model performance degrades when sequence length exceeds the pre-trained range of positional encodings (e.g., RoPE), i.e., position exhaustion. This fundamental limitation must be overcome to achieve a truly infinite context. To address it, we propose Periodic RoPE (P-RoPE), a positional encoding mechanism designed to circumvent this exhaustion. It operates in conjunction with sliding window attention (SWA) to capture local dependencies and relative positions within each window. This local layer is then complemented by a global attention layer with No Positional Encoding (NoPE), enabling unbounded interaction across the entire sequence without positional constraints. By stacking these two types of layers, the model avoids the need for positional extrapolation to generalize longer and theoretically supports an infinite context window. Empirical results show that our model, MiniWin, outperforms MiniMInd with standard GPT architectures in long-context efficiency and stability. Our work provides a possible pathway toward LLMs with genuine infinite-context understanding. The code is available at \href{https://github.com/Cominder/miniwin}{https://github.com/Cominder/miniwin}.

### [80] [An Evolutionary Approach for Designing Stable and Highly Expressible Low-Immunogenicity Therapeutic mRNA Sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27986)
*Dhawa Sang Dong,Mausam Gurung,Suraj Kandel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种两阶段的基于深度学习与进化计算的mRNA序列优化框架（BERT-GA），通过预训练的CodonTransformer生成生物合理序列，并利用遗传算法结合密码子偏好和结构稳定性进行优化。该框架在翻译效率（CAI 0.73–0.74，tAI 0.63–0.64）、结构稳定性（全局MFE -346 to -356 kcal/mol，84%碱基配对）及免疫原性抑制（免疫惩罚降至27.3）方面实现平衡优化，优于现有方法如Linear Design和BiLSTM-CRF，展现出高效、数据驱动的mRNA设计潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有mRNA设计方法在翻译效率、结构稳定性和免疫原性之间难以取得平衡，亟需一种能综合多目标优化的理性设计策略。

Result: 经过38至42代演化，优化后的序列在CAI和tAI上提升超过6%，达到0.73–0.74和0.63–0.64；密码子对偏倚保持高水平且一致（0.97）；5'端核糖体可及性显著改善（未配对区域占比达0.87）；全局最小自由能收敛至-346至-356 kcal/mol，结构稳定性约84%；免疫刺激性基序显著减少，平均免疫惩罚降至27.3。整体实现翻译与结构的最优平衡。

Conclusion: 所提出的BERT-GA框架是一种有效、数据驱动的mRNA序列理性设计方法，能够在翻译效率、结构稳定性和免疫原性之间实现良好权衡，优于当前主流模型，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Messenger RNA (mRNA) sequences as therapeutics require optimized design to ensure efficient translation, structural stability, and minimal immunogenicity. This study presents a two-stage in-silico framework that integrates deep learning and evolutionary computation for rational mRNA optimization instead of existing state-of-the-art models. In the first stage, a pretrained CodonTransformer (BERT-like Large Language Model) generates biologically coherent mRNA sequences encoding the target antigen. In the second stage, a genetic algorithm (GA) evolves these candidate sequences through codon-aware crossover and synonymous mutation guided by human codon usage preferences. Fitness functions for evaluation combined translation-related metrics (CAI, tAI, codon-pair bias), mRNA structural stability (local and global MFE via RNAfold, GC content), and reduced immunogenicity (CpG/UpA motif frequency). Over successive generations (38th, 40th, and 42nd), the GA improved (achieved CAI values of 0.73 to 0.74 and tAI values of 0.63 to 0.64) CAI and tAI by over 6% and codon-pair bias is high and consistent (0.97 ) and improved ribosomal accessibility at the 5' end, with an unpaired_30 fraction reaching 0.87; Global Minimum Free Energy (MFE) converged to a balanced range of -346 to -356 kcal/mol, achieving approximately 84% base-paired structural stability, and reduced immune-stimulatory motifs - lowering the average immune penalty to 27.3 in the final generation. Linear Design produces hyper-stable transcripts (MFE < - 2000 kcal/mol) that risk translation inefficiency due to extreme rigidity, and BiLSTM-CRF focuses solely on high CAI (0.96 to 0.98) without structural constraints, our framework achieves an optimal translation-stability equilibrium, highlighting the proposed BERT-GA framework as an effective, data-driven approach for the design and optimization of in-silico mRNA sequences.

### [81] [Auditing Stance Asymmetry in Generative Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27988)
*Jiarui Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为对称性分解评估（SDE）的新方法，用于检测语言模型在生成解释时存在的立场偏向不对称问题。传统偏见评估多关注显性贬损或刻板印象，而SDE聚焦于开放式解释中责任归属、正当性与情境构建的隐性不平等。通过成对情景测试、角色重构和证据控制，发现部分表面差异在结构或证据调整下减弱，而某些责任分配模式则保持稳定，表明模型存在系统性立场偏向。研究还指出，人工评判标准因操作方式不同而变化，量化评分可能掩盖读者感知的关键区别。因此，该文主张将生成式偏见评估从单纯指标比较转向对解释立场的审计，关注各方获得的立场、其在分解中的稳定性以及自动评分的可靠性边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型偏见评估主要针对显性贬损或受控替换下的标签敏感差异，但开放生成解释中的隐性立场偏向（如责任归因、正当性判断）尚未被充分捕捉。此类偏向可能以非敌意语言形式存在，却导致一方被结构性合理化，另一方被个人化归责，从而造成认知失衡。因此亟需新方法识别并评估这种‘立场承载不对称’现象。

Method: 提出对称性分解评估（SDE）框架，包含三个核心机制：1）构造成对情境（配对的群体对比案例）；2）进行结构角色重写（改变角色身份以检验因果逻辑是否一致）；3）引入支持/反证信息以测试模型响应的敏感性。通过32组原型案例进行控制实验，分析模型在不同条件下的输出差异，并结合人工案例审查与裁判者对比分析，揭示评分系统的局限性。

Result: SDE结果显示，部分表面差异在结构或证据控制下消失，说明其可被情境重构所影响；但仍有若干责任分配、合法性赋予与情境建构模式保持稳定，体现深层立场偏向。此外，不同评判标准导致结果波动，数值评分难以反映人类读者所察觉的微妙立场差异，暴露出自动评估体系的不稳定性。

Conclusion: 生成式偏见评估应从衡量表面差异转向审计解释立场本身——即模型如何对待不同群体、其立场在结构与证据变动中是否稳固，以及自动评分是否可靠。SDE提供了一种系统化工具，推动偏见评估进入更深层次的语用与伦理维度。

Abstract: Bias evaluation for language models has made substantial progress on bounded comparisons, such as overt derogation, stereotype association, or label-sensitive differences under controlled substitutions. Open-ended explanations raise a different problem: they guide interpretation by assigning responsibility, legitimacy, context, and grievance. A model can avoid hostile language while making one side structurally understandable and another personally at fault, overreacting, or less worth taking seriously. We call this stance-bearing asymmetry in generative explanations. We propose Symmetry Decomposition Evaluation (SDE), which tests paired situations with concrete group labels, structural-role rewrites, and explicit support or counter-evidence. In a controlled 32-family prototype suite, this decomposition shows that surface differences are not all alike: some weaken under structural or evidence control, while others remain as stable differences in how the model assigns blame, context, or legitimacy. Targeted case review and judge comparison suggest a broader difficulty for evaluating open-ended framing asymmetries: judge readings shift across operationalizations, and scalar scores can flatten distinctions that readers use to interpret explanatory stance. SDE therefore reframes generative bias evaluation as an audit of explanatory stance -- what stance each side receives, how it changes under decomposition, and where automatic scoring becomes unstable.

</details>


### [82] [Rethinking Visual Neglect: Steering via Context-Preference for MLLM Hallucination Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27993)
*Jingwen Wu,Xijun Zhang,Ge Song*

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种无需训练的框架CAS，通过设计冲突样本提取语义不同的上下文偏好向量，在推理时通过单次符号残差注入控制模型对图像和文本上下文的依赖，有效缓解对象幻觉问题，且不增加解码延迟并保持文本生成质量。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前方法假设幻觉源于视觉信息不足，但实验发现过度依赖视觉可能加剧某些模型的幻觉，表明仅归因于视觉不足是不充分的；需考虑图像、参数知识与文本上下文之间的竞争关系。

Method: 提出Context-Preference Activation Steering（CAS）框架，利用少量设计的冲突样本提取两个语义不同的上下文偏好向量（CPVs），并通过在推理过程中对中早期MLP层进行单次符号残差注入来调节信息依赖。

Result: CAS显著减少对象幻觉，不增加解码延迟，并保持原有的文本生成质量。

Conclusion: 图像作为上下文会与模型的参数知识和文本上下文竞争，因此不能简单将幻觉归因于视觉忽视；通过控制上下文依赖关系可有效缓解幻觉问题。

Abstract: Object hallucination remains a primary obstacle to the reliable deployment of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs). Current inference-time mitigation methods mainly assume hallucinations stem from visual neglect, steering models to enhance visual reliance. In contrast, our systematic interventions on multiple MLLMs show that pushing toward more visual reliance may exacerbate hallucinations on some models, while less may mitigate hallucinations. This result suggests that attributing hallucinations solely to visual insufficiency is underdetermined. We argue that the image, as a context, simultaneously competes with the model's parametric knowledge and the textual context. For this, we propose a training-free framework, Context-Preference Activation Steering (CAS). It extracts two semantically distinct Context Preference Vectors (CPVs) via two small sets of designed conflict samples and applies them via single-pass signed residual injection at mid-early MLP layers during inference to control information reliance. Experiments show that CAS substantially mitigates object hallucinations without increasing decoding latency and preserves native text-generation quality.

</details>


### [83] [Where Does Toxicity Live? Mechanistic Localization and Targeted Suppression in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27997)
*Himanshu Beniwal,Mayank Singh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Meow2X和TRNE两种无需重训练的框架，通过分析有毒与中性提示之间的激活差异，定位并抑制特定层和神经元中的毒性，实现推理时缩放或最小秩一权重编辑，无需梯度下降。在五个语言模型、两个基准测试和90种配置下评估，显示持续降低毒性同时保持语言建模质量。分析发现毒性主要编码在早期MLP层，不同架构间存在差异，且单评估器设置会系统性低估毒性，强调多评估器安全评估的重要性。该框架结合机制可解释性与实际去毒化，为更安全、透明的语言模型提供原则性路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有缓解方法依赖昂贵的重训练或输出层面过滤，缺乏对毒性内部起源的机制洞察。需要一种无需重训练、能定位并抑制毒性来源的方法，以提高语言模型的安全性和透明度。

Method: 通过分析有毒与中性提示间的激活差异，定位毒性所在层和神经元；采用推理时缩放或最小秩一权重编辑进行抑制，不使用梯度下降。

Result: 在五个语言模型、两个基准测试和90种配置下，毒性显著降低，同时保持语言建模质量；揭示毒性主要集中在早期MLP层，不同架构表现不同，单评估器易低估毒性。

Conclusion: 提出的框架通过机制可解释性与实用去毒化相结合，为构建更安全、透明的语言模型提供了有效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models frequently generate toxic, hateful, or harmful content, yet existing mitigation methods rely on costly retraining or output-level filtering with no mechanistic insight into where toxicity originates internally. We introduce Meow2X and TRNE, two complementary retraining-free frameworks that localize toxicity to specific layers and neurons by analyzing activation differentials between toxic and neutral prompts, then suppress them via inference-time scaling or minimal rank-one weight edits -- without any gradient descent. Evaluations across five LMs, two benchmarks, and 90 configurations using dual safety evaluators demonstrate consistent toxicity reduction while preserving language modeling quality. Our analysis reveals that toxicity is disproportionately encoded in early MLP layers, varies across architectures, and is systematically underestimated by single-evaluator setups -- underscoring the need for multi-evaluator safety assessment. By bridging mechanistic interpretability with practical detoxification, our framework offers a principled path toward safer, more transparent language models.

</details>


### [84] [ResearchMath-14K: Scaling Research-Level Mathematics via Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28003)
*Guijin Son,Seungyeop Yi,Minju Gwak,Hyunwoo Ko,Wongi Jang,Youngjae Yu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了ResearchMath-14k，一个包含14,056个研究级数学问题的大型数据集，是目前最大的研究级数学问题集合。通过多智能体管道从学术来源收集，并生成了22万条教师轨迹（ResearchMath-Reasoning），发现模型存在回避行为（如不尝试或伪造引用）。新版本模型产生更多引用和虚假引用。经智能体过滤后，对Qwen3系列模型（4B至30B参数）进行微调，平均性能提升9.2分，表明即使缺乏完全正确的推理轨迹，经过筛选的开放问题尝试仍可提供有效监督。数据集已公开，以促进研究级数学推理的发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前语言模型在无须人类干预的情况下难以有效处理尚无解的前沿数学问题，主要障碍在于缺乏大规模的研究级数学数据集。因此，亟需构建高质量、规模大的研究级数学问题数据集及相应推理轨迹，以推动模型在解决复杂数学问题上的能力。

Method: 采用多智能体管道从学术来源收集并整理研究级数学问题，构建ResearchMath-14k数据集；利用两个开源模型生成22万条推理轨迹（ResearchMath-Reasoning）；通过智能体过滤机制清理低质量或有缺陷的轨迹；基于过滤后的轨迹对Qwen3系列模型（4B–30B参数）进行微调，并评估其性能提升。

Result: 经过智能体过滤后，使用筛选后的开放问题推理轨迹对Qwen3模型进行微调，平均性能相比基线模型提升9.2分。同时，观察到较新的模型在生成引用方面更频繁，但其中虚假引用比例也显著上升。该结果表明，即便推理轨迹不完整或存在错误，经过筛选的开放问题尝试仍可作为有效的监督信号。

Conclusion: ResearchMath-14k是目前最大的研究级数学问题数据集，结合过滤后的推理轨迹可用于训练语言模型解决复杂数学问题。研究表明，即使缺乏完全正确的推理路径，经过筛选的开放问题尝试也能提供有效监督，为未来研究级数学推理模型的发展提供了重要基础。

Abstract: The frontier of mathematics is defined by problems whose solutions are not yet known, yet it remains unclear whether language models can meaningfully engage with such problems without human intervention. A major obstacle is the lack of large-scale research-level math datasets. To this end, we introduce ResearchMath-14k, a set of $14{,}056$ problems curated from academic sources via a multi-agent pipeline, making it the largest collection of research-level mathematical problems to date. We further generate ResearchMath-Reasoning, $220$K teacher trajectories from two open models, where we observe recurring avoidance behaviors such as non-attempts and fabricated references. Interestingly, across eight open-weight models, newer generations produce $5.6\times$ more references and $5.0\times$ more fake references per trace. After agentic filtering of ResearchMath-Reasoning, fine-tuning Qwen3 models from 4B to 30B parameters improves over base models by $9.2$ points on average. This shows that filtered open-problem attempts can provide useful supervision even without fully correct reasoning traces. We make ResearchMath-14k publicly available for future works on research-level mathematical reasoning.

### [85] [Integrated and Cross-Architecture Interpretation of LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28006)
*Leonardo Matthew Yauw,Wei-Bin Kou,Yujiu Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为IAR（Integrated, cross-Architecture Reasoning）的统一框架，用于提升大语言模型推理过程的可解释性。通过结合带宽校准的互信息峰值（MIP）与Tukey IQR峰检测方法，识别输出层中对推理至关重要的标记；进一步通过分析MIP标记与深度思考比（DTR）标记的重叠，追踪这些关键标记在不同层间的演化轨迹，并检验其是否具有计算密集性；最后利用Jaccard稳定性度量验证跨领域任务中识别出的标记是否能保障推理质量。实验在Qwen-7B、Qwen-14B和Llama-8B三个模型上，覆盖数学、代码、逻辑和常识四个领域，证明了该方法在多种架构下的通用解释能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型的推理过程难以理解，因为虽然输出可见，但内部推理模式不透明。现有单一探测方法（如MIP或DTR）可能低估真实的推理结构，导致解释不足。因此需要一种更全面、跨架构的解释框架来揭示推理的本质。

Method: 提出IAR框架：1）使用带宽校准的MIP结合Tukey IQR峰检测法，定位输出层中推理关键的标记；2）进行MIP标记与DTR深度标记的重叠分析，以追踪关键标记在模型各层之间的演化路径；3）引入Jaccard稳定性指标，在多领域任务中验证所识别标记的推理质量保障能力。

Result: 在三个不同模型（Qwen-7B、Qwen-14B、Llama-8B）和四个领域（数学、代码、逻辑、常识）上的实验表明，IAR框架能够有效识别并稳定追踪推理关键标记，具备良好的跨架构通用性和解释力。

Conclusion: IAR框架为理解大语言模型的推理机制提供了统一、可推广的解释方法，克服了传统单点探测的局限性，有助于深入揭示模型内部推理模式的动态演化过程。

Abstract: Understanding how LLMs reason is hindered by a practical asymmetry: while their generated outputs are observable, the underlying reasoning patterns remain opaque. Relying on single probes, such as Mutual Information Peak (MIP) or Deep-Thinking Ratio (DTR), risks underestimating the genuine inferential structure. To response this deficiency, we present an Integrated, cross-Architecture Reasoning (IAR) framework, designed to provide a unified approach to LLM reasoning interpretability. Specifically, we first propose to use bandwidth-calibrated MIP coupled with Tukey IQR peak-detection to isolate reasoning-crucial tokens at the output layer. Second, we performed an overlap analysis between MIP-picked tokens and DTR-deep tokens to trace the cross-layer trajectories of those tokens. This also discloses whether reasoning-crucial tokens are computation-intensive as well, further facilitating to understand how reasoning patterns evolve across model layers. Finally, we apply a Jaccard stability metric over multi-domain problems to verify if the MIP-identified tokens are reasoning quality-guaranteed. Extensive experiments on three models (Qwen-7B, Qwen-14B, and Llama-8B) across four domains (mathematics, code, logic, and common sense) demonstrate IAR's generalizable interpretation capabilities across architectures.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出个性化观察归一化（PON）方法，每个智能体本地使用持续更新的运行均值和方差对原始状态输入进行归一化，避免跨智能体特征缩放冲突，并证明共享归一化参数无效。

Result: 在异构MuJoCo任务上，PON方法显著加速训练并取得更优性能，验证了个性化统计的必要性。

Abstract: Federated reinforcement learning (FedRL) enables multiple agents to collaboratively train a global policy without sharing raw data, making it ideal for privacy-sensitive applications. However, FedRL faces challenges in heterogeneous environments where differing state-transition dynamics lead to non-identical input distributions and imbalanced parameter updates during aggregation. Therefore, this paper develops a personalized observation normalization (PON) method, allowing each agent to locally normalize raw state inputs using a continuously updated running mean and variance. This design ensures consistent scaling of local feature without overshadowing across agents during aggregation. Furthermore, we demonstrate that sharing normalization parameters across agents is ineffective due to the diverse local input distributions, which highlights the necessity of personalized statistics. Experiments on heterogeneous MuJoCo tasks show that our developed PON accelerates training and achieves superior performance compared to baseline methods.

### [87] [IGADA-IoT: IoT Sensor Energy Optimization in Wireless Sensor Networks Driven by Automatic Data Augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27397)
*Mingchun Sun,Rongqiang Zhao,Muhammad Abdul Munnaf,Jie Liu*

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于信息间隙引导的物联网传感器自动数据增强框架IGADA-IoT，通过分层多生成器协作与调度策略（HMGCS）和信息间隙-模型性能联合评估与闭环方法（IGMP-EC），有效解决现有方法中生成器单一、样本异质性忽略及增广决策不准确的问题。实验表明，该方法在多个下游模型上平均准确率提升7.27%，优于先进方法8.67%，且具备良好的泛化能力。

  <summary>Details</summary>
