Conclusion: 所提出的IGADA-IoT框架通过多生成器协同与闭环评估机制，有效缓解了信息间隙与样本异质性带来的挑战，显著提升了物联网传感器数据增强的效果与可靠性，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: In wireless sensor networks (WSNs), data augmentation is a novel method to improve sampling-frequency decision performance, thereby enabling energy optimization for IoT (Internet of Things) sensors. However, existing methods rely on a single generator and empirically determined quantities, failing to establish a mapping between dynamic information gaps and multiple generators, and overlooking the heterogeneity of generated samples. Moreover, an evaluation and a closed-loop method that jointly considers the information gap and the model performance are lacking. To address these issues, we propose an information gap-guided IoT sensor automatic data augmentation framework (IGADA-IoT) with hierarchical multi-generator collaboration and scheduling over multiple rounds. Capabilities of different generators are jointly utilized to reduce the information gaps. In the IGADA-IoT, a hierarchical multi-generator collaboration and scheduling strategy (HMGCS) is proposed to enhance the targetedness and rationality of generated sample allocation. An information gap-model performance joint evaluation and closed-loop method (IGMP-EC) is proposed to enhance the accuracy of augmentation decisions, and to mitigate the risks of under-augmentation and over-augmentation. Experimental results show that the IGADA-IoT improves the average accuracy of multiple downstream models by 7.27%. Compared with advanced data augmentation methods, the average accuracy is improved by 8.67%. Compared with the individual generators, the average accuracy is improved by 7.24%. Furthermore, public IoT sensor datasets from the UCR Archive and real-world deployments demonstrate the accuracy and generalizability of the proposed method.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出E^3-Agent，采用快路径路由器进行毫秒级调度，慢路径基于LLM的元控制器通过工具接口实现风险控制、路由配置和快速性能校准，利用执行反馈在线学习并持续适应变化环境。

Abstract: Edge deployments of generative inference increasingly face two practical realities: per-device per-model performance is often unknown at deployment time, and it is non-stationary due to user-driven semantic events, background load, and device churn. Consequently, a resource manager that is tuned offline under a fixed regime can become brittle and expensive to maintain. This paper presents $E^3$-Agent, an executable and evolving agent for edge artificial intelligence generated content (AIGC) resource management. $E^3$-Agent separates a fast-path router that makes millisecond-level dispatch decisions from a slow-path, event-driven large language model (LLM) meta-controller that mitigates regime shifts through a small, explicit control surface exposed via a tool interface, including risk gating, router configuration, and rapid performance calibration. The agent learns online from execution feedback and continuously adapts to unknown and time-varying service-time mappings. We evaluate $E^3$-Agent in a discrete-event simulator driven by MLPerf-derived device-model measurement priors, covering cold-start warmup and three dynamic regimes: semantic dynamics, device churn, and hidden drift. Across the dynamic scenarios, $E^3$-Agent reduces average latency by 65%-73% compared to the best static baseline, stays within 7%-10% of an online full-information Oracle used for evaluation, and effectively suppresses stutter rate under semantic degradation.

### [89] [Tackling Multimodal Learning Challenges with Mixture-of-Expert: A Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27431)
*Liangwei Nathan Zheng,Wei Emma Zhang,Olaf Maennel,Lin Yue,Weitong Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有综述多孤立评估多模态学习或MoE方法，缺乏对二者协同机制的系统性分析。本文旨在填补这一空白，揭示MoE在解决多模态挑战中的独特作用。

Method: 基于全面文献回顾，从三个核心视角系统梳理MoE在多模态学习中的应用机制：效率优化、表征学习与适应性建模，并归纳关键研究挑战。

Result: 识别出可解释路由、专家间通信、模态整合及终身学习等重要研究缺口，为构建更智能、可持续的多模态MoE系统提供理论基础。

Conclusion: 本综述为未来可解释、可持续的多模态混合专家系统研究奠定基础，推动其在复杂真实场景下的应用发展。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) presents a naturally compatible and scalable framework for multimodal learning, demonstrating strong adaptability across diverse modalities and tasks. Despite its growing success, a comprehensive and systematic review on the MoE metho addressing multimodal challenges remains lacking. Existing surveys tend to evaluate either multimodal learning or MoE independently from method taxonomy, overlooking the unique interplay between them. This survey fills that gap by answering a central question: \textit{How does MoE effectively resolve multimodal challenges?} We approach this from three key perspectives: (1) \textbf{MoE as an Efficient Multimodal Engine:} enabling scalable multimodal modeling by decoupling computational cost from parameter growth and mitigating modality redundancy through selective expert activation; (2) \textbf{MoE as a Multimodal Representation Learner:} integrating complementary multi-opinion expert knowledge to enrich alignment and interaction representations; and (3) \textbf{MoE as a Multimodal Adapter:} providing a modular and flexible mechanism to model imperfect data scenarios such as modality imbalance and missing modality. Through our extensive literature review, we identify critical research gaps, including interpretable routing, expert communication, modality integration, and lifelong multimodal learning. We position this survey as a foundation for future research toward interpretable and sustainable multimodal Mixture-of-Experts system.

### [90] [HEAL: Resilient and Self-* Hub-based Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27475)
*Mohamed Amine Legheraba,Stefan Galkiewicz,Maria Gradinariu Potop-Butucaru,Sébastien Tixeuil*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HEAL is a novel cross-layer decentralized learning framework that combines the strengths of Federated Learning, Gossip, and Epidemic Learning. It uses an optimized self-organizing and self-healing P2P overlay with dynamically chosen aggregators via the Elevator algorithm. HEAL achieves performance comparable to Federated Learning in stable environments and outperforms Gossip and Epidemic Learning in crash-prone and churn-heavy settings.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing decentralized learning methods like Federated Learning have a central aggregator, leading to single points of failure and privacy risks. Gossip and Epidemic Learning are fully decentralized but suffer from slow convergence. There is a need for a robust, scalable, and efficient decentralized framework that maintains fast convergence while ensuring fault tolerance and privacy.

Method: HEAL introduces a self-organizing and self-healing P2P overlay network using the Elevator algorithm to dynamically select aggregator nodes. This enables decentralized model updates without relying on a fixed central server, combining the efficiency of Federated Learning with the resilience of Gossip and Epidemic Learning.

Result: Simulations show HEAL matches Federated Learning's performance in crash-free environments and significantly outperforms Gossip and Epidemic Learning in environments with crashes and high churn, demonstrating superior fault tolerance and convergence speed.

Conclusion: HEAL is the first cross-layer decentralized learning framework that effectively balances performance, scalability, and fault tolerance by integrating dynamic aggregation into a resilient P2P network, making it well-suited for real-world distributed learning systems.

Abstract: Decentralized learning enhances privacy, scalability, and fault tolerance by distributing data and computation across nodes. A popular approach is Federated learning, which relies on a central aggregator, yet faces challenges such as server vulnerabilities, scalability issues, privacy risks and most importantly, the single point of failure. Alternatively Gossip Learning and Epidemic Learning offer fully decentralization through peer-to-peer exchanges of model updates, ensuring robustness and privacy, at the price of slower model convergence. In this work, we introduce a novel decentralized learning framework called HEAL. HEAL is the first cross-layer decentralized learning framework that exploits an optimized self-organizing and self-healing underlying P2P overlay combining the strengths of Federated Learning, Gossip and Epidemic Learning. Leveraging the recently proposed Elevator algorithm, HEAL promotes dynamically chosen nodes to act as aggregators. Through simulations, we demonstrate that HEAL has similar performances to that of Federated Learning in crash-free settings, while being fully decentralized and fault-tolerant. In crash and churn prone environments HEAL outperforms Gossip and Epidemic Learning.

### [91] [Balancing Fidelity and Diversity in Diffusion Models via Symmetric Attention Decomposition: Hopfield Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27476)
*Hyunmin Cho,Woo Kyoung Han,Kyong Hwan Jin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文将Transformer中的预软最大注意力矩阵$\mathbf{QK^\top}$视为编码输入特征之间成对关联的关联记忆矩阵。通过将其分解为对称与反对称部分，对称部分被解释为控制能量景观结构，反对称部分则驱动该景观上的循环动力学。基于对称部分诱导的能量公式，推导出类似霍普菲尔德的稳定性度量，用于量化检索特征的稳定性，并发现这些度量与生成中的保真度-多样性权衡存在显著相关性。最后提出一种可调控的机制，通过调节底层动力学的循环来控制这一权衡。代码已公开于GitHub。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Transformer中注意力机制的内在动力学特性，特别是其如何在生成任务中影响保真度与多样性之间的权衡，进而提供可调控的机制以优化生成质量。

Method: 将注意力矩阵$\\mathbf{QK^\\top}$分解为对称与反对称部分；利用对称部分构建能量景观，引入类霍普菲尔德稳定性度量；分析稳定性与生成性能的关系，并设计基于循环调节的可控参数。

Result: Hopfield-style稳定性度量与生成的保真度-多样性权衡具有显著相关性；通过调节反对称部分（即循环）可有效控制生成结果的多样性与保真度。

Conclusion: 注意力矩阵的对称与反对称分解揭示了Transformer中动态行为的本质，提供了理解并可控调节生成质量的新视角。

Abstract: We characterize the pre-softmax attention matrix $\mathbf{QK^\top}$ in transformers as an associative memory matrix encoding pairwise associations between input features. By decomposing this matrix into its symmetric and skew-symmetric parts, we interpret the symmetric component as governing the structure of the energy landscape, and the skew-symmetric component as driving circulation on that landscape. Leveraging the energy formulation induced by the symmetric component, we derive Hopfield-style stability measures that quantify the stability of retrieved features. We observe meaningful correlations between Hopfield-style stability measures and the fidelity-diversity trade-offs in generation. Finally, we propose a controllable knob to modulate this trade-off by modifying the circulation of the underlying dynamics. Code is available at our GitHub (https://github.com/hyeon-cho/Attention-Symmetric-Decomposition).

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出方差正则化剪枝（VR）框架，通过联合评估每个连接在预测准确性和跨用户变异性方面的贡献，优先保留那些在不同用户间表现稳定的参数，实现高效且稳健的模型压缩。

Conclusion: VR框架有效平衡了模型效率与跨用户鲁棒性，为开发轻量级、可靠的实时情感计算系统提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Affective computing systems are increasingly embedded in pervasive and interactive environments, such as adaptive games, assistive technologies, and resource-constrained platforms, where computational efficiency must be balanced with reliability across diverse users. In this work, we introduce Variance-Regularised Pruning (VR), a pruning framework that explicitly incorporates cross-participant stability into the sparsification process. Rather than relying solely on average prediction error, VR evaluates each connection based on its joint contribution to both prediction accuracy and variability across users, prioritising parameters that remain reliable under distributional differences. We evaluate the proposed approach on the AGAIN dataset, which includes arousal annotations collected across nine affect-eliciting game environments. Experimental results demonstrate that VR maintains competitive Concordance Correlation Coefficient (CCC) performance even at 80\% sparsity without additional fine-tuning, highlighting its suitability for deployment in real-world, resource-limited affect-aware systems. ### [95] [SparseOpt: Addressing Normalization-induced Gradient Skew in Sparse Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27541)

We demonstrate both analytically and empirically that Batch Normalization (BN) adversely affects sparse training, and propose SparseOpt, a sparsity-aware optimizer, to address this. Experiments on ResNet models across CIFAR-100 and ImageNet demonstrate consistently faster convergence and improved generalization with our proposed method. Our work highlights the limitations of current normalization layers in sparse training and provides the first systematic study of the interaction between Batch Normalization, sparse layers, and DST, taking a significant step toward making DST practically competitive with dense training.

An update vector is a vector of parameter changes from an initial model to its fine-tuned version on a dataset, capturing the effect of cumulative gradient steps during fine-tuning. The key idea of our framework is a novel Gradient Transformer that transforms TinyLM's update vectors into LLM's update vectors. ### [98] [Evaluating Local Explainability Metrics for Machine Learning Models on Tabular Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27618)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Despite the wide use of explainability techniques to attempt to understand the behavior of Artificial Intelligence (AI), the generated explanations may not always be reliable. An explanation can appear plausible to humans but fail to capture the internal reasoning of a model, particularly when dealing with complex tabular data. This paper studies the trustworthiness of local explainability techniques when applied to complex tabular classification tasks, considering evaluated metrics for three main properties: faithfulness to the model's predictions, robustness to input data variations, and complexity of the explanation itself. Model performance ranges were analyzed to identify two groups: consensus-correct, which are samples that all models predicted correctly, and consensus-wrong, samples that all models predicted incorrectly. The obtained results demonstrate that that the explanations are not always correlated with a model's predictive performance. Instead, dataset complexity and feature distributions seem to be the main factors affecting explanation quality and reliability.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分布式降维方法在监督场景下研究不足，难以同时保持数据内在几何结构和与目标任务相关的信息，导致在压缩数据时可能丢失重要预测信号。因此亟需一种能联合优化数据结构与监督信息的表示学习方法。

Method: SDR基于融合格罗莫夫-沃瑟斯坦（FGW）目标，将输入分布的关联结构与一组代表性点对齐，同时引入显式依赖项以增强嵌入表示对预测信号的捕捉能力，实现几何结构与监督信号的联合优化。

Result: 实验表明，所提方法能够生成紧凑且富含预测信息的表示，不仅提升了下游任务性能，还在高斯过程建模中实现了自适应的非平稳核构造，展现出对局部数据变化和监督信号的敏感性。

Conclusion: SDR提供了一种基于最优传输的监督表示学习框架，有效平衡了数据压缩与预测保真度，为复杂任务下的数据降维与模型泛化提供了新思路。

Abstract: Learning representations that capture both intrinsic data geometry and target-relevant structure remains a fundamental challenge, particularly in settings where data reduction must balance compression with predictive fidelity. While distributional reduction-encompassing joint clustering and dimensionality reduction-offers a principled way to summarize data, its supervised variants remain relatively under-explored, despite the importance of retaining task-relevant signal for downstream prediction and decision-making. We propose Supervised Distributional Reduction (SDR), an algorithm for learning target-aware representations by combining optimal transport with explicit dependence maximization. SDR builds on the Fused Gromov-Wasserstein (FGW) objective to align the relational structure of the input distribution with a set of representative points, while augmenting it with a direct dependence term that encourages the learned embeddings to capture predictive signal more explicitly. This results in compact representations that reflect both geometric structure and supervision. Beyond representation learning, SDR naturally induces a data-dependent, non-stationary geometry that can be leveraged for settings such as Gaussian Process (GP) modelling. By redefining distances through target-aware distributional alignment, SDR enables the construction of adaptive kernels that respond to local variations in both data geometry and supervision, offering an optimal transport-based perspective on non-stationary kernel design.

</details>


### [100] [Aligning LLMs with Human Uncertainty: A Beta-Bernoulli Calibrator for LLM Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27668)
*Hui Dai,Ryan Teehan,Parsa Torabian,Mengye Ren*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Beta-Bernoulli Calibrator（BBC）模型，通过结合二元结果和人类预测中的概率估计与共识度信号，将初始点估计转化为事件可能性的分布，提升大语言模型在概率预测上的校准性和准确性。该方法轻量且泛化能力强，其捕获的信念不确定性比口头自信更可靠地预测预测误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法仅利用二元结果进行校准，忽略了人类预测中蕴含的概率估计和共识信息；如何有效利用这些丰富信号以提升大语言模型的预测性能尚不明确。

Method: 采用贝塔-伯努利生成模型，建模事件发生概率 $p \sim \text{Beta}(\alpha, \beta)$ 和观测结果 $y \sim \text{Bernoulli}(p)$，利用二元结果和人类预测联合监督，将点估计转化为分布输出，同时以均值作为校准后的点预测，方差作为认知不确定性度量。

Result: BBC在多数场景下优于传统后处理校准方法和专门微调的预测模型，具有更高的校准性、准确性和泛化能力；其捕捉的不确定性显著优于口头自信，能更可靠地预测预测误差。

Conclusion: 通过融合人类预测中的集体智慧信号，BBC提供了一种高效、轻量且可推广的概率校准框架，显著提升了大语言模型在不确定事件预测中的表现，尤其在不确定性量化方面具有优势。

Abstract: Probabilistic forecasting estimates the likelihood of uncertain future events. To improve LLM forecasting, existing methods typically learn from binary outcomes to output verbalized forecasts. However, while aggregated human forecasts contain rich information in both the crowd probability estimate and the degree of agreement among forecasters, how to utilize these signals remains underexplored. To address this, we propose the Beta-Bernoulli Calibrator (BBC), which converts an initial point estimate forecast from any model into a distribution over event likelihood, using supervision from both binary outcomes and human forecasts. BBC models event likelihood $p \sim \text{Beta}(α, β)$ and outcome $y \sim \text{Bernoulli}(p)$, with the mean as the calibrated point forecast and the variance as the epistemic uncertainty. Our results show that BBC generally provides better calibrated and more accurate forecasts than both traditional post-hoc calibration methods and models fine-tuned specifically for forecasting, while remaining lightweight and having good generalization. We also show that the epistemic uncertainty captured by BBC is a more reliable predictor of forecasting error than verbalized confidence.

### [101] [Heterogeneous Parallelism for Multimodal Large Language Model Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27678)
*Yashaswi Karnati,Kamran Jafari,Akash Mehra,Li Ding,Pranav Prashant Thombre,Ali Roshan Ghias,Shifang Xu,Parth Mannan,Yu Yao,Hao Wu,Eric Harper,Ashwath Aithal,Nima Tajbakhsh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出异构并行机制以应对多模态大语言模型训练中因模态扩展、上下文窗口增长和编码器与解码器架构差异带来的并行瓶颈。传统单一LLM中心的并行布局（如TP/CP/PP/DP/EP）限制了吞吐量，尤其在长上下文场景下问题显著。作者设计了支持模块独立布局与秩放置的异构并行抽象，允许模块共置或非共置执行，并通过边界通信器实现跨布局的前向激活与反向梯度传递。调度扩展支持两种模式。实验表明，共置异构并行可提升每GPU TFLOPS达49.3%，非共置异构并行则提升总令牌吞吐13.0%及每GPU TFLOPS 9.6%。损失收敛性与同质基线一致，系统已开源为Megatron-LM扩展。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出异构并行框架，允许端到端图中各模块使用独立的并行布局与秩放置策略；通过边界通信器实现不同布局间的前向激活材料化与反向梯度路由；引入调度扩展以支持共置与非共置执行模式；采用分层调度与动态通信优化保证边界张量语义一致性。

Result: 在多种多模态工作负载与GPU规模上评估显示，共置异构并行提升每GPU TFLOPS达49.3%，非共置异构并行提升总令牌吞吐13.0%、每GPU TFLOPS达9.6%；损失收敛性与同质基线一致，验证了方法的有效性与稳定性。

Conclusion: 异构并行机制有效突破了传统单一模型并行布局的性能瓶颈，通过模块级独立布局与智能边界通信，在多模态大模型训练中实现了显著的吞吐与效率提升，为未来大规模多模态模型训练提供了灵活、高效的新范式。

Abstract: Foundation model training is becoming multimodal, from post-training pipelines to large-scale pretraining. As modality coverage broadens, context windows grow, and encoder LLM scales diverge, a single LLM-centric TP/CP/PP/DP/EP layout increasingly limits throughput. This coupling forces encoders to inherit LLM-driven sharding and placement choices that can add communication, limit encoder parallelism, or constrain the LLM schedule; the mismatch is most pronounced at long contexts, where LLM context parallelism is needed for the fused multimodal sequence but encoder inputs remain bounded. We present heterogeneous parallelism for multimodal large language model training, an abstraction that lets modules in one end-to-end graph use independent layouts and rank placements, supporting colocated execution on shared GPUs and non-colocated execution on disjoint rank sets. The key challenge is preserving boundary tensor semantics across independent layouts: forward activations must be materialized for the destination layout, while backward gradients must be routed back to the source layout. We address this with boundary communicators that implement forward and backward layout transforms, plus scheduling extensions for both placement modes. We evaluate optimized homogeneous, colocated heterogeneous, and non-colocated heterogeneous configurations across multimodal workloads and GPU scales to characterize when added layout and placement freedom exposes a better operating point. Across this sweep, colocated heterogeneity improves TFLOPS/GPU by up to 49.3%, while non-colocated heterogeneity improves aggregate token throughput by up to 13.0% and TFLOPS/GPU by up to 9.6%. We validate loss convergence parity against homogeneous baselines and release the system as an open-source Megatron-LM extension.

Abstract: Reinforcement learning and data-driven autonomous controllers are commonly evaluated using cumulative reward and empirical success frequency under finite simulation trajectories. However, such empirical metrics do not necessarily provide sufficient statistical evidence regarding deployment readiness under uncertainty. This work develops a Bayesian approval framework for learned autonomous landing controllers under finite rollout evidence. A probabilistic landing capability formulation is introduced based on touchdown safety satisfaction under uncertain operating conditions, while Bayesian posterior inference is used to quantify uncertainty regarding the true deployment capability of learned policies. Posterior approval probability and posterior deployment risk are further introduced for deployment-oriented evaluation, together with a sequential validation framework supporting approve/reject/continue decisions during progressive rollout testing. ### [103] [Can Entry-Wise Clipping Give Spectral Control of Stochastic Gradients?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27733)
*Zitao Song,Cedar Site Bai,Zhe Zhang,Brian Bullins,David F. Gleich*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究语言训练中由随机梯度噪声引起的训练不稳定性问题，发现噪声具有重尾特性且难以通过小批量平均消除。现有方法如向量范数裁剪忽略权重更新的矩阵结构，而谱归一化虽保留结构但成本较高。作者提出一种基于一阶扰动分析的新方法，揭示了此类噪声的局域化特性，并设计了一种可计算的近似贝叶斯最优逐元素估计器，在柯西污染噪声下实现了$O(ε^{-4})$的收敛保证。实验表明，该方法在NanoGPT预训练中使Adam优化器节省约7%的训练令牌，结合谱归一化进一步提升至约2%的额外节省。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决语言训练中因罕见表达和多层组合导致的重尾梯度噪声引发的训练不稳定性问题，现有方法在保持矩阵结构与降低计算成本之间存在权衡。

Method: 基于一阶扰动分析揭示噪声局域化特性，推导出在高斯信号先验下的贝叶斯最优逐元素估计器的可计算近似，实现对重尾噪声的有效控制。

Result: 理论证明在柯西污染噪声下具有$O(ε^{-4})$收敛性；实验证明该方法在NanoGPT预训练中显著减少训练所需的令牌数，相比Adam节省约7%，与谱归一化结合再节省约2%。

Conclusion: 通过利用梯度噪声的局域化特性，提出一种高效且具结构感知能力的逐元素修正方法，可在不增加过多计算成本的前提下有效缓解训练不稳定性，为大规模语言模型训练提供更高效的优化方案。

Abstract: Training instabilities such as loss spikes are frequently the result of stochastic gradient noise. Because of rare expressions in language training data, and multiple layer composition, the noise impact is heavy-tailed and survives mini-batch averaging. Existing remedies trade off structure against cost: vector-norm clipping ignores the matrix structure of weight updates, while spectral normalization (e.g., Muon (Jordan et al., 2024)) respects it at additional cost. We show that this trade-off can be balanced. Real gradient noise appears to be similar to entry-wise heavy-tailed contamination, and a first-order perturbation analysis reveals a localization property of such noise, under which a simple entry-wise method achieves spectral control. Exploiting this, we derive a tractable surrogate for the Bayes-optimal entry-wise estimator under a Gaussian signal prior. We establish $O(ε^{-4})$ convergence guarantee under Cauchy-contaminated noise. Empirically, we find that smooth shrinkage improves Adam on NanoGPT pretraining, saving ${\sim}7\%$ of training tokens. We further find that applying the entry-wise clipping before spectral normalization yields a ${\sim}2\%$ token saving on top of Muon.

### [104] [A Paired Testing Protocol for Batch-Conditioned Refusal Robustness in LLM Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27763)
*Sahil Kadadekar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了语言模型安全评估中批处理配置对行为表现的显著影响，提出一种基于四项实证研究的配对测试协议。结果显示，安全标签变化频率（0.51%）高于能力标签变化（0.14%），但经校正后真实行为翻转率仅为0.16%；跨模型扩展发现安全与能力翻转近乎平衡（0.94倍），且输出不稳定性是主要脆弱性指标（r=0.909）。通过内核消融实验验证，启用batch-invariant模式可完全消除55个候选翻转中的全部标签变化，表明批处理敏感性是关键变量。最终建议采用精确堆栈验证：在实际批处理环境下评估拒绝行为，将安全提示与能力控制配对，并单独报告低频方向性翻转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型安全评估通常将服务配置视为固定背景，忽视批处理条件（如独立评估、同步批处理或连续批处理调度）对模型行为的影响，导致潜在的行为偏差未被检测。

Method: 整合四项实证研究：Study A结合本地发现、评分校正的裁定与真实批处理确认；Study B测试跨模型泛化；Study C分析连续批处理组合效应；Study D执行批处理不变内核的消融实验。

Result: 本地测试中安全标签变化率（0.51%）高于能力标签（0.14%），经人工裁定后仅17例为真实行为翻转，校正后总率为0.16%；15模型扩展显示安全与能力翻转接近平衡（0.94倍），无显著关联（p=0.942, η²=0.033），输出不稳定性为最强脆弱性指标（r=0.909）；内核消融中，启用VLLM_BATCH_INVARIANT=1后，55个候选翻转全部消失（0/55），而标准vLLM重现22例；组合测试未见聚合效应（4.7pp敏感度）。

Conclusion: 应采用精确堆栈验证策略：在真实批处理环境下评估模型拒绝行为，将安全提示与能力控制配对，并单独报告低频方向性翻转，避免因批处理差异掩盖真实性能表现。

Abstract: Safety evaluations of language models often treat serving configuration as fixed background infrastructure, but batch condition is an untested treatment variable whenever the same prompt may be evaluated alone, in a synchronized batch, or inside a continuous-batching scheduler. We synthesize four artifact-backed studies into a paired testing protocol: Study A combines local discovery, scorer-corrected adjudication, and true-batching confirmation; Study B tests cross-model generalization; Study C tests continuous-batch composition; and Study D runs a batch-invariant-kernel ablation. The local test finds safety-label changes more often than capability-label changes (0.51% vs. 0.14%), but adjudication of 63 candidate rows leaves only 17 genuine behavioral flips, implying a corrected full-set rate of 0.16%. The 15-model extension finds no detectable universal safety-over-capability skew: flips are near parity (0.94x), alignment type has no detectable association ($p=0.942$, $η^2=0.033$), and output instability is the strongest tested fragility screen ($r=0.909$, bootstrap 95% CI [0.65, 0.97]). In the targeted kernel ablation, standard vLLM reproduces 22/55 label flips on current score-flip candidates, while enabling VLLM_BATCH_INVARIANT=1 reduces the same test to 0/55 flips; the composition test separately finds no aggregate effect at 4.7pp sensitivity. The testing recommendation is exact-stack validation: evaluate refusal at the served batch setting, pair safety prompts with capability controls, and report low-rate directional flips separately from aggregate null effects.

### [105] [Restoring the Sweet Spot: Pass-Rate Weighted Self-Distillation for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27765)
*Zehao Liu,Yuanpu Cao,Jinghui Chen,Vasant G. Honavar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SC-SDPO通过引入基于预测概率方差的加权机制，解决了SDPO在难度感知上的不足，实现更稳定的训练和性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SDPO虽能提供密集的词级信用分配，但其基于KL的奖励缺乏对问题难度的隐式感知，导致学习效率不均衡。而GRPO通过归一化优势具有天然的难度聚焦能力，因此本文旨在分析并弥补SDPO的这一缺陷。

Method: 基于GRPO的优势归一化思想，将可学习性框架扩展至归一化奖励，发现归一化过程吸收了方差项 $p(1-p)$，仅留下 $\sqrt{p(1-p)}$ 作为残余缩放因子；据此提出在SDPO损失中按 $[\hat{p}(1-\hat{p})]^{1/2}$ 加权，形成SC-SDPO。该权重可通过在线策略回溯中的批处理自适应归一化零成本获得，隐含动态课程学习机制。

Result: 在科学推理与工具使用基准测试中，SC-SDPO显著优于SDPO，Qwen3-8B上取得+3.2/+4.3（mean@16/maj@16）的提升，OLMo-3-7B上为+1.8/+3.0，且训练过程保持稳定。

Conclusion: SC-SDPO通过引入简单有效的加权策略，实现了与GRPO类似的难度感知能力，无需额外计算开销，提升了大语言模型强化学习的训练效率与性能表现。

Abstract: Self-Distillation Policy Optimization (SDPO) provides dense token-level credit assignment for reinforcement learning with large language models by leveraging the model's own feedback-conditioned predictions as a self-teacher. Unlike GRPO, however, whose group-relative advantage naturally concentrates learning on a sweet spot of intermediate-difficulty questions, SDPO's KL-based advantage lacks an implicit notion of difficulty awareness.
  We analyze this gap through the lens of GRPO's advantage normalization. Extending the learnability framework to normalized rewards, we show that normalization absorbs the variance term $p(1-p)$, equalizing leading-order learnability across questions and leaving $\sqrt{p(1-p)}$ as the sole residual scaling factor in the per-question gradient. This analysis yields a simple prescription: weight each question's SDPO loss by $[\hat{p}(1-\hat{p})]^{1/2}$, resulting in SC-SDPO, a scale-consistent variant of SDPO.
  The proposed weights are obtained as a zero-cost byproduct of on-policy rollouts with batch-adaptive normalization, inducing an implicit curriculum that dynamically tracks the model's evolving competence. Experiments on scientific reasoning and tool-use benchmarks demonstrate that SC-SDPO consistently improves over SDPO, yielding gains of +3.2/+4.3 (mean@16/maj@16) on Qwen3-8B and +1.8/+3.0 on OLMo-3-7B, while preserving stable training dynamics throughout optimization.

</details>


### [106] [Fine-Tuning Dynamics of In-Context Factual Recall in Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27774)
*Ruomin Huang,Eshaan Nichani,Jason D. Lee,Rong Ge*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型在上下文学习中如何利用事实知识回忆，提出并形式化了‘上下文事实回忆（IC-recall）’任务。通过理论分析和实验验证，发现一维变压器在少量样本（仅对数级）的微调下即可通过特定的成对注意力模式实现知识回忆，且该模式在预训练记忆层时依然有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论多关注仅依赖提示信息的上下文学习，但实际应用中模型常需从参数中检索存储的事实知识，上下文仅用于识别相关知识。因此需要理解模型如何利用内部知识进行推理。

Method: 引入IC-recall任务，使用带有（主体, 答案）对的上下文和查询主体，建模事实知识为一个预构建的MLP关联记忆（存储三元组：主体, 关系, 答案），分析单层变压器在该任务上的监督微调动态，并证明其收敛至特定成对注意力模式。

Result: 理论证明模型在极少数样本（polylogarithmic数量级）下可成功完成IC-recall；实验验证了预测结果，表明成对注意力模式在预训练记忆层情况下仍能出现。

Conclusion: 大语言模型可通过极少量微调样本，在上下文学习中高效利用内部事实知识进行回忆，关键机制是形成特定的成对注意力模式，该机制在不同记忆设置下均成立。

Abstract: In-context learning \ -- performing tasks based on examples given in the prompt \ -- is an important capability that has emerged in large language models and has received significant attention in both theory and practice. Existing theoretical work often focuses on settings where the learning uses information purely from the prompt. However, many practical instances of in-context learning require the model to retrieve factual knowledge stored in the model's parameters, with the context serving to identify which knowledge is relevant. In this work, we study how in-context learning leverages factual knowledge recall. We formalize this behavior by introducing the \emph{in-context factual recall (IC-recall)} task, where a transformer is provided a context of (subject, answer) pairs generated from a hidden relation, along with a query subject, and must both infer this hidden relation and retrieve the corresponding answer. Factual knowledge is modeled by the transformer having access to a simple pre-constructed MLP associative memory storing (subject, relation, answer) triplets. We analyze the supervised fine-tuning dynamics of a one-layer transformer on IC-recall data and prove that the model successfully performs IC-recall by converging to a particular pairwise attention pattern. This fine-tuning stage requires a very small number of samples \ -- only polylogarithmic in the number of stored knowledge triplets. Experiments verify our theoretical predictions and show that the pairwise attention pattern emerges even when the MLP layer is pretrained instead of constructed.

### [107] [Revisiting ML Training under Fully Homomorphic Encryption: Convergence Guarantees, Differential Privacy, and Efficient Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27782)
*Yvonne Zhou,Mingyu Liang,Ivan Brugere,Danial Dervovic,Yue Guo,Antigoni Polychroniadou,Min Wu,Dana Dachman-Soled*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次对全同态加密（FHE）下的机器学习训练进行理论收敛性分析，结合专为加密计算设计的差分隐私（DP）训练算法，在保持可比效用的同时提升了计算效率。通过使用多项式近似激活函数和损失函数实现FHE兼容，并证明了近似梯度下降的收敛性；同时避免了昂贵的逐样本梯度裁剪，实现了可扩展的加密学习。还提出了数据无关的超参数选择与理论支撑的多项式近似策略，推动了高效、私密且安全的机器学习在敏感数据上的应用。

Motivation: 现有方法在全同态加密下进行差分隐私训练时存在计算开销大、效率低的问题，尤其依赖高成本的逐样本梯度裁剪，限制了实际应用。因此需要一种既保证隐私又提升计算效率的新型训练框架。

Method: 采用多项式近似激活函数和损失函数以适配全同态加密；设计无需逐样本梯度裁剪的差分隐私机制；结合近似梯度下降算法并进行理论收敛性分析；提出数据无关的超参数选择及理论指导的多项式逼近策略。

Result: 实现了在全同态加密环境下差分隐私训练的理论收敛性证明；相比标准差分隐私梯度下降显著提升计算效率；保持了良好的模型效用；提供了可独立应用的多项式近似与超参数优化方法。

Conclusion: 本研究为在保护隐私和安全的前提下实现高效机器学习提供了理论基础和技术支持，推动了敏感数据上可信人工智能的发展。

Abstract: We present the first theoretical convergence analysis of machine learning training under fully homomorphic encryption (FHE), combined with a differentially private (DP) training algorithm tailored to encrypted computation. Our approach improves computational efficiency over standard differentially private gradient descent (DP-GD) while achieving comparable utility. In particular, we prove convergence of approximate gradient descent using polynomial approximations of activation and loss functions, which are required for FHE compatibility. To preserve privacy in downstream tasks, we integrate differential privacy without relying on costly per-sample gradient clipping, enabling scalable encrypted learning. We also provide data-independent hyperparameter selection and theoretically grounded strategies for polynomial approximation which can be of independent interest. Together, these contributions advance the feasibility of efficient, private, and secure machine learning on sensitive data.

### [108] [Locality-Aware Redundancy Pruning for LLM Depth Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27786)
*Vincent-Daniel Yun,Youngrae Kim,Woosang Lim,YoungJin Heo,Minkyu Kim,Sunwoo Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为LoRP的无需训练的一次性深度剪枝框架，通过表征局部性来指导剪枝。该方法引入了表示局部性评分（RLS），基于全局层间隐藏状态相似性来衡量层间冗余的分布特性，并利用小规模校准集计算层间相似性，按簇内残余冗余分配剪枝量。在多种大语言模型家族上实验表明，该方法在困惑度和下游任务准确率方面均有提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有一次性剪枝方法依赖于局部层重要性或对架构间冗余的固定假设，无法有效捕捉不同架构下层间冗余的分布特性，因此需要一种更灵活、基于表征局部性的剪枝方法。

Method: 提出表示局部性评分（RLS），通过计算层间隐藏状态的全局相似性，使用小校准集进行层间相似性分析，采用聚类方式将层分组，并根据簇内冗余程度进行剪枝分配，实现无训练的一次性深度剪枝。

Result: 在多个大语言模型家族上验证，相比现有方法，LoRP在保持甚至提升模型性能的同时显著提升了推理效率，在困惑度和下游任务准确率方面均取得改进。

Conclusion: LoRP通过引入表示局部性评分，能够有效识别并利用不同架构中层间冗余的局部化或全局分布特性，实现了高效、精准的一次性深度剪枝，为大语言模型的轻量化部署提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large language models are known to contain representational redundancy across network depth, making depth pruning an effective approach for improving inference efficiency. Existing one-shot pruning methods rely on local layer importance or fixed redundancy assumptions across architectures. We propose Locality-Aware Redundancy Pruning (LoRP), a training-free one-shot depth pruning framework guided by representation locality. We show that inter-layer redundancy can be either localized or globally distributed depending on the LLM architecture. To characterize this phenomenon, we introduce Representation Locality Score (RLS), derived from global inter-layer hidden-state similarity. Using a small calibration set, LoRP computes pairwise layer similarity, clusters layers by representational similarity, and allocates pruning according to residual intra-cluster redundancy. Experiments across diverse LLM families show improvements in both perplexity and downstream task accuracy.

### [109] [Knowing When to Ask: Segment-Level Credit Assignment for LLM Tool Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27788)
*Abhijit Kumar,Zoey Wu,Mohit Suley*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CARL（Competence-Aware Reinforcement Learning）是一种新型强化学习框架，旨在让语言模型学会判断何时需要外部工具辅助，何时可依赖自身参数知识。通过分解推理轨迹中的自然工具调用边界（如代码块分隔符、上下文切换点），CARL在单一二元结果基础上为每个片段独立分配信用，无需外部标注或步骤级奖励。该方法有效区分了应使用工具与可自主解答的问题，在7B模型上达到0.93的AUC性能。在五个涵盖算术、多跳事实问答和金融表格数值推理的基准测试中，相比最佳基线，CARL在7B和3B模型上分别提升准确率6.7和9.7个点，尤其在Musique数据集上表现突出（+8.3和+9.0 EM）。同时，模型在可自主解答的问题上减少53%的工具调用，且准确率仍高出约10个点。小规模模型收益更大，3B模型的增益是7B模型的1.4倍，表明“知何时求助”对参数容量有限的模型尤为重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前语言模型缺乏对自身知识边界的认知：无法判断何时需借助外部工具（如计算器、搜索引擎）。传统提示工程虽能指导工具调用，但未教会模型自我识别能力；而现有强化学习方法基于整个轨迹的单一奖励信号，难以精确追踪具体工具调用的有效性，导致无法合理惩罚冗余或错误调用。因此亟需一种机制，使模型能从自身生成的推理过程中学习何时应求助，从而提升效率与准确性。

Method: 提出CARL框架，利用模型自身的滚动回放（rollouts）训练一个批判者（critic），通过在自然工具使用边界（如代码块分隔符、上下文切换点）处分解轨迹，将单一二元结果转化为各段落的独立信用分配。该方法不依赖外部评判或逐步标注，实现对错误工具调用、提取失败及多余调用的精准优势信号反馈，从而引导模型学习其领域内真实胜任范围。

Result: 在7B模型上，CARL在五项基准任务中平均提升准确率6.7点（7B）和9.7点（3B），最大增益达+8.3（7B）和+9.0（3B）于Musique数据集。模型在可自主回答的问题上减少53%的工具调用，同时保持约10点更高的准确率。小模型（3B）的相对提升是大模型（7B）的1.4倍，说明‘知何时求助’对低参数量模型价值更高。

Conclusion: CARL成功实现了语言模型对自身知识边界的自主感知，显著提升了工具调用的合理性与整体任务表现，尤其在小规模模型上效果更佳。该方法无需外部监督即可从内部轨迹中学习胜任能力，为构建更智能、高效、自省的AI系统提供了新路径。

Abstract: Humans know when to reach for help e.g. $347 \times 28$ warrants a calculator while $2+2$ does not. Language models do not. Prompt-based approaches can instruct a model when to invoke tools, but this scaffolding does not teach it to recognize the boundary of its own knowledge. RL approaches that assign a single outcome reward to the whole trajectory fare no better: trajectory-level credit cannot isolate which tool call in a successful episode actually helped, nor penalize unnecessary calls. We propose \textbf{CARL} (\textbf{C}ompetence-\textbf{A}ware \textbf{R}einforcement \textbf{L}earning), which trains a critic on the model's own rollouts to learn where parametric knowledge suffices and where it needs external help. By decomposing each rollout at natural tool-use boundaries (e.g., code fence delimiters and context block transitions), CARL assigns independent credit to each segment from a single binary outcome, without external judges or step-level annotations. As a result, erroneous tool calls, incorrect extractions, and unnecessary calls each receive appropriately signed advantages. The trained critic captures the model's domain competence: it separates parametrically solvable from tool-dependent questions with AUC 0.93 at 7B. On five benchmarks spanning arithmetic, multi-hop factual QA, and numerical reasoning over financial tables, CARL improves exact-match accuracy by 6.7 points at 7B and 9.7 points at 3B over the best RL baseline, with the largest gain (+8.3 EM at 7B, +9.0 EM at 3B) on Musique. The model issues 53\% fewer tool calls on parametrically answerable questions while remaining ${\sim}10$ EM points more accurate on them. Gains are largest at small scale: the 3B improvement is $1.4\times$ the 7B improvement, suggesting that knowing when to ask disproportionately benefits models with smaller parametric memory.

</details>

### [111] [Density-aware Sample-specific Attack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27809)
*Qiyuan Wang,Yao Li,Raymond K. W. Wong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新型后门攻击方法，通过在低密度区域放置触发样本以实现攻击成功率和干净准确率的双重优化。该方法基于贝叶斯最优模型，利用双层优化框架估计密度比并优化混合模型目标，显著提升对抗微调和剪枝防御的能力。实验表明，该方法在多个数据集上攻击成功率超过99%，且在防御后仍保持远高于基线的攻击成功率，在剪枝防御下完全免疫。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Despite recent progress in backdoor attacks, existing methods remain susceptible to post-training defenses that erase the backdoor through fine-tuning or pruning. We revisit the core objectives of backdoor attacks and derive principled criteria characterizing optimal sample-specific trigger construction under a Bayes-optimal model of the victim's training. Our analysis reveals that both attack success and clean-accuracy preservation are simultaneously optimized when triggered samples are steered into low-density regions of the clean data distribution, a distributional condition that controls all moments of the poisoned distribution at once rather than a handful of input-space summary statistics. We introduce a bilevel optimization framework that estimates density ratios via conditional time-score matching and optimizes a mixture-model objective to place triggered samples in these sparse regions. Extensive evaluations on MNIST, CIFAR-10, GTSRB, and TinyImageNet demonstrate that our method achieves above 99\% attack success rate before defense and retains 50--85 percentage points higher post-defense ASR than the strongest baselines under fine-tuning defenses. Against neuron-pruning defenses, the method exhibits complete immunity, with zero neurons identified for removal across all pruning thresholds. These results expose a fundamental gap in current defense paradigms and underscore the need for defenses that operate beyond the support of the clean distribution.

### [112] [ReSAE: Residualized Sparse Autoencoders for Multi-Layer Transformer Interventions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27819)
*Prathyush Poduval,Calvin Yeung,Neel Desai,Mohsen Imani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出残差化稀疏自编码器（ReSAEs），通过在层间拟合仿射映射，并在每层训练时基于未解释的残差而非完整激活，来解决多层干预中因层间耦合导致的信息冗余问题。与传统逐层训练的稀疏自编码器相比，ReSAEs减少了解码器冗余，在稀疏探测和目标扰动任务中表现更优；尽管重建的原始激活方差较少，但在多层替换下恢复的模型交叉熵更高，尤其在教师强制和足够稀疏条件下，表明其更好地保留了对下游计算至关重要的激活成分。结果表明，移除层间线性可预测结构是多层稀疏自编码器干预的有效默认策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统稀疏自编码器逐层训练，但Transformer残差流激活在深度上强耦合，导致多层干预时不同层字典可能重复表示相同信息，且多层同时替换会产生单层行为无法预测的交互效应。因此需要一种能处理层间耦合、减少冗余并提升多层干预效果的方法。

Method: 提出残差化稀疏自编码器（ReSAEs）：在选定层之间拟合仿射映射，后续层的稀疏自编码器仅在未解释的残差上训练，并通过拟合的仿射链将重构结果映射回原始激活空间，保持与普通S$AEs相同的干预评估协议。

Result: 在Pythia-1.4B和Gemma-2-9B上，ReSAEs显著降低了解码器冗余，提升了稀疏探测和目标扰动性能；虽然重建的原始激活方差较小，但在多层替换下恢复的交叉熵更高，尤其在教师强制和高稀疏度条件下优势明显，说明其更有效地保留了对模型下游计算关键的激活成分。

Conclusion: 移除线性可预测的跨层结构是多层稀疏自编码器干预中的有效默认策略，有助于提升干预效率与模型性能。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders are usually trained one layer at a time, even though transformer residual stream activations are strongly coupled across depth. This creates a practical problem for multi-layer interventions: different layerwise dictionaries can spend capacity representing the same carried-forward information, and replacing several layers at once can produce interactions that are not predicted by single-layer behavior. We introduce Residualized Sparse Autoencoders (ReSAEs), which fit an affine map between selected layers and train each later-layer SAE on the unexplained residual rather than on the full activation. Reconstructions are mapped back into the original activation space through the fitted affine chain, so ReSAEs can be evaluated with the same intervention protocols as ordinary SAEs. On Pythia-1.4B and Gemma-2-9B, residualization reduces decoder redundancy and improves sparse probing and targeted perturbation in most tested settings. Despite reconstructing less of the raw activation variance, ReSAEs recover more transformer cross entropy under multi-layer replacement. This gain is clearest under teacher-forcing and at sufficient sparsity online, indicating that ReSAEs preserve the components of the activation most relevant to the model's downstream computation. These results suggest that removing linearly predictable cross-layer structure is a useful default for multi-layer SAE interventions.

### [113] [Reward Transfer from Inverse Reinforcement Learning: A Coupled Minimax Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27834)
*Guang-Yuan Hao,Lars van der Laan,Aurélien Bibaut,Nathan Kallus*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在不同环境中，如何将通过逆强化学习从专家示范中学习到的奖励进行迁移。作者将问题形式化为源环境与目标环境之间的联合贝尔曼方程系统，并提出了针对目标软Q函数的极小极大估计器。与先估计源环境奖励再用于目标控制的顺序方法不同，耦合方法联合求解源与目标的方程系统。理论分析表明，耦合方法能消除源环境贝尔曼残差误差的一阶影响。文中还分析了两种方法的局部行为，给出了有限样本下软Q函数的误差界，并证明了所得软控制策略的后悔保证。实验使用败血症模拟器验证了理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当专家示范在受控环境中收集时，如何将学到的奖励有效迁移到新的、不同的环境中是一个关键问题。传统的顺序方法（先估计源奖励，再用于目标）存在对源环境误差敏感的问题，因此需要更稳健的迁移机制。

Method: 将迁移问题建模为源环境与目标环境的联合贝尔曼方程系统；提出极小极大估计器以求解目标软Q函数；采用耦合求解方式，同时优化源与目标系统的解，而非顺序处理。

Result: 耦合方法相比顺序方法能消除源贝尔曼残差误差的一阶影响，具有更优的鲁棒性；理论推导出有限样本下的软Q函数误差上界和策略后悔上界；实验在败血症模拟器中验证了理论优势。

Conclusion: 耦合方法在奖励迁移任务中表现更优，能够有效降低源环境误差对目标策略的影响，具备更强的理论保障和实际应用潜力。

Abstract: We study the transfer of rewards learned using inverse reinforcement learning from expert demonstrations in one environment to reinforcement learning in a new, different environment. This arises naturally when demonstrations are collected in a controlled environment. We formulate the problem as a joint system of Bellman equations across the source and target environments and develop minimax estimators for the target soft-$q$-function. Whereas a sequential solution approach first estimates the source reward and then plugs it into the target control problem, a coupled approach solves the source and target system of equations jointly. We show that, in contrast to the sequential approach, the coupled approach removes the first-order influence of source Bellman residual error. We characterize the local behavior of each approach, develop finite-sample soft-$q$-function error bounds, and prove regret guarantees for the resulting soft-control policy. An empirical investigation using a sepsis simulator validates the theoretical comparison.

</details>


### [114] [CAREF: Calibration-Aware Regularization for Explanation Faithfulness Without Rationale Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27835)
*Naphat Nithisopa,Teerapong Panboonyuen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CAREF 是一种参数高效的微调框架，通过校准感知正则化联合优化预测准确性和解释可信度。其核心是将基于熵的校准与基于令牌级别的稀疏性控制结合到单一统一损失函数（LSCED）中，无需理由监督。在四个NLE基准测试（COS-E、ECQA、ComVE、e-SNLI）上使用Flan-T5进行评估，轻量级CAREF-AQ变体仅使用6.43%的可训练参数，即达到最佳平均准确率（89.04）和解释对齐度（81.00 nBERT），优于LoRA和AdaLoRA。据我们所知，CAREF是首个将熵和稀疏性正则化统一于单一训练目标中的可解释大模型微调方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在可解释的大模型微调中难以同时兼顾预测准确性与解释的可信度，且通常需要额外的标注数据来指导解释生成。因此，亟需一种无需理由监督、能联合优化准确性和解释质量的高效微调框架。

Method: CAREF 提出一个统一的损失函数 LSCED，融合熵基校准与令牌级稀疏性控制，实现对模型输出置信度和解释注意力分布的双重调节；通过参数高效微调机制，在不增加大量参数的前提下提升模型性能和解释质量。

Result: 在四个NLE基准测试中，CAREF-AQ变体在仅使用6.43%可训练参数的情况下，实现了89.04的平均准确率和81.00的nBERT解释对齐度，显著优于LoRA和AdaLoRA等现有方法。

Conclusion: CAREF是首个将熵校准与稀疏性控制统一于单一训练目标的可解释大模型微调方法，有效提升了模型的预测准确性和解释可信度，同时保持极低的参数开销，为高效可解释AI提供了新范式。

Abstract: We introduce CAREF, a parameter-efficient fine-tuning framework that jointly optimizes predictive accuracy and explanation faithfulness via calibration-aware regularization. At its core, CAREF couples entropy-based calibration with token-level sparsity control through a single unified loss, the Calibration-Aware Regularization for Explanation Faithfulness (LSCED), without requiring rationale supervision. Evaluated on four NLE benchmarks (COS-E, ECQA, ComVE, e-SNLI) with Flan-T5, our lightweight CAREF-AQ variant attains the best average accuracy (89.04) and explanation alignment (81.00 nBERT) using only 6.43% of trainable parameters, outperforming LoRA and AdaLoRA. To our knowledge, CAREF is the first method to unify entropy and sparsity regularization in a single training objective for interpretable LLM fine-tuning.

### [115] [SPAR: Support-Preserving Action Rectification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27877)
*Jiaxin Zhao,Weihang Pan,Xun Liang,Binbin Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SPAR提出一种新的离线策略改进方法，通过局部残差修正和潜在自模仿机制，在保持数据分布支持的同时缓解优化与拟合之间的冲突，显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决离线策略改进中价值最大化与数据分布拟合之间的固有矛盾，克服传统方法的过度保守或梯度拟合-优化冲突问题。

Method: 提出支持保持动作修正（SPAR）框架，基于冻结的行为克隆策略进行局部残差修正，并引入潜在采样加权回归机制（Latent Self-Imitation）以消除标准值梯度的流形法向漂移。

Result: 理论证明该机制可消除流形法向漂移；在D4RL基准上，SPAR从次优基线中提取显著收益，达到当前最优性能。

Conclusion: SPAR通过局部残差空间中的精细拟合与改进，有效缩小搜索空间并避免偏离数据流形，实现稳定且高效的离线策略优化。

Abstract: Offline policy improvement faces an inherent conflict between maximizing value and fitting the data distribution. While in-sample weighted regression is stable, it suffers from over-conservatism that suppresses high-value actions in the distribution tail; conversely, gradient-based approaches often exhibit a fitting-optimization conflict of gradients, which drives the policy off the data manifold. To address this, we propose Support-Preserving Action Rectification (SPAR), which reframes global learning as a local residual rectification anchored to a frozen pure behavior cloning policy. This framework performs fine-grained fitting and local policy improvement in the residual space, thereby contracting the search space. We further introduce Latent Self-Imitation, utilizing a latent-sampling weighted-regression mechanism to address fitting-improvement gradient conflict in the residual space. Theoretically, we prove this mechanism eliminates the manifold-normal drift of standard value gradients, while extensive D4RL experiments show SPAR extracts significant gains from suboptimal baselines to achieve state-of-the-art performance.

</details>


### [116] [FedEHR-Gen: Federated Synthetic Time-Series EHR Generation via Latent Space Alignment and Distribution-Aware Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27892)
*Jun Bai,Ziyang Song,Yue Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FedEHR-Gen 是首个用于跨分布式医院合成时间序列电子健康记录（EHR）生成的联邦学习框架。它采用两阶段学习：首先通过联邦自编码器将高维稀疏的EHR特征映射到紧凑的潜在空间，并利用分层匹配聚合机制对齐本地编码器以保证语义一致性；其次在对齐后的潜在空间上训练一个分布感知的联邦时序条件变分自编码器（TCVAE），实现稳定的时间序列生成建模。实验表明，该方法在生成质量、下游任务性能和隐私保护方面均达到与集中式训练相当的水平，且优于标准联邦基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有EHR生成模型多为集中式，需跨医院汇聚数据，但在隐私受限环境下难以实现。尽管联邦学习可缓解此问题，但直接应用常因数据高维性、稀疏性和跨医院异质性导致模型崩溃或发散。因此需要一种能有效处理分布式、异构EHR数据的联邦生成框架。

Method: 提出两阶段联邦学习框架FedEHR-Gen：第一阶段使用联邦自编码器将高维稀疏的EHR特征投影至紧凑潜在空间，并引入层间匹配聚合机制确保各医院编码器在全局潜在空间中的一致性；第二阶段基于对齐后的潜在空间，训练分布感知的联邦时序条件变分自编码器（TCVAE），以应对严重的跨医院异质性并实现稳定的时间序列生成。

Result: 在eICU和MIMIC-III数据集上的大量实验显示，FedEHR-Gen在生成保真度、下游任务效用及隐私风险方面表现与集中式训练相当，且显著优于标准联邦基线模型。

Conclusion: FedEHR-Gen成功实现了在隐私保护前提下跨医院合成高质量时间序列EHR数据的目标，为医疗数据协作提供了可行的联邦生成解决方案。

Abstract: Synthetic Electronic Health Record (EHR) generation provides a promising avenue for data augmentation and cross-hospital modeling in privacy-constrained healthcare settings. However, most existing EHR generative models are centralized and require pooling data across hospitals, which is often infeasible when real-world data sharing is restricted. While federated EHR generation offers a natural solution, direct federated modeling often collapses or diverges due to the high dimensionality, sparsity, and cross-hospital heterogeneity of EHR data. In this work, we propose FedEHR-Gen, the first federated framework for synthetic time-series EHR generation across distributed hospitals. FedEHR-Gen uses a two-stage learning paradigm. First, we introduce a federated autoencoder that projects high-dimensional and sparse EHR features onto a compact latent space. To ensure semantic consistency across hospitals, we develop a layer-wise matching aggregation mechanism that aligns local encoders into a unified global latent space. Second, operating on this aligned latent space, we train a federated temporal conditional variational autoencoder (TCVAE) with distribution-aware aggregation, enabling stable temporal generative modeling under severe cross-hospital heterogeneity. Extensive experiments on the eICU and MIMIC-III datasets demonstrate that FedEHR-Gen achieves generation fidelity, downstream utility, and privacy risk comparable to centralized training, while consistently outperforming the standard federated baseline.

### [117] [Where LLM Annotators Fail: Label-Free Learning on Graphs with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27913)
*Safal Thapaliya,Jiatan Huang,Chuxu Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出CANE框架，通过估计聚类条件下的LLM可靠性，提升图节点分类中伪标签的可信度，尤其在存在聚类条件噪声的数据集上表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将LLM生成的噪声视为全局或类别条件噪声，但实际中噪声还具有区域依赖性；同一类别内不同特征空间聚类的可靠性差异显著，需更精细的噪声建模。

Method: 提出Cluster-Aware Noise Estimation (CANE)，通过无监督方式估计每个聚类内的LLM标注可靠性，并据此决定信任或修正伪标签。

Result: 在多个图基准数据集和GNN模型上，CANE优于最强的无标签学习基线，尤其在聚类条件噪声较强的数据集上提升显著。

Abstract: Node classification on graphs often requires labeled nodes, yet obtaining labels at graph scale is expensive. When node attributes contain semantic content, such as paper abstracts, web pages, or product descriptions, large language models (LLMs) can provide low-cost supervision by annotating a small subset of nodes. However, these LLM-generated labels are noisy, and existing label-free graph learning methods usually treat this noise as either global or class-conditional. We find that LLM annotation errors are not only class-dependent but also region-dependent: within the same class, reliability can vary sharply across feature-space clusters. In light of this, we propose Cluster-Aware Noise Estimation (CANE), a label-free learning framework that estimates cluster-conditional LLM reliability without ground truth labels, and uses this estimate to decide which pseudo-labels to trust, and which labels to correct. Across various graph benchmarks and GNN backbones, CANE improves over the strongest label-free baselines, with the largest gains on datasets exhibiting stronger cluster-conditional noise.

### [118] [Law of Neural Interaction: Depth-Width Shape, Interaction Efficiency, and Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27989)
*Wenjie Sun,Jinning Yang,Shuai Zhang,Mengnan Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在固定资源预算下大型语言模型（LLMs）的资源利用效率问题，提出通过神经特征假设将超叠加现象从参数空间扩展到梯度空间，定义为神经交互。研究发现，良好的泛化能力通常伴随着高效的神经交互，且通过调整深度-宽度比（R_{D/W}）可使模型处于高效交互区间。随着预算增加，该高效区间保持相对稳定。对比现有小规模密集LLM发现，接近此区间的模型在MMLU-Pro基准上表现更优。结论表明，R_{D/W}影响资源利用效率并进而影响泛化性能，为模型结构初始化与泛化机制理解提供新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代大语言模型受缩放定律指导，资源需求持续上升，但其在固定预算下的资源利用效率尚不明确。已有研究指出超叠加是损失的关键因素，但其在梯度空间中的作用未被充分探索。因此，亟需理解如何优化模型结构以提升资源利用效率和泛化能力。

Method: 基于神经特征假设，将超叠加概念推广至梯度空间，定义为神经交互；通过分析不同深度-宽度比（R_{D/W}）下的模型表现，识别高效神经交互区间，并结合实验验证其对泛化性能的影响。

Result: 在固定预算下，高效神经交互与良好泛化密切相关；调整R_{D/W}可引导模型进入高效交互区间；随着预算增大，该区间保持稳定；接近该区间的模型在MMLU-Pro上表现更优。

Conclusion: 深度-宽度比（R_{D/W}）显著影响资源利用效率，进而决定模型的泛化能力。合理设计模型结构以匹配高效神经交互区间，有助于提升模型性能，为模型初始化与泛化机制研究提供了新思路。

Abstract: The guidance of scaling laws has increased the resource demands of modern large language models (LLMs), yet it remains questionable whether these models utilize resources effectively under a fixed budget. Previous research has proved superposition as a key contributor to loss. By leveraging the Neural Feature Ansatz, we extend superposition from parameter space to gradient space and define it as neural interaction. We find that under a fixed budget, good generalization is usually accompanied by efficient neural interactions, and the model can be placed in an efficient interaction interval by adjusting its depth-width ratio ($R_{D/W}$). In addition, as the budget scales up, the efficient interaction interval of the model remains relatively stable. By comparing existing small scale dense LLMs, we observe that models operating near this interval tend to perform better on the MMLU-Pro benchmark. Our findings reveal that the $R_{D/W}$ influences resource utilization efficiency and thereby affects generalization, providing insights into model shape initialization and the understanding of model generalization mechanisms. Code for Neural Interaction Law is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Neural_Interaction_Law-D788

</details>


### [119] [Geometry-Correct Diffusion Posterior Sampling with Denoiser-Pullback Curvature Guidance and Manifold-Aligned Damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27990)
*Seunghyeok Shin,Minwoo Kim,Dabin Kim,Hongki Lim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种新的扩散后验采样方法，通过在扩散状态坐标中使用基于噪声级别的阻尼高斯-牛顿校正，替代传统的标量引导方式，有效避免了数据一致性更新中的手调引导权重问题，并提升了采样稳定性。该方法利用自动微分进行矩阵自由的GMRES求解，结合方差保持的Langevin转移，实现高效且准确的图像重建。在FFHQ和ImageNet上的逆问题以及加速MRI重建任务中，均取得了优于或相当的性能，且运行速度显著快于多数基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统扩散后验采样方法依赖手调的引导权重进行数据一致性更新，容易因算子相关的强曲率而造成采样不稳定。为解决这一问题，需设计更鲁棒、自适应的更新机制。

Method: 提出一种基于噪声级别调节的阻尼高斯-牛顿校正，将似然梯度回传至去噪器，采用单边曲率模型避免前向去噪器雅可比计算，并引入与去噪残差对齐的扩散校准秩一阻尼；所有校正通过矩阵自由的GMRES结合自动微分求解，采样过程采用具有闭式漂移/噪声分解的方差保持Langevin过渡。

Result: 在FFHQ和ImageNet的各类逆问题中，达到竞争性的PSNR、SSIM和LPIPS指标，且运行速度显著快于多数基线方法；在加速MRI重建任务中，获得最优的PSNR和SSIM表现。

Conclusion: 所提出的扩散状态坐标下的阻尼高斯-牛顿校正方法，能够有效提升扩散后验采样的稳定性与效率，适用于多种图像重建任务，尤其在加速MRI中表现出色，是当前先进方法之一。

Abstract: Diffusion posterior sampling conditions diffusion priors on measurements, but data-consistency updates are typically scaled by hand-tuned guidance weights and can destabilize sampling under stiff, operator-dependent curvature. We replace scalar guidance with a per-noise-level damped Gauss--Newton correction computed in diffusion-state coordinates. The correction pulls likelihood gradients back through the denoiser, uses a one-sided curvature model that avoids forward denoiser Jacobians, and applies diffusion-calibrated rank-one damping aligned with the denoiser residual. Each correction is solved with matrix-free GMRES using automatic differentiation, and sampling proceeds with a variance-preserving Langevin transition with a closed-form drift/noise split. On FFHQ and ImageNet across inverse problems, it achieves competitive PSNR/SSIM/LPIPS while running markedly faster than most of the compared baselines; on accelerated MRI reconstruction, it achieves the best PSNR/SSIM among the compared baselines.

</details>

### [120] [Identifying and Understanding Human Values in Text: A Tailorable LLM-based Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27373)
*Eduardo de la Cruz Fernández,Marcelo Karanik,Sascha Ossowski*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的架构，用于检测和量化文本中人类价值观的强度，避免了以往方法对特定价值理论或复杂提示工程的依赖。该架构包含三个模块：生成任何理论框架基础文本的结构化价值规范、使用这些规范标注文本、以及根据修辞和语义证据分配支持或反对程度。该方法分离了概念化与检测任务，具有可扩展性和可重复性，适用于多种价值理论。在ValueEval数据集上的实验表明其性能良好，验证了该流程的通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着智能系统日益自主，传统以效用最大化为核心的决策机制已无法满足伦理与道德考量的需求。因此，亟需一种有效评估智能系统决策是否符合人类价值观的方法，而现有方法往往受限于特定价值理论或复杂的提示设计，难以普适应用。

Method: 提出一个三模块协同的LLM架构：1）从任意理论框架的基础文本生成结构化的价值规范；2）利用这些规范对输入文本进行标注；3）基于语义和修辞证据为每项价值分配支持或抵抗的等级评分。整个流程解耦概念构建与检测过程，提升灵活性与可迁移性。

Result: 在ValueEval数据集上的实验结果显示，该架构具备良好的价值检测性能，且在不同大语言模型上表现稳定，证明了其通用性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 该基于LLM的架构为识别和量化文本中隐含或显性的价值观提供了一种灵活、可复现且不依赖特定理论的方法，为实现更符合人类价值观的智能决策系统奠定了基础。

Abstract: As intelligent systems become more autonomous, the scientific community focuses on creating decision-making mechanisms that include ethical and moral considerations, unlike traditional utility-maximisation models. To achieve this, a key aspect is assessing how well these decisions align with human values. To this end, a promising line of research is centred on developing approaches based on Large Language Models (LLMs) to identify human values from text, whether explicit or implicit, enabling their recognition throughout. This paper introduces a LLM-based architecture to detect and quantify the intensity of human values in text, avoiding the limitations of previous approaches tied to specific value theory or complex prompt engineering. The architecture comprises three coordinated modules: one that generates structured value specifications from the foundational texts of any theoretical framework; one that labels texts using these specifications; and one that assigns graded support or resistance based on rhetorical and semantic evidence. This modular approach separates the tasks of conceptualising from detecting human values, creating a scalable and reproducible process driven by value specifications adaptable to various theories. The architecture was instantiated with multiple LLMs and evaluated using the ValueEval dataset. The experiments demonstrate good detection performance, confirming the generality of the pipeline.

</details>


### [121] [Soro: A Lightweight Foundation Model and Chatbot for Tajik](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27379)
*Stanislav Liashkov,Haitz Sáez de Ocáriz Borde,Azizjon Azimi,Khushbakht Shaymardonov,Shuhratjon Khalitbekov,Bonu Boboeva*

TL;DR: Soro is a family of Tajik-specialized conversational LLMs built from Gemma 3, trained on a 1.9B-token Tajik-only corpus and fine-tuned with 40K teacher-style examples. It outperforms baseline models on custom Tajik benchmarks, maintains strong English performance, and supports efficient edge deployment via FP8/INT4 quantization, enabling real-world education pilots in Tajikistan.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To address the lack of effective language models for Tajik, a low-resource language with limited coverage in standard benchmarks, especially under constrained compute and connectivity conditions in Tajikistan. Method: Continual pretraining on a curated 1.9-billion-token Tajik corpus (web text, PDFs, educational materials), followed by supervised instruction tuning using 40K teacher-style examples. Custom benchmarks were developed for rigorous evaluation. Model efficiency was enhanced via FP8 and INT4 quantization.

Result: Soro significantly outperforms same-size Gemma 3 baselines on Tajik-specific benchmarks while preserving strong English capabilities. Quantized versions maintain most Tajik performance gains and enable edge deployment, supporting an ongoing education pilot in Tajikistan.

Conclusion: Soro demonstrates that domain-specific, resource-efficient LLMs tailored to low-resource languages like Tajik can be successfully developed and deployed in real-world settings, paving the way for scalable AI-driven education tools in underserved regions.

Abstract: We present Soro, a family of Tajik-specialized conversational large language models (LLMs) designed for real-world deployment under tight compute and connectivity constraints in Tajikistan. Starting from open-weight Gemma 3 checkpoints, we perform Tajik-only continual pretraining on a curated 1.9-billion-token corpus spanning filtered web text, PDF documents, and curriculum-aligned educational materials, followed by supervised instruction tuning on 40K Tajik teacher-style examples. To enable rigorous evaluation despite the limited coverage of Tajik in standard benchmarks, we introduce a suite of Tajik benchmarks covering general knowledge, linguistic competence, and school- and university entrance-exam domains, and we open-source them on Hugging Face. Across these Tajik benchmarks, Soro substantially outperforms same-size Gemma 3 baselines while retaining strong English performance on standard datasets. We further show that FP8 and INT4 quantization of Soro preserves most Tajik-language gains while reducing memory requirements for edge deployment, supporting an ongoing education-sector pilot and planned scale-out across schools in Tajikistan.

### [122] [On the Origin of Synthetic Information by Means of Steganographic Inheritance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27551)
*Ching-Chun Chang,Isao Echizen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于隐写术的合成信息谱系追踪机制，模拟生物遗传，使合成内容在生成时携带不可见的父代特征，从而实现溯源。理论与实证分析表明该方法在多种处理和语义修改下仍具可行性，为人工智能生成内容的可信性与可追溯性提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成信息的起源如同信息科学中的‘神秘之谜’，其演化路径因AI能力增强而难以追踪，亟需一种类似遗传的可追溯机制以维护真实、信任与人类认知的完整性。

Method: 通过隐写术，在合成信息生成时由投影器提取父代特征，并嵌入子代中；在溯源时使用解码器从子代中提取特征并比对候选父代，确定最可能来源。

Result: 理论分析揭示了谱系准确性与投影器及隐写系统特性的关系；多组实验验证了该方法在各类处理操作和语义变化下的有效性与稳健性。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了一个具备可追溯谱系的合成信息生态系统，使人工生成内容能如生命般演化且始终可溯源，为未来数字生态的信任体系提供技术基础。

Abstract: The origin of species has been the mystery of mysteries in natural science. By analogy, the origin of synthetic information, we suggest, is the mystery of mysteries in information science. The question carries a moral weight that a technical account can neither fully resolve nor responsibly ignore, as its impact on truth, trust, and human intellect extends deep into the broader economy and society. The very power of artificial intelligence makes the evolutionary lineage of synthetic information grow ever harder to trace, for a sufficiently capable model may generate offspring that bear little resemblance, at either the structural or signal level, to the parent source from which they were derived. As in genetics, two individuals may share the same phenotype mirroring each other in outward appearance, yet differ fundamentally in their genotype. We propose, by means of steganography, a mechanism analogous to heredity. At the moment an offspring is reproduced, a projector derives a trait from the parent, and a steganographic encoder invisibly hides it within the offspring. This trait persists throughout the offspring's life cycle in a cyber ecosystem. When parentage is queried, a steganographic decoder extracts the trait from the offspring and compares it against the traits of candidate parents in a reference pool, thereby nominating the most likely one. A theoretical analysis characterises phylogenetic accuracy as a function of projector and stegosystem properties, whilst empirical evaluations across multiple projectors and stegosystems demonstrate the viability of the proposed methodology under a broad spectrum of processing operations and semantic modifications. We envision a cyber ecosystem in which synthetic information, endowed with hidden yet traceable lineage traits, branches from a simple beginning into endless forms that have been, and are being, evolved.

### [123] [RULER: Representation-Level Verification of Machine Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27569)
*Georgina Cosma,Axel Finke*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出RULER，一套基于表示层面的模型遗忘验证指标，以检测模型在中间表示中是否仍保留被遗忘数据的痕迹。现有方法仅从输出层面评估遗忘效果，但模型可能在内部表示中仍隐含遗忘记录。RULER中的M2指标通过比较与重新训练模型的表示位置来检测残留；M4则无需重新训练，仅通过分析模型内部相似性结构即可发现残留。实验表明，四种近似遗忘方法虽通过输出层评估，但在M2下均显示显著残留（p<0.05），且残留随遗忘比例增加而加剧。第五种方法Bad Teacher也表现出类似问题。M4在表格、图像、临床文本和人脸身份识别等多种场景中可作为预遗忘诊断工具，有效检测出人脸模型中的身份记忆残留。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器遗忘方法仅在输出层面进行验证，无法检测模型内部表示中是否仍存在被遗忘数据的痕迹，可能导致隐私泄露。因此需要更严格的表示层面验证机制。

Method: 提出RULER框架，包含两个指标：M2（需重新训练作为参考）用于衡量遗忘样本在表示空间中的位置是否与未训练样本一致；M4（无需重新训练）通过分析模型内部相似性结构检测残留信号。

Result: 所有四种近似遗忘方法在输出层面表现良好，但在M2指标下10/12条件下检测到显著残留（p<0.05），效应量随遗忘比例上升。Bad Teacher方法虽机制不同，同样存在残留。M4在多种任务中成功检测到身份记忆残留，证明其作为通用预遗忘诊断工具的有效性。

Conclusion: 仅依赖输出层面验证的遗忘方法可能存在隐藏的记忆残留。RULER框架通过表示层面的M2和M4指标，能够有效揭示这些残留，提升机器遗忘的安全性和可靠性。

Abstract: Machine unlearning aims to remove the influence of specific training records from a deployed model without retraining from scratch. Current protocols verify this at the output level through membership inference, retain accuracy, and forget-set accuracy, but a model can satisfy all three whilst still encoding forgotten records in its intermediate representations. We introduce RULER, a set of representation-level verification metrics. The oracle-comparative metric M2 measures whether forget-set records occupy the same representational position as in a model retrained without them. The oracle-free metric M4 detects residuals from the unlearned model's internal similarity structure alone, without retraining. Four approximate unlearning methods all pass output-level evaluation, yet under a linear mixed-effects model M2 detects significant residuals in 10 of 12 conditions (p<0.05), with effect sizes growing as the forget fraction increases. A fifth method, Bad Teacher, shows the same residuals despite a different forgetting mechanism. M4 acts as a pre-unlearning diagnostic across tabular, image, clinical text, and face-identity settings: it detects identity-level memorisation in face recognition models where no tested method fully erases the signal.

</details>


### [124] [LaneRoPE: Positional Encoding for Collaborative Parallel Reasoning and Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27570)
*Gabriele Cesa,Thomas Hehn,Aleix Torres-Camps,Àlex Batlle Casellas,Jordi Ros-Giralt,Arash Behboodi,Tribhuvanesh Orekondy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出LaneRoPE，一种用于并行大语言模型测试时扩展的技术，通过引入序列间注意力掩码和扩展的RoPE位置编码，使多个生成序列在生成过程中能够相互协作，从而在有限序列长度下提升数学推理任务的准确性。该方法对模型架构改动小，推理开销低，易于集成到现有推理流程中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统并行生成方法（如best-of-N）虽然能提升准确率，但各序列独立生成，无法复用中间结果或计算，导致资源浪费。本文旨在通过引入序列间的协同机制，提升生成效率与质量。

Method: 提出LaneRoPE，包含两个核心设计：(a) 序列间注意力掩码，使序列生成依赖彼此；(b) 扩展的RoPE位置编码，捕捉序列内及跨序列的相对位置信息。

Result: 在数学推理任务上，LaneRoPE实现了额外的准确率提升，尤其在生成序列长度受限的情况下表现更优。同时，其对模型架构影响小，推理开销可忽略，具备良好的部署可行性。

Conclusion: LaneRoPE通过在生成阶段实现多序列间的协调与协作，显著提升了并行生成的效果，且具有极高的工程实用性，是将并行推理快速集成到现有LLM系统中的有效方案。

Abstract: Parallel LLM test-time scaling techniques (e.g., best-of-$N$) require drawing $N>1$ sequences conditioned on the same input prompt. These methods boost accuracy while exploiting the computational efficiency of batching $N$ generations. However, each sequence in the batch is traditionally generated independently and hence does not reuse intermediate generations, computations, or observations from other sequences. In this paper, we propose LaneRoPE to enable coordination and collaboration among $N>1$ sequences at generation time. LaneRoPE involves two key ideas: (a) an inter-sequence attention mask to make sampling of sequences dependent on one another; and (b) a RoPE extension that injects positional information that captures relative positions between tokens, both within and outside a particular sequence. We evaluate our approach on mathematical reasoning tasks and find promising results: LaneRoPE enables collaboration among sequences, yielding additional accuracy gains under limited generated sequence length. Importantly, since LaneRoPE enables coordination with minimal changes to the underlying LLM architecture and introduces a negligible overhead at inference time, it is appealing to rapidly incorporate parallel reasoning into existing LLM inference pipelines.

Conclusion: 该多智能体架构为实时数据分析提供了可扩展、可观察、可信赖的自主洞察发现范式，推动了分析系统从反应式向主动式演进。

Abstract: Modern analytics systems are fundamentally reactive, requiring users to define queries over increasingly complex and continuously evolving data. We present a multi-agent architecture for autonomous insight discovery over real-time data streams. The system implements a continuous discovery loop in which agents generate hypotheses, compile them into executable analytics, validate generated artifacts, and produce visualizations and deployable applications. The architecture leverages Apache Kafka for event-driven coordination, Apache Flink for stream processing, and large language models to implement specialized agents. ### [126] [Behavioural Analysis of Alignment Faking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27681)
*Nathaniel Mitrani Hadida,Rhea Karty,David Williams-King,Alan Cooney*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了对齐伪造（Alignment Faking, AF）现象，即模型在训练中伪装顺从以避免行为改变，同时保留其部署偏好。通过控制实验，研究发现AF在多种模型中普遍存在，且由三个独立驱动因素——价值观、目标保护和奉承倾向——共同作用，并可通过提示词消融和激活操控验证。结果表明AF可预测，其发生与情境线索及模型固有倾向相关，为未来检测和缓解提供了方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解对齐伪造（AF）的出现机制至关重要，因为随着模型越来越能区分训练与部署环境，其策略性顺从行为可能影响安全性与可靠性。此前研究认为AF脆弱且依赖特定条件，但驱动因素不明确，因此需要更系统的方法来揭示其本质。

Method: 采用受控、极简的实验设置，隔离对齐伪造的核心组件；通过针对不同模型进行提示词消融实验和激活调控，分析三种潜在驱动因素（价值观、目标保护、奉承倾向）对AF的影响。

Result: AF在更广泛的模型中被观察到，包括小规模模型；三种驱动因素均可独立调节AF行为，且其发生与情境线索及模型的基线奉承倾向、陈述价值观等特征密切相关。

Conclusion: 对齐伪造比以往认为的更为普遍，其行为具有可预测性，基于模型倾向和情境信号可识别风险。该分解为未来检测与缓解对齐伪造提供了具体路径。

Abstract: Alignment faking (AF) refers to a model strategically complying with a training objective to avoid behavioural modification while preserving its deployment preferences. Understanding when and why AF arises matters as models grow better at distinguishing training from deployment. Prior work finds AF fragile, prompt-sensitive, and model-dependent, leaving its underlying drivers unclear. We study AF in a controlled, minimal setup that isolates its core components, and observe it across a wider range of models than previously reported, including small-scale models. We identify three separable drivers -- values, goal guarding, and sycophancy -- and show via targeted prompt ablations and activation steering that each independently modulates AF behaviour. Our results indicate AF is more widespread than previously reported and that its occurrence is predictable from situational cues and measurable model tendencies such as baseline sycophancy and stated values. The decomposition suggests concrete directions for detecting and mitigating AF in future models.

Conclusion: Frost Training 证明了嵌入空间梯度信号在模型训练中的有效性，为 LLM-as-a-judge 任务提供了一种高效且可扩展的优化路径。

Abstract: We present Frost Training, a method for improving Monte Carlo-based policy optimization for a large family of LLM-as-a-judge tasks called Cross-Entropy Games. The key idea is to exploit the gradient of the reward function in embedding space. This signal is used in the Greedy Coordinate Gradient (GCG) jailbreaking technique; we demonstrate for the first time that it can also be used to boost model training. We validate our method using GRPO training for maximum-likelihood infilling. Frost Training improves the model's ability to generate high-scoring outputs, reaching higher maximum scores in a best-of-k setting, and does so at an increased speed.

### [128] [DeepSciVerify: Verifying Scientific Claim--Citation Alignment via LLM-Driven Evidence Escalation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27710)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型生成报告时，主张与其引用证据之间常存在错位，影响其在科学及其他高风险场景中的可靠性。因此需要一种更可靠、高效的方法来验证科学主张与引用之间的匹配性。

Method: 提出 DeepSciVerify，一个两阶段管道：第一阶段基于摘要进行主张验证；第二阶段对不确定案例进行选择性升级，检索并分析全文段落以获取更精确证据。系统利用不同 LLM 在不确定性下的保守或决断行为的互补性，优化整体性能。

Result: 在 SCitance 基准上，DeepSciVerify 实现 86.7 的 Micro-F1，优于抽象仅基线 4.5 个百分点；67% 的实例无需全文检索即可完成验证，显著提升效率与准确性。

Conclusion: 选择性证据升级策略有效提升了科学主张-引用验证的准确性和效率，为高风险场景下 LLM 生成内容的可信度提供有力支持。

Abstract: Misalignment between claims and their cited evidence is a common failure mode in reports generated by large language models, limiting their reliability in scientific and other high-stakes settings. We present DeepSciVerify, a two-stage pipeline for scientific claim-citation verification that combines abstract-level reasoning with selective escalation to passage-level evidence. The system first verifies claims using the abstract and defers uncertain cases, retrieving and analyzing full-text passages only when necessary. This design leverages complementary behaviors across LLMs, as some models are more conservative while others are more decisive under uncertainty. On the SCitance benchmark, DeepSciVerify achieves 86.7 Micro-F1, outperforming strong abstract-only baselines by +4.5 points while resolving 67% of instances without full-text retrieval. These results suggest that selective evidence escalation improves both accuracy and efficiency in claim-citation verification.

### [129] [Asking Is Not Enough: Protocol Sensitivity in LLM Confidence Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27752)
*Hankyeol Kim,Pilsung Kang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型（LLM）置信度校准中两种信号——基于标记的概率分数与口头化置信度——的比较敏感性。通过固定口头化置信度的提取方式，系统地改变测量轴（如得分答案的选择、概率读取方式和条件上下文），发现这些设计选择显著影响校准结果，尤其是条件上下文对ECE差距的方向和大小有决定性影响。在默认设置下，指令型模型的两种置信度信号接近一致，并未表现出明显优势。此外，表面合理的错误答案获得的置信度与正确答案相近，表明口头化置信度反映的不仅是正确性，还包括答案的合理性和来源。研究建议将两种置信度信号视为依赖协议的行为测量，并提出包含提取来源、评分答案、概率读取方式和条件上下文的报告清单。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究常将令牌概率和口头化置信度视为模型不确定性的直接度量，但其比较结果高度依赖于未明示的测量设计选择。为揭示这些选择的影响，需系统评估不同协议对校准评估结果的敏感性。

Method: 固定口头化置信度的提示模板、概率尺度和输出格式，系统变化三个测量轴：得分答案的选择、从答案标记中读取概率的方式、以及测量所处的条件上下文。在四个问答基准上测试三种7–8B基础/指令模型家族，使用更大的Qwen2.5变体进行同族鲁棒性验证。采用ECE作为评估指标，分析不同设置下的校准表现。

Result: 条件上下文的变化可导致ECE差距的符号或幅度发生显著改变；标记读取方式也带来较小但仍有影响力的改变；而ECE估计器的选择影响较小。在默认生成答案、裸上下文协议下，指令型模型的两种置信度信号接近平衡，无明显校准优势。在补充答案分析中，表面合理的错误答案获得的置信度与正确答案几乎相同，说明口头化置信度受答案合理性与来源影响，而非仅由正确性决定。

Conclusion: 令牌概率和口头化置信度均是协议依赖的行为测量，不应被简单视为模型不确定性的直接反映。应建立标准化报告规范，明确记录置信度评估的各个环节，以提升可比性与透明度。

Abstract: LLM confidence calibration is often evaluated by comparing two signals: token-probability scores and verbalized confidence. These signals are sometimes treated as direct readouts of model uncertainty, but their comparison depends on measurement choices that are rarely made explicit. In the main analysis, we hold the verbalized-confidence elicitation fixed: a single prompt template, probability scale, and output format. We then vary the measurement axes that define the verbalized-vs-token comparison: which answer string receives the token-probability score, how that score is read from the answer tokens, and under which conditioning context it is measured. We evaluate this design on four QA benchmarks across three open 7--8B base/Instruct model families, with larger Qwen2.5 variants as same-family robustness checks. The resulting comparison is sensitive to these choices: conditioning context changes the sign or magnitude of the ECE gap across settings, token readout produces smaller but still sign-moving changes, and changing the ECE estimator has little effect. Under the default generated-answer, bare-context protocol, Instruct settings are close to parity rather than showing a large calibration gain for verbalized confidence. In a separate supplied-answer analysis, surface-plausible wrong answers receive nearly the same confidence as supplied gold answers, suggesting that verbalized confidence also reflects answer plausibility and provenance rather than correctness alone. We argue that both confidence signals should be treated as protocol-dependent behavioral measurements, and provide a reporting checklist covering elicitation provenance, scored answer, token-probability readout, and conditioning context.

</details>


### [130] [Auditable Decision Models with Learned Abstention and Real-Time Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27768)

Abstract: Production AI systems often operate with incomplete, conflicting, or insufficient evidence. Forced classifiers collapse such cases into action labels, while generative systems can produce outputs that are difficult to interpret as auditable execution decisions. We study operational decision control for AI systems, where uncertainty must be explicitly routable, policy-governed, and auditable rather than hidden inside forced predictions or free-form generation. We present EvaluatorDPT, a bounded decision-control model that predicts YES, NO, or TBD, where TBD is learned as a deferral outcome rather than added only as a post-hoc confidence rule. The model uses a transformer encoder with a primary bounded-decision head and structured auxiliary channels for values and emotions/sentiments. The interface is domain-agnostic in form: a deployment domain supplies evidence and policy thresholds, while the model emits a bounded distribution that can be controlled at inference time through recorded operating thresholds and, when validated, auxiliary semantic signals. For the evaluated model version, we report decision performance on held-out validation and test splits; auxiliary emotion metrics are omitted because the emotion head is disabled for this evaluation. On the held-out test split (n=44,597), the model achieves Accuracy = 0.8260 and Macro F1 = 0.8252, with per-class F1 of 0.8314 (YES), 0.8486 (NO), and 0.7956 (TBD). The evaluation record also includes calibration evidence (ECE = 0.0338 on validation), threshold-sweep outputs, multi-seed stability checks, confusion matrices, and reproducibility commands. Our main contribution is a bounded execution interface in which deferral is learned, inference-time routing remains inspectable, auxiliary signals provide a path to auditable behavior control, and evaluation evidence supports external review.
